window.onerror=function(msg,src,line,col){

  try{

    var d=document.getElementById('bootsnag');

    if(!d){ d=document.createElement('div'); d.id='bootsnag';

      d.style.cssText='position:fixed;top:8px;left:8px;right:8px;z-index:9999;background:#5b1a1a;color:#ffd7d7;font:12px monospace;padding:10px 12px;border-radius:8px;white-space:pre-wrap;';

      if(document.body){ document.body.appendChild(d); } else { document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',function(){document.body.appendChild(d);}); }

    }

    d.textContent='The dance stumbled at load:\n'+msg+'\n(line '+line+':'+col+')';

  }catch(e){}

  return false;

};

window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection',function(ev){ window.onerror(String((ev.reason&&ev.reason.message)||ev.reason),'',0,0); });

/* ============================================================

   THRONE — Solo vs AI · game engine

   Part A: constants, state, helpers, UI primitives

   ============================================================ */

'use strict';

 

const ALL_TRACKS = ['Faerie Ring','Faerie Fort','Faerie Mound','Faerie Bridge'];

/* ---------- game modes ----------

   MASQUERADE: the intro — social deduction core only. Three dances, plain

   numbered runes (no powers, no gift icons), no Faerie Magik, no conjured

   stones, no reaction windows.

   MIDSUMMER: the full game — adds the Faerie Bridge path, conjured stones,

   rune powers, and Faerie Magik. */

const MODES = {

  masquerade: {

    id:'masquerade', name:'Faerie Masquerade',

    tracks:['Faerie Ring','Faerie Fort','Faerie Mound'],

    runePowers:false, magik:true, conjuredStart:false, reactionWindows:true,

    completionMagik:true,     // every completed dance grants a Faerie Magik card

  },

  midsummer: {

    id:'midsummer', name:'Midsummer Dance',

    tracks:ALL_TRACKS,

    runePowers:true, magik:true, conjuredStart:true, reactionWindows:true,

    completionMagik:false,    // Magik flows from the Faerie Bridge path instead

  },

};

/* TRACKS reflects the active mode; defaults to the full set until a game boots. */

let TRACKS = ALL_TRACKS;

const SLOTS = 10;                            // stone stations available along each spiral groove

function trackLen(tr){ return G.steps[tr].length; }

function mkTrack(isConjured, len){ return Array(len||6).fill(null).map(()=>({c:!!isConjured})); }

const HOUSES = [

  {id:'mountain', name:'Mountain Court', css:'#6d4a7a', hex:0x6d4a7a},

  {id:'meadow',   name:'Meadow Court',   css:'#7a8a34', hex:0x7a8a34},

  {id:'river',    name:'River Court',    css:'#2f6f8a', hex:0x2f6f8a},

];

const HOUSE_BY_ID = Object.fromEntries(HOUSES.map(h=>[h.id,h]));

const AI_NAMES = ['Thistle','Bramblewyn','Elderlight','Nightmoth','Fernshade'];

/* True Names bestowed by the High Fae on the winner — invented coinages in

   Welsh & Gaelic orthography, chosen to be gorgeous and unpronounceable.

   The epithet is drawn from the Court in which the True Name was called,

   so the title always echoes the winner's Court. */

const TRUE_NAMES = [

  'Llywarchwen','Gwenddolau','Rhoswyddlan','Bleiddwynne','Myfyrniawg','Ynyswyllt',

  'Aoibhneas\u00e1n','S\u00ecthbheartach','Niamhsheolta','Faoildhearg','Caoimhrialta',

];

const TRUE_EPITHETS = {

  mountain: [

    'of the Hollow Hills','of the Sleeping Peaks','of the Windworn Crag',

    'of the Thunder-Crowned Heights','of the Deep Granite Halls',

    'of the Last High Pass','of the Starlit Summit'

  meadow: [

    'of the Clover Crown','of the Golden Furrows'

    'of the Reed-Sung Shallows','of the Deepwater Song',

  ],

};

function bestowTrueName(courtId){

  const pool = TRUE_EPITHETS[courtId] || TRUE_EPITHETS.forest;

  return pick(TRUE_NAMES)+' '+pick(pool);

}

const PLAYER_COLORS = ['#8763c6','#d97b33','#3fa7a0','#c75b8b','#cfc6ae','#5b6b8c'];

const INTRIGUE_DEFS = {

  'Midsummer Reel':    {n:2, d:'Choose your dance steps (1\u20136) and dance in place of a Fae Rune. The chosen rune\u2019s gift applies (its stone gifts are optional here).'},

  'Whispered Lore':    {n:2, d:'Search the Faerie Magik discards and take one. Play during your turn.'},

  'Bountiful Harvest': {n:2, d:'Gain 3 dance steps. Play anytime during your turn.'},

};

/* Cards playable at any moment — even on rivals' turns (interrupts + host validation). */

const ANYTIME=['Scrying Pool','Wisp-Lure','Snuff Out','Wisp-Call'];

 

let G = null;          // game state

let SCENE = null;      // 3D handles

let EPOCH = 0;         // generation counter — bumped by newGame(); stale async turn logic checks it and bails

let INTERRUPT_BUSY = false;   // true while an anytime-Magik interrupt dialog is open

 

/* ---------- utilities ---------- */

const $ = s => document.querySelector(s);

const wait = ms => new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,ms));

const shuffle = a => { for(let i=a.length-1;i>0;i--){const j=Math.floor(Math.random()*(i+1));[a[i],a[j]]=[a[j],a[i]];} return a; };

const rint = n => Math.floor(Math.random()*n);

const pick = a => a[rint(a.length)];

const d6 = () => 1+rint(6);

class GameOver extends Error {}

 

function log(msg, cls){

  const p=document.createElement('p'); if(cls)p.className=cls; p.innerHTML=msg;

  $('#logbody').appendChild(p); $('#logbody').scrollTop=1e9;

  // Minimized turn updates: the latest line rides on the Telling's toggle pill.

  const lt=$('#logticker');

  if(lt) lt.textContent=String(msg).replace(/<[^>]*>/g,'').slice(0,80);

}

function banner(t){

  const b=$('#banner'); b.textContent=t; b.style.opacity=1;

  b.style.pointerEvents='auto';   // draggable while visible

  clearTimeout(b._t); b._t=setTimeout(()=>{ b.style.opacity=0; b.style.pointerEvents='none'; }, 2200);

}

 

/* A slider question in the same modal chrome as choose(). Resolves the number, or null on Back. */

function sliderChoose(title, desc, min, max, val, fmt){

  /* Renders INTO the shared modal skeleton (#mtitle/#mdesc/#opts) and cleans

     up after itself, so choose() always finds the skeleton intact. */

  return new Promise(res=>{

    const wrap=$('#modalwrap');

    $('#mtitle').textContent=title;

    $('#mdesc').innerHTML=desc;

    const box=$('#opts'); box.innerHTML=`

      <div style="padding:10px 4px 2px;">

        <div id="slval" style="font-family:var(--disp); letter-spacing:.08em; font-size:13px; color:var(--gold); margin-bottom:8px; text-align:center;"></div>

        <input id="slrange" type="range" min="${min}" max="${max}" step="1" value="${val}" style="width:100%; accent-color:#d8b45a;">

      </div>

      <div style="display:flex; gap:10px; margin-top:14px;">

        <button class="btn" id="slback" style="flex:1;">Back</button>

        <button class="btn gold" id="slok" style="flex:2;">Begin</button>

      </div>`;

    const paint=()=>{ $('#slval').textContent=fmt(+$('#slrange').value); };

    $('#slrange').oninput=paint; paint();

    const done=v=>{ box.innerHTML=''; wrap.style.display='none'; res(v); };

    $('#slok').onclick=()=>done(+$('#slrange').value);

    $('#slback').onclick=()=>done(null);

    wrap.style.display='flex';

  });

}

/* ---------- modal choice (promise-based) ----------

   opts: [{label, sub, value, cls}] ; returns chosen value.

   choose() is SERIALIZED: if a modal is already open (e.g. the human opened an

   anytime-Magik confirmation during an AI turn) and a second choose() arrives

   (e.g. the AI's completed dance raises a reaction popup), the second call waits

   in a queue for the first to resolve instead of overwriting its buttons. This

   prevents orphaned promises — the old cause of a permanent INTERRUPT_BUSY lock. */

let CHOOSE_CHAIN = Promise.resolve();

function choose(title, desc, opts, modalCls, ctl){

  if(!opts || !opts.length) return Promise.resolve(null); // never freeze on an empty choice

  let cancelled=false, live=null;

  if(ctl) ctl.cancel=()=>{           // cancels THIS choose only: queued (never shows) or active (closes)

    cancelled=true;

    if(live){ const r=live; live=null;

      if(ACTIVE_CHOOSE===r) ACTIVE_CHOOSE=null;

      $('#modalwrap').style.display='none';

      r(null);

    }

  };

  const run = ()=> new Promise(res=>{

    if(cancelled){ res(null); return; }

    if(typeof clockExpired==='function' && clockExpired()){ res(null); return; }  // expired mid-queue

    live=res;

    ACTIVE_CHOOSE=res;

    $('#modal').className = 'panel' + (modalCls? ' '+modalCls : '');

    $('#mtitle').textContent=title; $('#mdesc').innerHTML=desc||'';

    const box=$('#opts'); box.innerHTML='';

    opts.forEach(o=>{

      const b=document.createElement('button');

      b.className='opt'+(o.cls?' '+o.cls:'');

      b.innerHTML=`<div class="ot">${o.label}</div>`+(o.sub?`<div class="os">${o.sub}</div>`:'');

      b.onclick=()=>{ live=null; ACTIVE_CHOOSE=null; $('#modalwrap').style.display='none'; res(o.value); };

      box.appendChild(b);

    });

    $('#modalwrap').style.display='flex';

    const _m=$('#modal');

    if(_m.style.position==='fixed'){

      const r=_m.getBoundingClientRect();

      if(r.left<4) _m.style.left='4px';

      if(r.top<4) _m.style.top='4px';

      if(r.left>window.innerWidth-120) _m.style.left=(window.innerWidth-Math.min(r.width,window.innerWidth-8))+'px';

      if(r.top>window.innerHeight-120) _m.style.top=Math.max(4, window.innerHeight-r.height-8)+'px';

    }

    const first=box.querySelector('.opt'); if(first) first.focus();

  });

  // Chain onto any in-flight modal; the result is this call's own resolution.

  const result = CHOOSE_CHAIN.then(run);

  CHOOSE_CHAIN = result.catch(()=>{});   // keep the chain alive even if a link rejects

  return result;

}

async function notice(title, desc, btn='Continue', ctl){

  await choose(title, desc, [{label:btn, value:1}], undefined, ctl);

}

 

/* ---------- state helpers ---------- */

function quorum(){ return (G && G.qN) || 5; }

function coupAt(){ return quorum()+2; }

function others(p){ return G.players.filter(q=>q!==p); }

function drawFrom(deck, discard){

  if(!deck.length){ deck.push(...shuffle(discard.splice(0))); }

  return deck.pop();

}

function housesAtQuorum(){ return HOUSES.filter(h=>G.nobles[h.id]>=quorum()); }

function fmtP(p){ return `<b style="color:${p.color}">${p.name}</b>`; }

function fmtH(id){ const h=HOUSE_BY_ID[id]; return `<b style="color:${h.css}">${h.name}</b>`; }

 

/* Everyone can see every OTHER player's status. An AI's belief about its

   own status = mean of the statuses it cannot see (its own + the pile). */

function unseenStatuses(p){

  const visible = others(p).map(q=>q.status);

  const all=[1,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9];

  return all.filter(s=>!visible.includes(s));

}

function selfEstimate(p){

  if(p.knownStatus!==null) return p.knownStatus;

  const u=unseenStatuses(p); return u.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0)/u.length;

}

 

/* ---------- setup ---------- */

function newGame(nPlayers, modeId, opts){

  opts = opts || {};

  const qN = Math.min(10, Math.max(5, +opts.quorum || 5));

  const humanSeats = opts.humanSeats || [0];

  const seatNames = opts.names || {};

  EPOCH++;   // invalidate any in-flight turn logic from a previous game

  const mode = MODES[modeId] || MODES.midsummer;

  TRACKS = mode.tracks;

  const statusDeck=shuffle([1,2,3,4,5,6,7,8,9]);

  const houseDeck=shuffle(HOUSES.flatMap(h=>[h.id,h.id,h.id,h.id]));

  const intrigueDeck = mode.magik

    ? shuffle(Object.entries(INTRIGUE_DEFS).flatMap(([k,v])=>Array(v.n).fill(k)))

    : [];

  const players=[];

  for(let i=0;i<nPlayers;i++){

    players.push({

      i, isHuman: humanSeats.includes(i),

      name: seatNames[i] || (humanSeats.includes(i) ? (i===MY_SEAT?'You':'Player '+(i+1)) : AI_NAMES[(i-1+AI_NAMES.length)%AI_NAMES.length]),

      color: PLAYER_COLORS[i],

      house: houseDeck.pop(),

      status: statusDeck.pop(),

      knownStatus: null,                    // what this player knows about their OWN status

      intrigues: mode.magik ? [intrigueDeck.pop()] : [],

      hand:[1,2,3,4,5,6], discard:[],

      cands: [{track:null,steps:0},{track:null,steps:0}],

      knownHouses:{},                       // houses learned about others, {playerIndex: houseId}

    });

  }

  const steps={};

  mode.tracks.forEach(tr=>{ steps[tr]=mkTrack(tr==='Faerie Bridge' && mode.conjuredStart, tr==='Faerie Bridge'?7:6); });   // the Bridge runs seven stones: no rune crosses it in one turn

  G = {

    mode,

    players, qN, statusDeck, houseDeck, intrigueDeck,

    statusDiscard:[], houseDiscard:[], intrigueDiscard:[],

    nobles:{mountain:0,meadow:0,forest:0,river:0},

    /* Public behavioral evidence: how many Wisps each player has placed into

       each Court. Placements are visible to everyone, so every AI may use this

       to infer allegiances — it is table-reading, not cheating. */

    placeEvidence: players.map(()=>({mountain:0,meadow:0,forest:0,river:0})),

    steps,

    turn: rint(nPlayers), over:false, round:1,

  };

  log(`The Midsummer die is cast: ${fmtP(players[G.turn])} shall dance first.`, 'sys');

  log(`A True Name may be called at <b>${quorum()}</b> Wisps in a Court, and the <b>${coupAt()}th</b> Wisp placed in a Court forces the Call there at once.`, 'sys');

}

 

/* ============================================================

   Part B: 3D throne room (three.js r128)

   ============================================================ */

function textSprite(text, color='#e9dcbe', size=64, letter=6){

  const c=document.createElement('canvas'); c.width=512; c.height=128;

  const x=c.getContext('2d');

  x.font=`700 ${size}px Cinzel, Georgia, serif`;

  x.textAlign='center'; x.textBaseline='middle';

  x.fillStyle=color; x.shadowColor='rgba(0,0,0,.7)'; x.shadowBlur=8;

  const chars=text.split('').join(String.fromCharCode(8202).repeat(letter?1:0));

  x.fillText(chars,256,64);

  const tex=new THREE.CanvasTexture(c); tex.minFilter=THREE.LinearFilter;

  const m=new THREE.Sprite(new THREE.SpriteMaterial({map:tex,transparent:true,depthWrite:false}));

  m.scale.set(3.4,0.85,1); return m;

}

 

let PICK = null; // System for 3D element selection: { mode, filter, resolve }

/* The four dances form a symmetrical four-arm cross.

   Each arm starts N/S/E/W as a straight line across the court boundaries,

   then curls 180° inward to the standing stones. */

const ARM_BASE={

  'Faerie Fort':  -Math.PI/2,  // North

  'Faerie Ring':  0,           // East

  'Faerie Bridge': Math.PI/2,   // South

  'Faerie Mound': Math.PI      // West

};

const ARM_SWEEP=Math.PI, R_OUT=6.2, R_IN=1.8;

function spiralPoint(track, t){ // t in 0..1 from outer edge to the stones

  const base = ARM_BASE[track];

  if(t < 0.25){

    // Straight line from boundary to start of the spiral

    const r = R_OUT + 0.25 * (1 - t/0.25);

    return {x:Math.cos(base)*r, z:Math.sin(base)*r};

  } else {

    // 180 degree curl inwards

    const st = (t - 0.25) / 0.75;

    const a = base + ARM_SWEEP * st;

    const r = R_OUT - (R_OUT - R_IN) * st;

    return {x:Math.cos(a)*r, z:Math.sin(a)*r};

  }

}

/* Stones sit at stations spaced by EQUAL ARC LENGTH along the groove. */

const SLOT_T=(()=>{

  const N=600, ts=[0], lens=[0];

  let prev=null, total=0;

  for(let i=0;i<=N;i++){

    const t=i/N;

    let a, r;

    if(t<0.25){

      a=0; r=R_OUT + 0.25*(1 - t/0.25);

    } else {

      const st=(t-0.25)/0.75;

      a=ARM_SWEEP*st; r=R_OUT - (R_OUT-R_IN)*st;

    }

    const p={x:Math.cos(a)*r, z:Math.sin(a)*r};

    if(prev){ total+=Math.hypot(p.x-prev.x,p.z-prev.z); }

    prev=p; ts.push(t); lens.push(total);

  }

  const out=[];

  for(let s=0;s<SLOTS;s++){

    const target=total*s/(SLOTS-1);

    let i=lens.findIndex(l=>l>=target); if(i<0)i=lens.length-1;

    out.push(ts[Math.min(i,ts.length-1)]);

  }

  return out;

})();

function slotPoint(track, slot){ // slot 1..SLOTS, 1 = outermost

  const t=SLOT_T[slot-1];

  const base=ARM_BASE[track];

  if(t<0.25){

    const r=R_OUT + 0.25*(1 - t/0.25);

    return {x:Math.cos(base)*r, z:Math.sin(base)*r};

  } else {

    const st=(t-0.25)/0.75;

    const a=base+ARM_SWEEP*st, r=R_OUT-(R_OUT-R_IN)*st;

    return {x:Math.cos(a)*r, z:Math.sin(a)*r};

  }

}

function tilePos(track, step){

  return slotPoint(track, SLOTS - trackLen(track) + step);

}

 

/* ============ THE NIGHT GLADE ============

   Sky dome, stars, forest rim, mist, moon, fireflies, meteors, ritual ring —

   everything the prologue promises the glade to be. One dome mesh, one star

   draw call (tiny shader for per-star twinkle), one merged tree silhouette,

   four mist sprites, two firefly clouds, one meteor sprite: cheap on phones.

   Under prefers-reduced-motion the night stands perfectly still. */

function buildNightGlade(scene, camera, cam){

  const softDot=(()=>{ const c=document.createElement('canvas'); c.width=c.height=64; const x=c.getContext('2d');

    const g=x.createRadialGradient(32,32,0,32,32,32);

    g.addColorStop(0,'rgba(255,255,255,1)'); g.addColorStop(.35,'rgba(255,255,255,.85)'); g.addColorStop(1,'rgba(255,255,255,0)');

    x.fillStyle=g; x.fillRect(0,0,64,64);

    return new THREE.CanvasTexture(c); })();

  // sky dome: dusk-violet horizon rising to near-black zenith, one cool afterglow low in the west

  { const c=document.createElement('canvas'); c.width=1024; c.height=512; const x=c.getContext('2d');

    const g=x.createLinearGradient(0,512,0,0);

    g.addColorStop(0,'#2a1e4e'); g.addColorStop(.25,'#1d1440'); g.addColorStop(.55,'#120c28'); g.addColorStop(1,'#070510');

    x.fillStyle=g; x.fillRect(0,0,1024,512);

    const r=x.createRadialGradient(300,505,20, 300,505,360);

    r.addColorStop(0,'rgba(110,140,150,.5)'); r.addColorStop(.45,'rgba(70,100,120,.22)'); r.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');

    x.fillStyle=r; x.fillRect(0,0,1024,512);

    const dome=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.SphereGeometry(230,32,20),

      new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({map:new THREE.CanvasTexture(c), side:THREE.BackSide, fog:false, depthWrite:false}));

    dome.renderOrder=-10; scene.add(dome); }

  // stars: one draw call; per-star size, tint, and twinkle in a tiny shader

  const starUniforms={ uTime:{value:0} };

  { const N=1500, NB=800, R=224;

    const pos=[], size=[], phase=[], tw=[], tint=[];

    const push=(p,s,ph,twk,col)=>{ pos.push(p[0],p[1],p[2]); size.push(s); phase.push(ph); tw.push(twk); tint.push(col[0],col[1],col[2]); };

    const onSphere=()=>{ let x,y,z;

      do{ const u=Math.random()*2-1, a=Math.random()*Math.PI*2, q=Math.sqrt(1-u*u);

          x=q*Math.cos(a); y=u; z=q*Math.sin(a); }while(y<-0.04);

      return [x*R,y*R,z*R]; };

    for(let i=0;i<N;i++){

      const big=Math.random()<.045, mid=!big&&Math.random()<.2;

      const s= big? 3.4+Math.random()*1.8 : mid? 2.0+Math.random()*.8 : 1.05+Math.random()*.7;

      const warm=Math.random()<.18, cool=!warm&&Math.random()<.3;

      const col= warm? [1,.92,.78] : cool? [.8,.88,1] : [.95,.95,1];

      push(onSphere(), s, Math.random()*6.283, big? .55 : mid? .3 : .15, col);

    }

    const n=new THREE.Vector3(.35,.62,.55).normalize();

    const u=new THREE.Vector3(1,0,0).sub(n.clone().multiplyScalar(n.x)).normalize();

    const v=new THREE.Vector3().crossVectors(n,u);

    for(let i=0;i<NB;i++){

      const a=Math.random()*6.283;

      const gg=(Math.random()+Math.random()+Math.random()-1.5)/1.5*.16;

      const p=u.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.cos(a)).add(v.clone().multiplyScalar(Math.sin(a))).add(n.clone().multiplyScalar(gg)).normalize();

      if(p.y<-0.04) continue;

      push([p.x*R,p.y*R,p.z*R], .9+Math.random()*.6, Math.random()*6.283, .1, [.82,.82,.95]);

    }

    const geo=new THREE.BufferGeometry();

    geo.setAttribute('position', new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(pos,3));

    geo.setAttribute('aSize', new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(size,1));

    geo.setAttribute('aPhase', new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(phase,1));

    geo.setAttribute('aTw', new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(tw,1));

    geo.setAttribute('aTint', new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(tint,3));

    const mat=new THREE.ShaderMaterial({

      uniforms:starUniforms, transparent:true, depthWrite:false, blending:THREE.AdditiveBlending, fog:false,

      vertexShader:'attribute float aSize; attribute float aPhase; attribute float aTw; attribute vec3 aTint;\n'+

        'varying float vPhase; varying float vTw; varying vec3 vTint;\n'+

        'void main(){ vPhase=aPhase; vTw=aTw; vTint=aTint;\n'+

        '  vec4 mv=modelViewMatrix*vec4(position,1.0);\n'+

        '  gl_PointSize=aSize*(470.0/max(1.0,-mv.z));\n'+

        '  gl_Position=projectionMatrix*mv; }',

      fragmentShader:'uniform float uTime; varying float vPhase; varying float vTw; varying vec3 vTint;\n'+

        'void main(){ float d=length(gl_PointCoord-vec2(.5));\n'+

        '  float a=smoothstep(.5,.12,d);\n'+

        '  a*=1.0-vTw*(0.5+0.5*sin(uTime*1.6+vPhase))*0.8;\n'+

        '  gl_FragColor=vec4(vTint, a*0.9); }' });

    const stars=new THREE.Points(geo, mat); stars.renderOrder=-9; scene.add(stars); }

  // the moon: a soft lantern hung where the moonlight already falls from

  { const c=document.createElement('canvas'); c.width=c.height=256; const x=c.getContext('2d');

    const g=x.createRadialGradient(128,128,10,128,128,128);

    g.addColorStop(0,'rgba(236,240,255,.95)'); g.addColorStop(.18,'rgba(214,222,250,.8)');

    g.addColorStop(.34,'rgba(170,180,230,.28)'); g.addColorStop(1,'rgba(140,150,220,0)');

    x.fillStyle=g; x.fillRect(0,0,256,256);

    const moon=new THREE.Sprite(new THREE.SpriteMaterial({map:new THREE.CanvasTexture(c), transparent:true, depthWrite:false, fog:false, opacity:.95}));

    // low on the far sky (the visible band), not 54° up behind the viewer

    moon.position.set(Math.sin(2.55)*Math.cos(.26), Math.sin(.26), Math.cos(2.55)*Math.cos(.26)).multiplyScalar(216);

    moon.scale.set(34,34,1); moon.renderOrder=-8; scene.add(moon); }

  // the forest rim: dark silhouettes merged into a single mesh around the glade

  { const deIndex=g=>g.index? g.toNonIndexed() : g;   // r128: polyhedra are born non-indexed

    const cone=deIndex(new THREE.ConeGeometry(1,1,7));

    const blob=deIndex(new THREE.IcosahedronGeometry(.62,0));

    const posArr=[]; const M=new THREE.Matrix4(); const Q=new THREE.Quaternion();

    const S=new THREE.Vector3(); const P=new THREE.Vector3(); const V=new THREE.Vector3();

    const addShape=(g,px,py,pz,sx,sy,sz,ry)=>{

      M.compose(P.set(px,py,pz), Q.setFromEuler(new THREE.Euler(0,ry,0)), S.set(sx,sy,sz));

      const a=g.attributes.position.array;

      for(let i=0;i<a.length;i+=3){ V.set(a[i],a[i+1],a[i+2]).applyMatrix4(M); posArr.push(V.x,V.y,V.z); } };

    for(let i=0;i<52;i++){

      const a=(i/52)*6.283 + Math.random()*.09;

      const r=18.5+Math.random()*5.5;

      const px=Math.cos(a)*r, pz=Math.sin(a)*r;

      const h=2.6+Math.random()*3.8;

      if(Math.random()<.72) addShape(cone, px, -0.25+h/2, pz, .9+Math.random()*.9, h, .9+Math.random()*.9, Math.random()*6.283);

      else addShape(blob, px, -0.25+h*.42, pz, 1.5+Math.random(), h*.8, 1.5+Math.random(), Math.random()*6.283);

    }

    const geo=new THREE.BufferGeometry();

    geo.setAttribute('position', new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(posArr,3));

    geo.computeVertexNormals();

    scene.add(new THREE.Mesh(geo, new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0x0b1410, roughness:1}))); }

  // the ritual ring: faint gold glyphs engraved in the grass around the board

  { const c=document.createElement('canvas'); c.width=c.height=1024; const x=c.getContext('2d');

    const cx=512;

    x.strokeStyle='rgba(216,180,90,.55)'; x.lineWidth=2;

    x.beginPath(); x.arc(cx,cx,461,0,6.283); x.stroke();

    x.beginPath(); x.arc(cx,cx,507,0,6.283); x.stroke();

    x.lineWidth=2.6; x.lineCap='round';

    for(let i=0;i<44;i++){

      const a=(i/44)*6.283;

      x.save(); x.translate(cx+Math.cos(a)*484, cx+Math.sin(a)*484); x.rotate(a+Math.PI/2);

      x.beginPath(); x.moveTo(0,-11); x.lineTo(0,11);

      const nb=1+(Math.random()*3|0);

      for(let b=0;b<nb;b++){ const y0=-9+Math.random()*18;

        x.moveTo(0,y0); x.lineTo((Math.random()<.5?-1:1)*(4+Math.random()*5), y0+(Math.random()<.5?-1:1)*(3+Math.random()*6)); }

      x.stroke(); x.restore();

    }

    const ring=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.RingGeometry(12.15,13.55,96),

      new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({map:new THREE.CanvasTexture(c), transparent:true, opacity:.5, depthWrite:false}));

    ring.rotation.x=-Math.PI/2; ring.position.y=-0.24;

    scene.add(ring); }

  // mist: slow pale veils drifting around the rim

  const mists=[];

  { const c=document.createElement('canvas'); c.width=256; c.height=64; const x=c.getContext('2d');

    const g=x.createRadialGradient(128,32,4,128,32,120);

    g.addColorStop(0,'rgba(200,205,235,.55)'); g.addColorStop(.5,'rgba(180,185,220,.22)'); g.addColorStop(1,'rgba(160,170,210,0)');

    x.fillStyle=g; x.save(); x.translate(128,32); x.scale(1,.42); x.translate(-128,-32); x.fillRect(-200,-100,700,300); x.restore();

    const tex=new THREE.CanvasTexture(c);

    for(let i=0;i<4;i++){

      const s=new THREE.Sprite(new THREE.SpriteMaterial({map:tex, transparent:true, opacity:.075, depthWrite:false, fog:false}));

      s.scale.set(12+Math.random()*5, 3.4, 1);

      mists.push({s, a:Math.random()*6.283, r:14.5+Math.random()*3, y:.25+Math.random()*.9, w:.00006+Math.random()*.00005});

      scene.add(s);

    } }

  // fireflies: two small clouds blinking out of phase, kept off the play field

  const moteClouds=[];

  for(let ci=0;ci<2;ci++){

    const n=20, base=[], seed=[];

    for(let i=0;i<n;i++){

      const a=Math.random()*6.283, r=11.8+Math.random()*4.7;

      base.push(Math.cos(a)*r, .3+Math.random()*2.1, Math.sin(a)*r);   // lifted: silhouetted on the tree line

      seed.push(Math.random()*6.283, .4+Math.random()*.8);

    }

    const geo=new THREE.BufferGeometry();

    geo.setAttribute('position', new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(base.slice(),3));

    const pts=new THREE.Points(geo, new THREE.PointsMaterial({map:softDot, color:0xd9edaa, size:.42,

      transparent:true, opacity:0, depthWrite:false, blending:THREE.AdditiveBlending, sizeAttenuation:true}));

    scene.add(pts);

    moteClouds.push({pts, base, seed, off:ci*2.2});

  }

  // a shooting star, now and then

  const meteor=new THREE.Sprite(new THREE.SpriteMaterial({map:(()=>{

      const c=document.createElement('canvas'); c.width=128; c.height=32; const x=c.getContext('2d');

      const g=x.createLinearGradient(0,16,128,16);

      g.addColorStop(0,'rgba(255,255,255,0)'); g.addColorStop(.75,'rgba(230,238,255,.55)');

      g.addColorStop(.94,'rgba(255,255,255,.95)'); g.addColorStop(1,'rgba(255,255,255,0)');

      x.fillStyle=g; x.save(); x.translate(64,16); x.scale(1,.2); x.translate(-64,-16); x.fillRect(-200,-100,700,300); x.restore();

      return new THREE.CanvasTexture(c); })(),

    transparent:true, opacity:0, depthWrite:false, fog:false, blending:THREE.AdditiveBlending}));

  meteor.scale.set(11,1.9,1); scene.add(meteor);

  const met={next:-1, t0:0, dur:900, p0:new THREE.Vector3(), p1:new THREE.Vector3(), live:false};

  function update(t, dt, reduced){

    if(reduced) return;                       // a perfectly still night for reduced-motion folk

    starUniforms.uTime.value=t*0.001;

    mists.forEach(m=>{ m.a+=m.w*dt*1000;

      m.s.position.set(Math.cos(m.a)*m.r, m.y+Math.sin(t*.0004+m.a*3)*.12, Math.sin(m.a)*m.r); });

    moteClouds.forEach(mc=>{

      const arr=mc.pts.geometry.attributes.position.array;

      for(let i=0;i<arr.length/3;i++){

        arr[i*3]  =mc.base[i*3]  +Math.sin(t*.00035*mc.seed[i*2+1]+mc.seed[i*2])*.5;

        arr[i*3+1]=mc.base[i*3+1]+Math.sin(t*.00055*mc.seed[i*2+1]+mc.seed[i*2]*2.0)*.3;

        arr[i*3+2]=mc.base[i*3+2]+Math.cos(t*.0003*mc.seed[i*2+1]+mc.seed[i*2])*.5;

      }

      mc.pts.geometry.attributes.position.needsUpdate=true;

      mc.pts.material.opacity=.16+.55*Math.max(0,Math.sin(t*.0009+mc.off));

    });

    if(met.next<0) met.next=t+4000+Math.random()*6000;   // the first star falls soon after the glade wakes

    if(!met.live && t>met.next){

      met.live=true; met.t0=t;

      // the camera looks DOWN at the board: the only sky it sees is the low

      // band on the FAR side, just above the tree line — spawn there

      const az=cam.theta+Math.PI+(Math.random()-.5)*1.8;

      const el=.07+Math.random()*.21;

      met.p0.set(Math.sin(az)*Math.cos(el), Math.sin(el), Math.cos(az)*Math.cos(el)).multiplyScalar(205);

      const tang=new THREE.Vector3(Math.cos(az),0,-Math.sin(az)).multiplyScalar(66*(Math.random()<.5?1:-1));

      met.p1.copy(met.p0).add(tang).add(new THREE.Vector3(0,-9,0));

    }

    if(met.live){

      const k=(t-met.t0)/met.dur;

      if(k>=1){ met.live=false; meteor.material.opacity=0; met.next=t+9000+Math.random()*17000; }

      else{

        meteor.position.lerpVectors(met.p0, met.p1, k);

        meteor.material.opacity=Math.sin(Math.PI*k)*.85;

        const pa=met.p0.clone().project(camera), pb=met.p1.clone().project(camera);

        meteor.material.rotation=Math.atan2(pb.y-pa.y, pb.x-pa.x);

      }

    }

  }

  return {update};

}

function init3D(mode){

  mode = mode || MODES.midsummer;

  const holder=$('#c3d');

  const renderer=new THREE.WebGLRenderer({antialias:true});

  renderer.setPixelRatio(Math.min(devicePixelRatio,2));

  renderer.setSize(innerWidth,innerHeight);

  renderer.shadowMap.enabled=true;

  holder.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

 

  const scene=new THREE.Scene();

  const iconHitList=[];

  scene.background=new THREE.Color(0x120c1c);

  scene.body=null;

  scene.fog=new THREE.Fog(0x1d1440, 30, 52);   // the horizon dusk: the rim melts into sky, not void

 

  const camera=new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(45, innerWidth/innerHeight, .1, 300);

  const cam={theta:0, phi:0.9, r:21};

  function placeCam(){

    camera.position.set(cam.r*Math.sin(cam.phi)*Math.sin(cam.theta),

                        cam.r*Math.cos(cam.phi),

                        cam.r*Math.sin(cam.phi)*Math.cos(cam.theta));

    camera.lookAt(0,0,0);

  }

  placeCam();

 

  scene.add(new THREE.AmbientLight(0x9a90c8,.6));

  const sun=new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xcfd8ff,.55);

  sun.position.set(6,14,8); sun.castShadow=true;

  sun.shadow.mapSize.set(1024,1024);

  sun.shadow.camera.left=-10; sun.shadow.camera.right=10;

  sun.shadow.camera.top=10; sun.shadow.camera.bottom=-10;

  scene.add(sun);

  const crownGlow=new THREE.PointLight(0xffe08a,.9,9); crownGlow.position.set(0,2,0); scene.add(crownGlow);

 

  // the glade floor: moonlit grass falling away to shadow at the rim

  const grassTex=(()=>{ const c=document.createElement('canvas'); c.width=c.height=512; const x=c.getContext('2d');

    const g=x.createRadialGradient(256,256,30,256,256,256);

    g.addColorStop(0,'#1d2c12'); g.addColorStop(.5,'#18240e'); g.addColorStop(.78,'#101a0a'); g.addColorStop(1,'#070c06');

    x.fillStyle=g; x.fillRect(0,0,512,512);

    for(let i=0;i<1100;i++){ const a=Math.random()*6.283, r=Math.pow(Math.random(),.6)*252;

      const px=256+Math.cos(a)*r, py=256+Math.sin(a)*r, k=1-r/256;

      x.fillStyle='rgba('+(26+Math.random()*30|0)+','+(40+Math.random()*34|0)+','+(16+Math.random()*16|0)+','+(.10+.14*k).toFixed(2)+')';

      x.beginPath(); x.arc(px,py,.8+Math.random()*2.2,0,6.283); x.fill(); }

    return new THREE.CanvasTexture(c); })();

  const tableSide=new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0x090e07, roughness:1});

  const tableTop=new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({map:grassTex, roughness:.95});

  const table=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(16,16,.6,48), [tableSide, tableTop, tableSide]);

  table.position.y=-0.55; table.receiveShadow=true; scene.add(table);

  const glade=buildNightGlade(scene, camera, cam);

 

  // board base (parchment border)

  const base=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(15.7,.35,15.7),

    new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0x4a3f63,roughness:.8}));

  base.position.y=-0.18; base.receiveShadow=true; base.castShadow=true; scene.add(base);

  const inner=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(12.9,.06,12.9),

    new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0x171026,roughness:.9}));

  inner.position.y=0.015; inner.receiveShadow=true; scene.add(inner);

 

  // gold frame strips at the outer rim and around the play field

  const frameMat=new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0xb8923f,metalness:.7,roughness:.4});

  [15.45, 13.08].forEach(s=>{

    [[s,0.12,0,s/2-.06],[s,0.12,0,-(s/2-.06)],[0.12,s,s/2-.06,0],[0.12,s,-(s/2-.06),0]].forEach(([w,d,px,pz])=>{

      const bar=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(w,.04,d), frameMat);

      bar.position.set(px,.005,pz); scene.add(bar);

    });

  });

 

  function drawIcon(g, kind, cx, cy){

    g.save(); g.translate(cx,cy);

    g.lineWidth=5.5; g.lineJoin=g.lineCap='round';

    g.strokeStyle='rgba(216,180,90,.45)'; g.strokeRect(-34,-34,68,68);

    g.strokeStyle='rgba(216,180,90,.95)'; g.fillStyle='rgba(216,180,90,.95)';

    if(kind==='swap'){

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(-22,-10); g.lineTo(16,-10); g.moveTo(8,-19); g.lineTo(18,-10); g.lineTo(8,-1); g.stroke();

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(22,10); g.lineTo(-16,10); g.moveTo(-8,1); g.lineTo(-18,10); g.lineTo(-8,19); g.stroke();

    }

    if(kind==='draw'){

      g.strokeRect(-24,-20,26,40);

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(6,0); g.lineTo(26,0); g.moveTo(18,-8); g.lineTo(27,0); g.lineTo(18,8); g.stroke();

    }

    if(kind==='force'){

      g.beginPath(); g.arc(-12,-10,8,0,6.3); g.stroke();

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(-24,20); g.quadraticCurveTo(-12,2,0,20); g.stroke();

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(6,-8); g.lineTo(26,-8); g.moveTo(18,-16); g.lineTo(27,-8); g.lineTo(18,0); g.stroke();

    }

    if(kind==='eye'){

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(-24,0); g.quadraticCurveTo(0,-20,24,0); g.quadraticCurveTo(0,20,-24,0); g.stroke();

      g.beginPath(); g.arc(0,0,6,0,6.3); g.fill();

    }

    if(kind==='x'){

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(-16,-16); g.lineTo(16,16); g.moveTo(16,-16); g.lineTo(-16,16); g.stroke();

    }

    if(kind==='die'){

      g.strokeRect(-20,-20,40,40);

      [[-9,-9],[9,-9],[0,0],[-9,9],[9,9]].forEach(([a,b])=>{g.beginPath(); g.arc(a,b,4,0,6.3); g.fill();});

    }

    if(kind==='flip'){

      g.beginPath(); g.arc(-4,-4,13,0,Math.PI*2); g.stroke();

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(2,2); g.lineTo(20,20); g.stroke();

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(9,20); g.lineTo(20,20); g.lineTo(20,9); g.stroke();

    }

    if(kind==='move'){

      g.beginPath(); g.arc(-13,0,10,0,Math.PI*2); g.stroke();

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(0,0); g.lineTo(21,0); g.stroke();

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(13,-8); g.lineTo(21,0); g.lineTo(13,8); g.stroke();

    }

    g.restore();

  }

  /* ---- corner ornaments: gossamer tendrils curling from each corner of the

     border toward the side titles. Pure decoration; never raycast. ---- */

  function cornerOrnamentTexture(){

    const S=1024, c=document.createElement('canvas'); c.width=c.height=S;

    const g=c.getContext('2d');

    const gold=(a)=>`rgba(216,180,90,${a})`, pale=(a)=>`rgba(245,230,184,${a})`;

    g.lineCap='round';

    function wisp(x,y,r,a){

      const rg=g.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,r);

      rg.addColorStop(0,pale(a)); rg.addColorStop(1,pale(0));

      g.fillStyle=rg; g.beginPath(); g.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); g.fill();

    }

    function leaf(x,y,len,ang,a){

      g.save(); g.translate(x,y); g.rotate(ang);

      g.fillStyle=gold(a);

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(0,0);

      g.quadraticCurveTo(len*0.5,-len*0.34, len,0);

      g.quadraticCurveTo(len*0.5, len*0.34, 0,0);

      g.fill(); g.restore();

    }

    function curl(x,y,r,turns,dir,a,w){

      g.strokeStyle=gold(a); g.shadowColor=gold(.55); g.shadowBlur=7;

      let ang=Math.PI, rad=r;

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(x+Math.cos(ang)*rad, y+Math.sin(ang)*rad*dir);

      const steps=Math.floor(26*turns);

      for(let i=1;i<=steps;i++){

        ang+=turns*2*Math.PI/steps; rad*=0.94;

        g.lineWidth=Math.max(1,w*rad/r);

        g.lineTo(x+Math.cos(ang)*rad, y+Math.sin(ang)*rad*dir);

      }

      g.stroke(); g.shadowBlur=0;

    }

    /* a small offshoot growing from a stem point, tipped with a curl or leaf */

    function branch(x,y,ang,len,a,tip){

      g.strokeStyle=gold(a); g.shadowColor=gold(.4); g.shadowBlur=5;

      g.lineWidth=2.1;

      const ex=x+Math.cos(ang)*len,          ey=y+Math.sin(ang)*len;

      const mx=x+Math.cos(ang-0.55)*len*0.6, my=y+Math.sin(ang-0.55)*len*0.6;

      g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(x,y); g.quadraticCurveTo(mx,my,ex,ey); g.stroke();

      g.shadowBlur=0;

      if(tip==='curl') curl(ex,ey,len*0.42,1.35, ang<0? -1:1, a*.9, 2.6);

      else { leaf(ex,ey,len*0.62,ang,a*.85); leaf(ex-6,ey+4,len*0.44,ang+0.85,a*.6); }

    }

    /* one arm along +x: THREE strands weaving over and under each other,

       sprouting branches as they run toward the side title */

    function arm(){

      const strands=[

        {phase:0.00, amp:30, alpha:.85, w:5.2},

        {phase:0.33, amp:36, alpha:.62, w:3.8},

        {phase:0.66, amp:24, alpha:.48, w:2.9},

      ];

      const paths=strands.map(s=>{

        const pts=[];

        for(let i=0;i<=64;i++){

          const t=i/64, taper=1-0.55*t;

          const x=56+t*900;

          const y=64 + Math.sin((t*3.1+s.phase)*Math.PI*2)*s.amp*taper + 22*Math.sin(t*Math.PI);

          pts.push([x,y,taper]);

        }

        for(let i=1;i<pts.length;i++){

          g.strokeStyle=gold(s.alpha); g.shadowColor=gold(.5); g.shadowBlur=6;

          g.lineWidth=Math.max(1.1, s.w*pts[i][2]);

          g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(pts[i-1][0],pts[i-1][1]); g.lineTo(pts[i][0],pts[i][1]); g.stroke();

        }

        g.shadowBlur=0;

        return pts;

      });

      /* branches alternate strand, side, and tip along the run, shrinking */

      const spots=[ [0,10,-1,'leaf'], [1,18, 1,'curl'], [2,26,-1,'leaf'],

                    [0,34, 1,'curl'], [1,42,-1,'leaf'], [2,50, 1,'curl'], [0,57,-1,'leaf'] ];

      spots.forEach(([si,pi,side,tip],k)=>{

        const [x,y]=paths[si][pi];

        const len=48-k*4.5;

        branch(x,y, side*(0.95+0.12*(k%3)), len, .7-0.05*k, tip);

      });

      /* terminal flourish where the arm meets the title's neighborhood */

      const [tx,ty]=paths[0][62];

      curl(tx,ty,24,1.5,1,.6,3);

      wisp(430,60,24,.42); wisp(700,84,18,.36);

    }

    arm();

    g.save(); g.transform(0,1,1,0,0,0); arm(); g.restore();   // mirror across the diagonal

    /* the corner root: a bloom where the six strands meet */

    curl(84,84,58,1.8,1,.9,6);

    wisp(84,84,54,.5);

    const tex=new THREE.CanvasTexture(c); tex.minFilter=THREE.LinearFilter;

    return tex;

  }

  {

    const tex=cornerOrnamentTexture();

    const size=4.35, off=7.58-size/2;

    [[-off,-off,0],[off,-off,-Math.PI/2],[off,off,Math.PI],[-off,off,Math.PI/2]].forEach(([x,z,rz])=>{

      const m=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.PlaneGeometry(size,size),

        new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({map:tex, transparent:true, depthWrite:false,

          blending:THREE.AdditiveBlending, opacity:.85}));

      m.rotation.set(-Math.PI/2,0,rz);

      m.position.set(x,.018,z);

      m.renderOrder=1;

      scene.add(m);

    });

  }

  function boardSide(text, sub, icons, tips, x, z, rotZ){

    const c=document.createElement('canvas'); c.width=1400; c.height=176;

    const g=c.getContext('2d');

    g.textAlign='center'; g.textBaseline='middle';

    g.fillStyle='#d8b45a'; g.shadowColor='rgba(0,0,0,.6)'; g.shadowBlur=6;

    g.font='700 54px Cinzel, Georgia, serif';

    g.fillText(text,700,58);

    g.shadowBlur=0;

    g.font='700 27px Cinzel, Georgia, serif';

    g.fillStyle='rgba(216,180,90,.82)';

    g.fillText(sub.split('').join('\u2009'),700,126);

    const nL=Math.ceil(icons.length/2);

    const slots=[]; // canvas x for each icon, in icons order

    icons.slice(0,nL).forEach((k,i)=>{ const cx=700-380-i*170; slots.push(cx);

      g.save(); g.translate(cx,88); g.scale(2,2); g.translate(-cx,-88); drawIcon(g,k,cx,88); g.restore(); });

    icons.slice(nL).forEach((k,i)=>{ const cx=700+380+i*170; slots.push(cx);

      g.save(); g.translate(cx,88); g.scale(2,2); g.translate(-cx,-88); drawIcon(g,k,cx,88); g.restore(); });

    const tex=new THREE.CanvasTexture(c); tex.minFilter=THREE.LinearFilter;

    const m=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.PlaneGeometry(7.5,.94),

      new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({map:tex,transparent:true,depthWrite:false}));

    m.rotation.set(-Math.PI/2,0,rotZ); m.position.set(x,.02,z);

    scene.add(m);

    // invisible hover targets over each icon

    const holder=new THREE.Object3D();

    holder.rotation.set(-Math.PI/2,0,rotZ); holder.position.set(x,.03,z);

    scene.add(holder);

    slots.forEach((cx,i)=>{

      const hit=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CircleGeometry(.42,12),

        new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({transparent:true,opacity:0,depthWrite:false,side:THREE.DoubleSide}));

      hit.position.set((cx-700)*7.5/1400, 0, 0.001);

      hit.userData.tip=tips[i];

      holder.add(hit); iconHitList.push(hit);

    });

  }

  boardSide('FAERIE FORT',  'WISP ACTIONS',     ['move','flip'],

    ['Lure a Wisp into a different Court.',

     'Snuff two Wisps, from any Courts.'],

    0, -7.18, Math.PI);

  boardSide('FAERIE RING',  'RADIANCE ACTIONS', ['swap','eye'],

    ['Swap your Radiance card with a rival\u2019s; you\u2019ll know what you receive.',

     'Look at your own Radiance.'],

    7.18, 0, Math.PI/2);

  boardSide('FAERIE MOUND', 'COURT ACTIONS',    ['swap','eye'],

    ['Swap your Court card with a rival\u2019s; both of you see your new allegiance.',

     'Look at a rival\u2019s Court.'],

    -7.18, 0, -Math.PI/2);

 

  if(mode.tracks.includes('Faerie Bridge')){

    boardSide('FAERIE BRIDGE', 'MAGIK + STONE',    ['move','flip'],

      ['Gain a Faerie Magik card, then move a conjured stone to a dance\u2019s outer end; its Glamours ride along.',

       'Gain a Faerie Magik card, then flip a stone. Anyone on it tumbles from the dance.'],

      0, 7.18, 0);

  }

 

  // court quadrants (corners) with faint emblems

  function courtTexture(id, hex){

    const c=document.createElement('canvas'); c.width=c.height=256;

    const x=c.getContext('2d');

    const base='#'+hex.toString(16).padStart(6,'0');

    x.fillStyle=base; x.fillRect(0,0,256,256);

    x.lineJoin=x.lineCap='round';

    const ink=a=>`rgba(244,236,255,${a})`;

    const S=(d,w,a)=>{ x.strokeStyle=ink(a); x.lineWidth=w; x.stroke(new Path2D(d)); };

    // wheat-head awns (used by meadow): seven fine strokes fanning from the head

    const awns=(hx,hy)=>`M${hx} ${hy} L${hx-14} ${hy-14} M${hx+2} ${hy-12} L${hx-10.8} ${hy-24.8} M${hx+3.6} ${hy-23.2} L${hx-8.4} ${hy-36} `+

      `M${hx} ${hy} L${hx+14.4} ${hy-12} M${hx+2} ${hy-12} L${hx+15.6} ${hy-23.2} M${hx+3.6} ${hy-23.2} L${hx+16} ${hy-33.6} M${hx+4.8} ${hy-34.4} L${hx+6} ${hy-49.6}`;

    if(id==='mountain'){

      S('M36 200 L76 120 L116 200', 6, .12);     // left flanker, taller of the two

      S('M148 200 L188 132 L228 200', 5.5, .10); // right flanker, a touch shorter

      S('M72 200 L132 56 L192 200', 7, .20);     // the great centre peak, drawn in front

      S('M132 56 C128 96 138 128 130 164 C127 180 134 190 130 200', 4.5, .12);

    }

    if(id==='meadow'){

      S('M68 216 C64 188 60 160 70 128 M128 216 C132 184 126 156 132 120 M184 216 C188 192 194 164 182 136', 7, .20);

      S('M68 192 C48 182 38 166 36 148 M132 184 C150 174 160 158 162 140 M184 196 C166 186 158 170 156 152', 5.5, .11);

      S(awns(70,128)+' '+awns(132,120)+' '+awns(182,136), 5.5, .19);

    }

    if(id==='forest'){

      S('M128 40 L96 96 L112 96 L80 148 L100 148 L72 200 L184 200 L156 148 L176 148 L144 96 L160 96 Z', 7, .20);

    }

    if(id==='river'){

      S('M36 60 C68 44 100 76 132 60 C164 44 192 68 220 56', 6.8, .20);

      S('M28 92 C60 76 92 108 124 92 C156 76 188 100 224 88', 6.8, .11);

      S('M48 124 C80 108 112 140 144 124 C172 112 196 128 212 120', 6.8, .20);

      S('M28 156 C60 140 92 172 124 156 C156 140 188 164 224 152', 6.8, .11);

      S('M44 188 C76 172 108 204 140 188 C168 176 192 192 208 184', 6.8, .20);

    }

    const tex=new THREE.CanvasTexture(c); tex.minFilter=THREE.LinearFilter;

    return tex;

  }

  const qpos={mountain:[-3.225,-3.225], meadow:[3.225,-3.225], forest:[-3.225,3.225], river:[3.225,3.225]};

  const quads={};

  HOUSES.forEach(h=>{

    const m=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(6.45,.1,6.45),

      new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({map:courtTexture(h.id,h.hex),roughness:.75}));

    m.position.set(qpos[h.id][0],.07,qpos[h.id][1]); m.receiveShadow=true;

    scene.add(m); quads[h.id]=m;

  });

 

  // the golden thread of each dance traces the full groove

  const threadMat=new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0xd8b45a,emissive:0x8a6a1f,emissiveIntensity:.6,transparent:true,opacity:.5});

  TRACKS.forEach(tr=>{

    const pts=[];

    for(let k=0;k<=48;k++){ const p=spiralPoint(tr,k/48); pts.push(new THREE.Vector3(p.x,.15,p.z)); }

    const thread=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.TubeGeometry(new THREE.CatmullRomCurve3(pts),64,.026,6,false), threadMat);

    scene.add(thread);

  });

  const tileGroup=new THREE.Group(); scene.add(tileGroup);

 

 

  // the standing stones at the board's centre

  const stones=new THREE.Group();

  const stoneMat=new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0x4a4458,roughness:.85});

  for(let i=0;i<7;i++){

    const a=i/7*Math.PI*2;

    const s=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(.16,.55+((i*37)%3)*.09,.11), stoneMat);

    s.position.set(Math.cos(a)*.58, .4, Math.sin(a)*.58);

    s.rotation.y=-a; s.castShadow=true; stones.add(s);

  }

  const goldRing=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.TorusGeometry(.58,.025,10,40),

    new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0xd8b45a,metalness:.8,roughness:.35}));

  goldRing.rotation.x=Math.PI/2; goldRing.position.y=.13; stones.add(goldRing);

  scene.add(stones);

  const orb=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.SphereGeometry(.18,16,16),

    new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0xfff4d0,emissive:0xf0cf7a,emissiveIntensity:1.6}));

  orb.position.y=.85; orb.castShadow=true; scene.add(orb);

  // Victory spikes: cones that erupt from the orb and sink back, randomly, when a Call resolves.

  const orbSpikes=[];

  {

    const spikeMat=new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0xfff4d0,emissive:0xf7dd92,emissiveIntensity:2.0});

    for(let i=0;i<12;i++){

      const dir=new THREE.Vector3(Math.random()*2-1, Math.random()*2-1, Math.random()*2-1).normalize();

      const g=new THREE.ConeGeometry(.045,.3,6); g.translate(0,.15,0); // base at origin, tip grows outward

      const cone=new THREE.Mesh(g, spikeMat);

      cone.quaternion.setFromUnitVectors(new THREE.Vector3(0,1,0), dir);

      cone.position.copy(dir.clone().multiplyScalar(.155));

      cone.scale.set(1,.001,1);

      orb.add(cone);

      orbSpikes.push({m:cone, phase:Math.random()*Math.PI*2, speed:2.2+Math.random()*2.6});

    }

  }

  const mound=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(.72,.85,.22,24),

    new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0x2f4a2a,roughness:.9}));

  mound.position.y=.11; mound.castShadow=true; scene.add(mound);

 

  // dynamic groups

  const pawnGroup=new THREE.Group(); scene.add(pawnGroup);

  const nobleGroup=new THREE.Group(); scene.add(nobleGroup);

 

  // input

  let drag=null, pawnDrag=null;

  let tapSel=null;   // click/tap a dancer to select it, then click/tap a lit stone to place

  SELECT_DANCER=(ci)=>{        // called by the hand's dancer chips

    if(!(MOVE && MOVE.active) || MOVE.owner.i!==MY_SEAT) return;

    if(MOVE.lockCi!=null && MOVE.lockCi!==ci) return;

    tapSel=ci;

    highlightReach(MOVE.owner, ci, MOVE.points);

    document.querySelectorAll('#mydancers .dancerchip').forEach(el=>

      el.classList.toggle('sel', +el.dataset.ci===ci));

  };

  const ray=new THREE.Raycaster(), ndc=new THREE.Vector2(), v3=new THREE.Vector3();

  const dragPlane=new THREE.Plane(new THREE.Vector3(0,1,0), -0.14);

  function setRay(e){

    const r=renderer.domElement.getBoundingClientRect();

    ndc.x=((e.clientX-r.left)/r.width)*2-1; ndc.y=-((e.clientY-r.top)/r.height)*2+1;

    ray.setFromCamera(ndc,camera);

  }

  renderer.domElement.addEventListener('pointerdown',e=>{

    if(PICK){

      setRay(e);

      let hitSomething = false;

      if(PICK.mode === 'stone'){

        const hits = ray.intersectObjects(SCENE.tiles, false);

        if(hits.length && PICK.filter(hits[0].object.userData)){

          PICK.resolve({tr: hits[0].object.userData.track, k: hits[0].object.userData.step});

          hitSomething = true;

        }

      } else if(PICK.mode === 'dest'){

        const hits = ray.intersectObjects(SCENE.ghosts, false);

        if(hits.length){

          PICK.resolve({tr: hits[0].object.userData.track, end: hits[0].object.userData.end});

          hitSomething = true;

        }

      }

      if(hitSomething) return; // Prevent drag parsing if interacting with stones

    }

    if(!(MOVE && MOVE.active)) tapSel=null;   // a selection never outlives its move

    if(MOVE && MOVE.active){

      setRay(e);

      // A dancer is selected: a click or tap on a lit stone places it.

      if(tapSel!=null && (MOVE.lockCi==null || MOVE.lockCi===tapSel)){

        const reach=reachTilesFor(MOVE.owner, tapSel, MOVE.points);

        const hits=ray.intersectObjects(reach, false);

        if(hits.length){

          const r=MOVE.resolve; const ci=tapSel; tapSel=null;

          clearTileHighlights();

          r({ci, track:hits[0].object.userData.track, step:hits[0].object.userData.step});

          return;

        }

      }

      const mine=SCENE.pawnList.filter(g=>g.userData.pi===MOVE.owner.i &&

        (MOVE.lockCi==null || g.userData.ci===MOVE.lockCi));

      const hits=ray.intersectObjects(mine,true);

      if(hits.length){

        let g=hits[0].object; while(g.parent && g.userData.pi===undefined) g=g.parent;

        pawnDrag={g, ci:g.userData.ci, sx:e.clientX, sy:e.clientY, moved:false, touch:e.pointerType==='touch'};

        highlightReach(MOVE.owner, g.userData.ci, MOVE.points);

        return;

      }

      // a click on empty ground drops the selection

      if(tapSel!=null){ tapSel=null; clearTileHighlights();

        document.querySelectorAll('#mydancers .dancerchip.sel').forEach(el=>el.classList.remove('sel')); }

    }

    drag={x:e.clientX,y:e.clientY};

  });

  addEventListener('pointermove',e=>{

    // Camera and pawn dragging should continue even if mouse briefly leaves canvas

    if(pawnDrag){

      if(Math.abs(e.clientX-pawnDrag.sx)>8 || Math.abs(e.clientY-pawnDrag.sy)>8) pawnDrag.moved=true;

      setRay(e);

      if(ray.ray.intersectPlane(dragPlane,v3)) pawnDrag.g.position.set(v3.x,.55,v3.z);

      return;

    }

    if(drag){

      cam.theta-=(e.clientX-drag.x)*.006;

      cam.phi=Math.min(1.35,Math.max(.35,cam.phi-(e.clientY-drag.y)*.004));

      drag={x:e.clientX,y:e.clientY}; placeCam();

      return;

    }

    // 3D Hover effects (ONLY trigger if the mouse is directly over the 3D board, not UI)

    if(e.target !== renderer.domElement) {

        document.body.style.cursor = 'default';

        const tipEl=$('#tip3d');

        if(!tipEl.dataset.hud) tipEl.style.display = 'none';   // don't kill HUD-owned tooltips

        if(PICK && PICK.mode === 'stone') {

            SCENE.tiles.forEach(t => {

                if(PICK.filter(t.userData) && t.userData.hovered){

                   t.material.emissive.setHex(0xaaaa55);

                   t.material.emissiveIntensity = 0.6;

                   t.userData.hovered = false;

                }

            });

        } else if (PICK && PICK.mode === 'dest') {

            SCENE.ghosts.forEach(g => {

               if(g.userData.hovered){

                   g.material.emissive.setHex(0xddaa22);

                   g.material.emissiveIntensity = 0.6;

                   g.userData.hovered = false;

               }

            });

        }

        return;

    }

    if(PICK){

      setRay(e);

      if(PICK.mode === 'stone'){

        SCENE.tiles.forEach(t => {

           if(PICK.filter(t.userData)){

               t.material.emissive.setHex(t.userData.hovered ? 0xffffbb : 0xaaaa55);

               t.material.emissiveIntensity = t.userData.hovered ? 0.9 : 0.6;

               t.userData.hovered = false;

           }

        });

        const hits = ray.intersectObjects(SCENE.tiles, false);

        if(hits.length && PICK.filter(hits[0].object.userData)){

            hits[0].object.userData.hovered = true;

            hits[0].object.material.emissive.setHex(0xffffbb);

            hits[0].object.material.emissiveIntensity = 0.9;

            document.body.style.cursor = 'pointer';

        } else {

            document.body.style.cursor = 'default';

        }

      } else if(PICK.mode === 'dest'){

        SCENE.ghosts.forEach(g => {

           g.material.emissive.setHex(g.userData.hovered ? 0xffffff : 0xddaa22);

           g.material.emissiveIntensity = g.userData.hovered ? 1.0 : 0.6;

           g.userData.hovered = false;

        });

        const hits = ray.intersectObjects(SCENE.ghosts, false);

        if(hits.length){

            hits[0].object.userData.hovered = true;

            hits[0].object.material.emissive.setHex(0xffffff);

            hits[0].object.material.emissiveIntensity = 1.0;

            document.body.style.cursor = 'pointer';

        } else {

            document.body.style.cursor = 'default';

        }

      }

    } else if(SCENE && SCENE.iconHits.length){

      setRay(e);

      const tip=$('#tip3d');

      // Dancers first: hovering one names its owner.

      const ph=ray.intersectObjects(SCENE.pawnList, true);

      if(ph.length){

        let g=ph[0].object; while(g.parent && g.userData.pi===undefined) g=g.parent;

        const owner=G && G.players[g.userData.pi];

        if(owner){

          tip.textContent = owner.i===MY_SEAT ? 'Your Glamour' : `${owner.name}\u2019s Glamour`;

          tip.style.display='block';

          tip.style.left=(e.clientX+14)+'px';

          tip.style.top=(e.clientY+12)+'px';

          document.body.style.cursor='pointer';

          return;

        }

      }

      document.body.style.cursor='default';

      const hh=ray.intersectObjects(SCENE.iconHits);

      if(hh.length){

        tip.textContent=hh[0].object.userData.tip;

        tip.style.display='block';

        tip.style.left=(e.clientX+14)+'px';

        tip.style.top=(e.clientY+12)+'px';

      } else tip.style.display='none';

    }

  });

  addEventListener('pointerup',()=>{

    if(pawnDrag){

      // A plain click or tap (no drag) on a dancer SELECTS it: its reachable

      // stones stay lit, and the next click on one of them moves there.

      if(!pawnDrag.moved){

        tapSel=pawnDrag.ci;

        syncBoard();                                        // snap the pawn home…

        if(MOVE && MOVE.active)

          highlightReach(MOVE.owner, tapSel, MOVE.points);  // …then relight the stones

        pawnDrag=null;

        return;

      }

      tapSel=null;

      const reach=MOVE? reachTilesFor(MOVE.owner, pawnDrag.ci, MOVE.points) : [];

      let best=null, bd=1e9;

      reach.forEach(t=>{ const d=t.position.distanceTo(pawnDrag.g.position); if(d<bd){bd=d; best=t;} });

      clearTileHighlights();

      if(best && bd<0.95 && MOVE){

        const r=MOVE.resolve;

        r({ci:pawnDrag.ci, track:best.userData.track, step:best.userData.step});

      } else syncBoard(); // snap back

      pawnDrag=null;

      return;

    }

    drag=null;

  });

  renderer.domElement.addEventListener('wheel',e=>{

    cam.r=Math.min(30,Math.max(9,cam.r+e.deltaY*.01)); placeCam();

  },{passive:true});

  addEventListener('resize',()=>{

    camera.aspect=innerWidth/innerHeight; camera.updateProjectionMatrix();

    renderer.setSize(innerWidth,innerHeight);

  });

 

  const reduced=matchMedia('(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)').matches;

  let t0=0, calling=false;

  function loop(t){

    requestAnimationFrame(loop);

    const dt=(t-t0)/1000; t0=t;

    glade.update(t, dt, reduced);

    if(!reduced){

      stones.rotation.y += (calling? 1.6 : 0.12)*dt;

      orb.rotation.y += 1.2*dt;

      orb.position.y = calling

        ? Math.min(3.4, orb.position.y+1.5*dt)

        : .85+Math.sin(t*.0012)*.06;

      crownGlow.intensity = calling? 3.2 : .9+Math.sin(t*.0016)*.2;

      // spikes of new-won power: each erupts and sinks on its own rhythm

      orbSpikes.forEach(s=>{

        const target = calling ? Math.max(.001, Math.sin(t*.001*s.speed + s.phase)) : .001;

        s.m.scale.y += (target - s.m.scale.y)*.18;

      });

    }

    renderer.render(scene,camera);

  }

  requestAnimationFrame(loop);

 

  SCENE={scene,pawnGroup,nobleGroup,quads,tileGroup,tiles:[],ghosts:[],pawnList:[],iconHits:iconHitList, callCrown:()=>{calling=true;}};

}

 

/* rebuild pawns + nobles from state */

function nameTagMat(name){

  // One cached sprite material per player name, canvas sized to the text so

  // "You" and "Bramblewyn" both render crisp at the same letter height.

  SCENE.nameTags=SCENE.nameTags||{};

  if(SCENE.nameTags[name]) return SCENE.nameTags[name];

  const label=(String(name||'').slice(0,14) || '?').toUpperCase();

  const tc=document.createElement('canvas');

  const meas=tc.getContext('2d');

  meas.font='700 30px Cinzel, Georgia, serif';

  const w=Math.min(300, Math.max(64, Math.ceil(meas.measureText(label).width)+28));

  tc.width=w; tc.height=48;

  const tx=tc.getContext('2d');            // resizing reset the context — set font again

  tx.font='700 30px Cinzel, Georgia, serif';

  tx.textAlign='center'; tx.textBaseline='middle';

  tx.lineWidth=6; tx.strokeStyle='rgba(10,6,18,.9)'; tx.strokeText(label, w/2, 24);

  tx.fillStyle='#f0d98a'; tx.fillText(label, w/2, 24);

  const mat=new THREE.SpriteMaterial({map:new THREE.CanvasTexture(tc), transparent:true, depthWrite:false});

  mat._w=w;

  SCENE.nameTags[name]=mat;

  return mat;

}

function syncBoard(){

  const {pawnGroup,nobleGroup}=SCENE;

  if(!SCENE.glowMat){

    const c=document.createElement('canvas'); c.width=c.height=64;

    const x=c.getContext('2d');

    const gr=x.createRadialGradient(32,32,2,32,32,30);

    gr.addColorStop(0,'rgba(255,244,208,.95)'); gr.addColorStop(.4,'rgba(240,207,122,.55)'); gr.addColorStop(1,'rgba(201,154,58,0)');

    x.fillStyle=gr; x.fillRect(0,0,64,64);

    SCENE.glowMat=new THREE.SpriteMaterial({map:new THREE.CanvasTexture(c), blending:THREE.AdditiveBlending, depthWrite:false, transparent:true});

  }

  while(pawnGroup.children.length) pawnGroup.remove(pawnGroup.children[0]);

  while(nobleGroup.children.length) nobleGroup.remove(nobleGroup.children[0]);

 

  // stepping stones

  const TG=SCENE.tileGroup;

  while(TG.children.length) TG.remove(TG.children[0]);

  SCENE.tiles=[];

  TRACKS.forEach(tr=>{

    const L=trackLen(tr);

    G.steps[tr].forEach((st,idx)=>{

      const step=idx+1;

      const mat = st.c

        ? new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0x6fb8d0,roughness:.3,emissive:0x4fc0e0,emissiveIntensity:.95,transparent:true,opacity:.82})

        : new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0x2a2144,roughness:.8});

      const m=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(.52,.56,.09,24), mat);

      const p=tilePos(tr,step); m.position.set(p.x,.14,p.z);

      m.receiveShadow=true; m.castShadow=true;

      m.userData={track:tr, step, baseEmissive:mat.emissive.getHex()};

      TG.add(m); SCENE.tiles.push(m);

      if(st.c){

        if(!SCENE.conjGlowMat){

          const cc=document.createElement('canvas'); cc.width=cc.height=64;

          const cx=cc.getContext('2d');

          const cg=cx.createRadialGradient(32,32,2,32,32,30);

          cg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(210,248,255,.9)'); cg.addColorStop(.45,'rgba(110,215,235,.45)'); cg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(60,170,200,0)');

          cx.fillStyle=cg; cx.fillRect(0,0,64,64);

          SCENE.conjGlowMat=new THREE.SpriteMaterial({map:new THREE.CanvasTexture(cc), blending:THREE.AdditiveBlending, depthWrite:false, transparent:true});

        }

        const halo=new THREE.Sprite(SCENE.conjGlowMat); halo.scale.set(1.5,1.5,1);

        halo.position.set(p.x,.28,p.z);

        TG.add(halo);

      }

    });

  });

 

  // dancers

  SCENE.pawnList=[];

  G.players.forEach((p,pi)=>{

    p.cands.forEach((c,ci)=>{

      const col=new THREE.Color(p.color);

      const mat=new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:col,roughness:.45});

      const wingMat=new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({

        color:col.clone().lerp(new THREE.Color(0xffffff),.6),

        transparent:true, opacity:.55, side:THREE.DoubleSide, roughness:.3});

      const g=new THREE.Group();

      g.userData={pi:p.i, ci};

      const body=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.ConeGeometry(.12,.36,10),mat); body.position.y=.18;

      const head=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.SphereGeometry(.085,10,10),mat); head.position.y=.42;

      const wingGeo=new THREE.CircleGeometry(.13,12);

      const w1=new THREE.Mesh(wingGeo,wingMat); w1.scale.set(.6,1.55,1);

      w1.position.set(-.1,.3,-.07); w1.rotation.set(.3,.55,.55);

      const w2=new THREE.Mesh(wingGeo,wingMat); w2.scale.set(.6,1.55,1);

      w2.position.set(.1,.3,-.07); w2.rotation.set(.3,-.55,-.55);

      const spark=new THREE.Sprite(SCENE.glowMat); spark.scale.set(.32,.32,1); spark.position.y=.46;

      g.add(body,head,w1,w2,spark);

      if(p.isHuman){

        const mat=nameTagMat(p.name);

        const tag=new THREE.Sprite(mat);

        tag.scale.set(Math.min(1.4, .6*(mat._w/128)), .22, 1);

        tag.position.y=.84;

        g.add(tag);

      }

      if(p.i===MY_SEAT){

        const ring=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.TorusGeometry(.21,.024,8,24),

          new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({color:new THREE.Color(p.color)}));

        ring.rotation.x=Math.PI/2; ring.position.y=.02;

        g.add(ring);

      }

      g.traverse(o=>{ if(o.isMesh) o.castShadow=true; });

      let x,z;

      if(c.track){

        const tp=tilePos(c.track, Math.min(c.steps,trackLen(c.track)));

        const a=(pi/G.players.length)*Math.PI*2 + ci*Math.PI;

        x=tp.x+Math.cos(a)*.29; z=tp.z+Math.sin(a)*.29;

      } else return;   // off-board dancers live beside the hand, not on the board

      g.position.set(x, .19, z);

      pawnGroup.add(g);

      SCENE.pawnList.push(g);

    });

  });

 

  // Wisps

  const qpos={mountain:[-4.6,-4.6], meadow:[4.6,-4.6], forest:[-4.6,4.6], river:[4.6,4.6]};

  const wispMat=new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0xfff4d0,emissive:0xf0cf7a,emissiveIntensity:1.5});

  HOUSES.forEach(h=>{

    const n=G.nobles[h.id];

    for(let i=0;i<n;i++){

      const grp=new THREE.Group();

      const w=new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.SphereGeometry(.13,10,10), wispMat);

      const glow=new THREE.Sprite(SCENE.glowMat); glow.scale.set(.9,.9,1);

      grp.add(w,glow);

      const col=i%5, row=Math.floor(i/5);

      const sz=Math.sign(qpos[h.id][1]);

      grp.position.set(qpos[h.id][0]+(col-2)*.5, .34+((i*29)%3)*.05, qpos[h.id][1]+sz*(0.7+row*.55));

      nobleGroup.add(grp);

    }

  });

}

 

/* ============================================================

   HUD rendering

   ============================================================ */

/* ============================================================

   SEAT LAYER — which seat is THIS client, and how the engine asks

   any human seat for a decision. In solo play MY_SEAT is 0 and every

   wrapper resolves locally; in multiplayer (Stages 2-3) the wrappers

   become the RPC boundary for remote seats. The engine below never

   assumes the human is seat 0 — it asks the seat layer.

   ============================================================ */

let MY_SEAT=0;

let SELECT_DANCER=null;   // bound inside init3D; lets the hand's dancer chips select

const mySeatP=()=>G.players[MY_SEAT];

/* FORCE_WIRE — a loopback shakedown for the RPC boundary. When on, the LOCAL

   human's own decisions travel the same road a remote seat's would: the prompt

   payload is serialized, answered by the guest-side handler, the reply is

   serialized back, and the host-side validators run on it — with no network

   involved. Anything non-serializable, index-broken, or validator-rejected

   surfaces as a red line in The Telling instead of a cross-machine mystery.

   Turn on with ?wire=1 or #wire=1 in the URL, or setForceWire(true) in the

   console. Never active on a guest (its decisions already cross a real wire). */

let FORCE_WIRE=false;

try{ FORCE_WIRE=/[?#&]wire=1\b/.test(location.search+location.hash); }catch(e){}

window.setForceWire=v=>{ FORCE_WIRE=!!v;

  try{ log(`FORCE_WIRE is now <b>${FORCE_WIRE?'ON':'OFF'}</b>.`, 'sys'); }catch(e){}

  return FORCE_WIRE; };

/* The transfer function for a seat whose decisions cross the wire (real or

   simulated), or null for the plain local path. */

function seatWired(p){

  if(typeof seatRemote!=='undefined' && seatRemote(p)) return (kind,payload)=>rpcTo(p.i,kind,payload);

  if(FORCE_WIRE && p.isHuman && p.i===MY_SEAT && NET.role!=='guest') return (kind,payload)=>loopRPC(p.i,kind,payload);

  return null;

}

async function loopRPC(seat, kind, payload){

  const snag=m=>{ try{ netCrumb('FORCE_WIRE: '+m); }catch(e){}

                  try{ log('\u26a0 FORCE_WIRE: '+m, 'alert'); }catch(e){} };

  // 1. the pre-prompt state sync a real rpcTo performs (catches snapG faults)

  try{ JSON.stringify(snapG(seat)); }

  catch(e){ snag('snapG('+seat+') failed to serialize \u2014 '+((e&&e.message)||e)); }

  // 2. the request must survive the wire out

  let req;

  try{ req=JSON.parse(JSON.stringify({id:-1, kind, payload})); }

  catch(e){ snag('request payload not serializable ('+kind+') \u2014 '+((e&&e.message)||e)); return null; }

  // 3. answer with the SAME guest-side handler a remote seat runs;

  // 4. the reply must survive the wire back

  return new Promise(res=>{

    guestRPCCore(req, v=>{

      try{ res(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(v===undefined? null : v))); }

      catch(e){ snag('reply not serializable ('+kind+') \u2014 '+((e&&e.message)||e)); res(null); }

    });

  });

}

async function seatChoose(p, title, desc, opts, cls){

  if(seatClockExpired(p)) return null;   // this seat's governing clock has run out

  const R=reactBegin(p);

  try{

    const wired=seatWired(p);

    if(!wired) return await choose(title, desc, opts, cls, R.ctl);

    // wire: ship label/sub/cls; the answer is an index mapped back to the live value

    const wire=opts.map(o=>({label:o.label, sub:o.sub, cls:o.cls}));

    const idx=await wired('choose', {title, desc, opts:wire, cls});

    return (idx==null || !opts[idx]) ? (opts.find(o=>o.value===null)? null : opts[0].value) : opts[idx].value;

  } finally { R.end(); }

}

async function seatPickStone(p, msg, filter){

  if(seatClockExpired(p)) return null;

  const R=reactBegin(p);

  try{

    const wired=seatWired(p);

    if(!wired) return await pickStoneAsync(msg, filter);

    const legal=[];

    TRACKS.forEach(tr=>G.steps[tr].forEach((st,i)=>{ if(filter({track:tr, step:i+1})) legal.push(tr+'|'+(i+1)); }));

    const r=await wired('pickStone', {msg, legal});

    // the reply must be one of the choices that were offered

    if(!r || typeof r!=='object' || !legal.includes(r.tr+'|'+r.k)) return null;

    return {tr:r.tr, k:r.k};

  } finally { R.end(); }

}

async function seatPickDest(p, fromTr){

  if(seatClockExpired(p)) return null;

  const R=reactBegin(p);

  try{

    const wired=seatWired(p);

    if(!wired) return await pickDestinationAsync(fromTr);

    const r=await wired('pickDest', {fromTr});

    if(!r || typeof r!=='object' || !TRACKS.includes(r.tr)) return null;

    return {tr:r.tr, end:'outer'};

  } finally { R.end(); }

}

async function seatNotice(p, title, html){

  if(seatClockExpired(p)) return;

  if(!p.isHuman) return;

  const R=reactBegin(p);

  try{

    const wired=seatWired(p);

    if(wired){ await wired('notice', {title, html}); return; }

    if(p.i===MY_SEAT) return await notice(title, html, 'Continue', R.ctl);

  } finally { R.end(); }

}

async function seatArm(p, kinds){

  if(seatClockExpired(p)) return {type:'end'};

  const R=reactBegin(p);

  try{

    const wired=seatWired(p);

    if(!wired) return await armHuman(kinds);

    const ev=await wired('arm', {kinds});

    return sanitizeArmEv(p, ev, kinds);

  } finally { R.end(); }

}

/* The host trusts no wire: a remote turn event must claim only what the seat

   actually holds and only what was armed. Anything else ends the turn. */

function sanitizeArmEv(p, ev, kinds){

  if(!ev || typeof ev!=='object') return {type:'end'};

  if(ev.type==='end') return {type:'end'};

  if(ev.type==='skip') return kinds.includes('skip') ? {type:'skip'} : {type:'end'};

  if(ev.type==='honor')

    return (kinds.includes('honor') && Number.isInteger(ev.v) && p.hand.includes(ev.v))

      ? {type:'honor', v:ev.v} : {type:'end'};

  if(ev.type==='intrigue')

    return (kinds.includes('intrigue') && typeof ev.name==='string' && INTRIGUE_DEFS[ev.name]

            && p.intrigues.includes(ev.name) && ev.name!=='Blight' && ev.name!=='Cold Iron')

      ? {type:'intrigue', name:ev.name} : {type:'end'};

  return {type:'end'};

}

/* The mover's per-step choice — local drag UI, or an RPC to the remote mover. */

async function seatMoveChoice(actor, owner, points, lockCi, opts){

  if(seatClockExpired(actor)) return 'stop';

  const R=reactBegin(actor);

  try{

    const wired=seatWired(actor);

    if(!wired) return await localMoveChoice(owner, points, lockCi, opts);

    const r=await wired('move', {ownerSeat:owner.i, points, lockCi, single:!!opts.single, guided:!!opts.noForfeit});

    if(r==null || r==='stop') return 'stop';

    return validRemoteMove(owner, r, points, lockCi) ? {ci:r.ci, track:r.track, step:r.step} : 'stop';

  } finally { R.end(); }

}

/* Logical mirror of reachTilesFor: a remote move must be a dancer the mover

   may move, on a reachable stone, within the steps remaining. */

function validRemoteMove(owner, r, points, lockCi){

  if(!r || typeof r!=='object') return false;

  if(!Number.isInteger(r.ci) || r.ci<0 || r.ci>=owner.cands.length) return false;

  if(lockCi!=null && r.ci!==lockCi) return false;

  if(!TRACKS.includes(r.track)) return false;

  if(!Number.isInteger(r.step) || r.step<1 || r.step>trackLen(r.track)) return false;

  const c=owner.cands[r.ci];

  if(c.track){

    if(r.track!==c.track) return false;                 // dancers dance outward on their spiral

    const cost=r.step-c.steps;

    return cost>=1 && cost<=points;

  }

  return r.step<=points;                                 // entering from the Glade

}

function localMoveChoice(owner, points, lockCi, opts){

  const hud=$('#movehud');

  const guided = !!(TUT.guide && TUT.guide.lock) || !!opts.noForfeit;

  $('#movemsg').innerHTML = `Dance: <b>${points}</b> step(s). Click, tap, or drag <b>${owner.i===MY_SEAT ? (opts.single?'ONE of your Glamours':'a Glamour') : (opts.single? 'ONE of '+owner.name+'\u2019s Glamours' : 'one of '+owner.name+'\u2019s Glamours')}</b>: its reachable stones light up. Send it to one.`;

  $('#forfeit').textContent = 'Forfeit rest';

  $('#forfeit').style.display = guided ? 'none' : '';

  hud.style.display='flex';

  const chipWake=(on)=>{

    document.querySelectorAll('#mydancers .dancerchip').forEach(el=>{

      el.classList.toggle('live', on && owner.i===MY_SEAT && (lockCi==null || +el.dataset.ci===lockCi));

      el.classList.toggle('lockedout', on && owner.i===MY_SEAT && lockCi!=null && +el.dataset.ci!==lockCi);

      if(!on) el.classList.remove('sel');

    });

  };

  chipWake(true);

  return new Promise(resolve=>{

    MOVE={active:true, owner, points, lockCi, resolve:v=>{ MOVE=null; hud.style.display='none'; chipWake(false); resolve(v); }};

    $('#forfeit').onclick=()=>{ if(MOVE){ MOVE=null; } clearTileHighlights(); hud.style.display='none'; chipWake(false); resolve('stop'); };

  });

}

let HUMAN=null; // {kinds:[...], res}

function armHuman(kinds){ return new Promise(res=>{ HUMAN={kinds,res}; renderHUD(); }); }

function humanEvent(ev){

  if(HUMAN && HUMAN.kinds.includes(ev.type)){ const r=HUMAN.res; HUMAN=null; renderHUD(); r(ev); }

}

/* Draw v stones (v = 1..6) resting along one canonical Archimedean spiral,

   mimicking the board: a golden thread curling outward from the centre, with

   stepping stones spaced evenly along it. Card v shows the first v stones of

   the same spiral, so the pattern visibly grows from card to card. */

const RUNE_SPIRAL=(()=>{

  const b=2.5, s=7, PH=0.8;

  const pts=[[0,0]], thetas=[0];

  let th=s/b;

  for(let k=1;k<6;k++){

    const r=b*th;

    pts.push([r*Math.cos(th+PH), r*Math.sin(th+PH)]);

    thetas.push(th);

    th+=s/r;

  }

  return {b, PH, pts, thetas};

})();

function runeStonesSVG(v){

  const {b,PH,pts,thetas}=RUNE_SPIRAL;

  const P=pts.slice(0,v);

  // centre this card's stones in the face (slight upward bias clears the numeral)

  const sr=3.4;

  let minX=1e9,maxX=-1e9,minY=1e9,maxY=-1e9;

  P.forEach(p=>{ minX=Math.min(minX,p[0]); maxX=Math.max(maxX,p[0]);

                 minY=Math.min(minY,p[1]); maxY=Math.max(maxY,p[1]); });

  const ox=20-(minX+maxX)/2, oy=25-(minY+maxY)/2;

  // the thread: the smooth spiral curve itself, from the centre out to stone v

  let thread='';

  if(v>1){

    const end=thetas[v-1], seg=[];

    for(let t=0;t<=1.0001;t+=1/28){

      const a=t*end, r=b*a;

      seg.push(`${(ox+r*Math.cos(a+PH)).toFixed(1)},${(oy+r*Math.sin(a+PH)).toFixed(1)}`);

    }

    thread=`<path d="M${seg.join(' L')}" fill="none" stroke="rgba(240,217,138,.30)" stroke-width="1.2" stroke-linecap="round"/>`;

  }

  const circles=P.map(p=>`<circle cx="${(ox+p[0]).toFixed(1)}" cy="${(oy+p[1]).toFixed(1)}" r="${sr}"/>`).join('');

  return `<svg class="stones" viewBox="0 0 40 56" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">${thread}${circles}</svg>`;

}

/* Shared HUD tooltip: uses the fixed #tip3d element (nothing can clip it).

   Sets an ownership flag so the 3D scene's pointermove doesn't hide it. */

function attachTip(el, getText){

  el.addEventListener('mouseenter', ()=>{

    const tip=$('#tip3d');

    tip.textContent=getText();

    tip.dataset.hud='1';

    tip.style.display='block';

    const r=el.getBoundingClientRect();

    tip.style.left=Math.max(8, Math.min(innerWidth-238, r.left+r.width/2-115))+'px';

    if(r.top < innerHeight/2){ tip.style.bottom=''; tip.style.top=(r.bottom+8)+'px'; }

    else { tip.style.top=''; tip.style.bottom=(innerHeight-r.top+8)+'px'; }

  });

  el.addEventListener('mouseleave', ()=>{

    const tip=$('#tip3d');

    delete tip.dataset.hud;

    tip.style.display='none'; tip.style.top=''; tip.style.bottom='';

  });

}

function renderHUD(){

  // A rebuild can destroy a hovered element before mouseleave fires — self-heal.

  { const tip=$('#tip3d');

    if(tip.dataset.hud){ delete tip.dataset.hud; tip.style.display='none'; tip.style.top=''; tip.style.bottom=''; } }

  const me=G.players[MY_SEAT];

  const magikOn = !!(G.mode && G.mode.magik);

  // dancers not yet on a dance wait beside the hand

  const roost=$('#mydancers'); roost.innerHTML='';

  if(!me.cands.some(c=>!c.track))

    roost.innerHTML='<span style="font-size:11px; color:var(--ink2); font-style:italic; align-self:center;">in the dance</span>';

  me.cands.forEach((c,ci)=>{

    if(c.track) return;

    const chip=document.createElement('div');

    chip.className='dancerchip';

    chip.dataset.ci=ci;

    chip.style.background=me.color;

    chip.textContent='\u2727';

    chip.title='A Glamour waiting to enter the dance. Click it, then a lit stone.';

    chip.onpointerdown=()=>{ if(SELECT_DANCER) SELECT_DANCER(ci); };

    roost.appendChild(chip);

  });

  const R=$('#rivals'); R.innerHTML='';

  G.players.filter(p=>p.i!==MY_SEAT).forEach(p=>{

    const houseMini = `<div class="mini back hcard" title="Courts stay hidden: remember what you glimpse, or consult The Telling">C</div>`;

    const d=document.createElement('div');

    d.className='stand panel'+(G.players[G.turn]===p && !G.over?' active':'');

    const away = (G.away && G.away.includes(p.i)) ||

                 (NET.role==='host' && NET.inGame && NET.names[p.i]!=null && !connForSeat(p.i));

    if(away) d.style.opacity=.55;

    const awayMark = away? ' <span style="font-size:8px; letter-spacing:.08em; color:var(--danger); vertical-align:1px;">AWAY</span>' : '';

    const nMagik = (p.intrigueCount!=null) ? p.intrigueCount : p.intrigues.length;

    const magikMeta = magikOn ? `<span data-magiktip style="cursor:help">Magik <b>${nMagik}</b></span>` : '';

    d.innerHTML=`

      <div class="nm"><span class="dot" style="background:${p.color}"></span>${p.name}${awayMark}</div>

      <div class="cardrow">

        <div class="mini status" title="${p.name}'s Radiance: visible to you, not to them"><span class="lbl">RADIANCE</span>${p.status}</div>

        ${houseMini}

      </div>

      <div class="meta"><span data-runetip style="cursor:help; text-decoration:underline dotted rgba(201,182,224,.5); text-underline-offset:3px;">Runes <b>${p.hand.length}</b></span>${magikMeta}${

        p.cands.some(c=>!c.track)

          ? `<span title="Glamours waiting to enter the dance" style="color:${p.color}">${p.cands.filter(c=>!c.track).map(()=>'\u2727').join('')}</span>` : ''}</div>`;

    const runeStr = p.hand.length? p.hand.slice().sort((a,b)=>a-b).join(', ') : 'none';

    attachTip(d.querySelector('[data-runetip]'), ()=>`Runes left to dance: ${runeStr}`);

    if(magikOn) attachTip(d.querySelector('[data-magiktip]'), ()=>'Faerie Magik cards are held in secret.');

    R.appendChild(d);

  });

  $('#intrcol').style.display = magikOn ? '' : 'none';

  const mh=$('#myhouse'); const H=HOUSE_BY_ID[me.house];

  mh.className='bigcard house cbg cbg-'+H.id;

  mh.style.backgroundColor=H.css;

  mh.style.backgroundSize='82%'; mh.style.backgroundPosition='center';

  mh.innerHTML='';

  mh.title=H.name+': your allegiance';

  const ms=$('#mystatus');

  ms.className='bigcard back'; ms.textContent='?';

  ms.title = me.knownStatus!==null

    ? 'Your Radiance faces away again; you glimpsed it once, so remember it.'

    : 'Your Radiance faces away from you. Rivals can see it; you cannot.';

  const hd=$('#hand'); hd.innerHTML='';

  for(let v=1; v<=6; v++){

    const inHand=me.hand.includes(v);

    const c=document.createElement('button');

    const canPlay = inHand && HUMAN && HUMAN.kinds.includes('honor') && (!TUT.forceRune || v===TUT.forceRune);

    c.className='honor'+(inHand?'':' spent')+(canPlay?'':' disabled');

    c.dataset.v=v;   // addressable per rune (the tutorial spotlights pairs)

    c.innerHTML = runeStonesSVG(v) + `<span class="numeral">${v}</span>`;

    // Rune gifts (Midsummer only): 1 flips, 2 moves, 3/4/5 offer an OR-choice, 6 is clean.

    const powers = G.mode && G.mode.runePowers;

    if(powers){

      if(v===1) c.innerHTML+=`<span class="lure" data-tip="Flip a stone, then move 1."><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><circle cx="7" cy="7" r="4.5" fill="none"/><path d="M9 9 l4 4 M11 13 l2 0 l0 -2"/></svg></span>`;

      if(v===2) c.innerHTML+=`<span class="lure" data-tip="Move a Conjured Stone, then move 2."><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><ellipse cx="8" cy="11.5" rx="5.2" ry="2.4"/><path d="M3 6 h4 M8 4 l3 2 l-3 2"/></svg></span>`;
