      if(v===3) c.innerHTML+=`<span class="lure" data-tip="Instead: Discard Court, draw new Court."><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path d="M4 3 h8 v10 h-8 z" fill="none"/><path d="M6 6.5 h4 M6 9 h4 M13 4 a4 4 0 0 1 0 8" fill="none"/></svg></span>`;

      if(v===4) c.innerHTML+=`<span class="lure magik" data-tip="Instead: Discard Radiance, draw new Radiance."><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><circle cx="8" cy="8" r="3" fill="none"/><path d="M8 2 v1.5 M8 12.5 v1.5 M2 8 h1.5 M12.5 8 h1.5 M4 4 l1 1 M11 11 l1 1 M12 4 l-1 1 M5 11 l-1 1"/></svg></span>`;

      if(v===6) c.innerHTML+=`<span class="lure" data-tip="Instead: Lure a Wisp into a different Court."><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><circle cx="4.5" cy="11" r="2.6"/><path d="M7 8 Q10 3 14 5 M14 5 l-3 .4 M14 5 l-.8 2.6"/></svg></span>`;

      if(v===5) c.innerHTML+=`<span class="lure" data-tip="Instead: Force a rival to discard Court or Radiance, draw new."><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path d="M4 3 h6 v9 h-6 z" fill="none"/><path d="M13 5 l-2.2 2.2 M13 5 l-2.2 -0.2 M13 5 l0.2 2.2 M5.8 6 h2.4 M5.8 8.4 h2.4"/></svg></span>`;

    }

    c.title = !powers ? `${v} dance steps`

            : v===1 ? 'Flip a stone, then move 1'

            : v===2 ? 'Move a Conjured Stone, then move 2'

            : v===3 ? 'Instead: Discard Court, draw new Court'

            : v===4 ? 'Instead: Discard Radiance, draw new Radiance'

            : v===6 ? 'Instead: Lure a Wisp'

            : v===5 ? 'Instead: Force a rival to discard Court or Radiance, draw new'

            : `${v} dance steps`;

    if(canPlay) c.onclick=()=>humanEvent({type:'honor', v});

    hd.appendChild(c);

  }

  const it=$('#intrigues'); it.innerHTML='';

  /* FAERIE MAGIK HAND — the fixed-footprint pill box.

     Invariant: the hand occupies a 118x40px cell (one tile wide, the height of

     the Court/Radiance cards) and NEVER grows; more cards mean smaller pills.

       - 1 card   -> one full-width pill (118px)

       - 2+ cards -> two columns of half-width pills (57px), first half left

       - pill height: rows share the 40px (3px gaps), capped at 22px

       - font: scales with pill height (52%), 9px max, 4.5px min,

               and capped at 7px in two-column mode so the longest

               abbreviated name fits a 57px pill

     Long names abbreviate in two-column mode (ABBR below); hover tooltips

     always carry the full name and rules text. The eyebrow shows a live

     count from 3 cards up. */

  const nI=me.intrigues.length;

  const cols = nI<=1 ? 1 : 2;

  const rows = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(nI/cols));

  const pillH = Math.min(22, (40 - 3*(rows-1)) / rows);

  let pillF = Math.max(4.5, Math.min(9, pillH*0.52));

  if(cols===2) pillF = Math.min(pillF, 7);

  let colEls=[it];

  if(cols===2){

    colEls=[document.createElement('div'), document.createElement('div')];

    colEls.forEach(c=>{ c.className='icol'; it.appendChild(c); });

  }

  const ABBR = {'Whispered Lore':'Whisp. Lore','Midsummer Reel':'Mids. Reel','Bountiful Harvest':'B. Harvest'};

  const eyeb = document.querySelector('#intrcol .eyebrow');

  if(eyeb) eyeb.textContent = 'Faerie Magik' + (nI>2 ? ' \u00d7'+nI : '');

  me.intrigues.forEach((name,idx)=>{

    const b=document.createElement('button');

    const canPlay = HUMAN && HUMAN.kinds.includes('intrigue') && name!=='Blight' && name!=='Cold Iron';

    const canInterrupt = !canPlay && ANYTIME.includes(name) && G && !G.over && !TUT.guide && !TUT.tourActive;

    b.className='intr'; b.style.opacity=(canPlay||canInterrupt)?1:.55;

    b.style.width = cols===1 ? '118px' : '57px';

    b.style.height = pillH.toFixed(1)+'px';

    b.style.minHeight = '0';

    b.innerHTML=`<div class="t" style="font-size:${pillF.toFixed(1)}px">${cols===2 ? (ABBR[name]||name) : name}</div>`;

   

    let tipText = INTRIGUE_DEFS[name].d;

    if(!canPlay) {

        if(canInterrupt) tipText = '(Play anytime, even on rivals\u2019 turns) ' + tipText;

        else tipText = (name==='Blight'||name==='Cold Iron' ? '(Played in reaction) ' : '(Playable on your turn) ') + tipText;

    }

    // The scrollable card row clips CSS tooltips, so use the fixed floating tip instead.

    attachTip(b, ()=>tipText);

   

    if(canPlay) b.onclick=()=>humanEvent({type:'intrigue', name, idx});

    else if(canInterrupt) b.onclick=async ()=>{

      // Don't collide with a dialog already awaiting a decision.

      if($('#modalwrap').style.display==='flex' || INTERRUPT_BUSY || G.over) return;

      if(NET.role==='guest'){

        const go=await choose(`Play ${name} now?`,

          `<i>${INTRIGUE_DEFS[name].d}</i><br>This interrupts the current turn.`,

          [{label:'Play it now', cls:'warn', value:1},{label:'Keep it', value:null}]);

        if(go){ try{ NET.conns[0].send({type:'interrupt', name}); }catch(e){} }

        return;

      }

      INTERRUPT_BUSY=true;

      try{

        const go=await seatChoose(mySeatP(), `Play ${name} now?`,

          `<i>${INTRIGUE_DEFS[name].d}</i><br>This interrupts the current turn.`,

          [{label:'Play it now', cls:'warn', value:1},{label:'Keep it', value:null}]);

        if(go) await playActiveIntrigue(me, name);

      }catch(e){ if(!(e instanceof GameOver)) throw e; }

      finally{ INTERRUPT_BUSY=false; renderHUD(); }

    };

    colEls[cols===2 ? (idx<rows?0:1) : 0].appendChild(b);

  });

  const canSkip = HUMAN && HUMAN.kinds.includes('skip') && me.discard.length>0;

  $('#skipbtn').disabled=!canSkip;

  $('#endbtn').style.display = HUMAN && HUMAN.kinds.includes('end') ? '' : 'none';

}

$('#skipbtn').onclick=()=>humanEvent({type:'skip'});

$('#endbtn').onclick=()=>humanEvent({type:'end'});

/* The most recently opened or touched panel stacks above its siblings —

   and all open panels sit above the stands and dock (but below dialogs at 40). */

let PANEL_Z = 12;

function bringToFront(el){

  PANEL_Z = PANEL_Z >= 38 ? 13 : PANEL_Z + 1;   // stay below the choice modal (40)

  el.style.zIndex = PANEL_Z;

}

function setPanel(panelId, btnId, show, disp){

  const panel = $('#'+panelId);

  const btn = $('#'+btnId);

  if (show) {

    const rect = btn.getBoundingClientRect();

    panel.style.display = disp;

    btn.style.display = 'none';

    bringToFront(panel);

    // Panels on the left half of the screen align left edges; right half, right edges.

    const leftSide = (rect.left + rect.width/2) < window.innerWidth/2;

    let newTop = rect.top;

    let newLeft = leftSide ? rect.left : rect.right - panel.offsetWidth;

    if (newLeft < 10) newLeft = 10;

    if (newLeft + panel.offsetWidth > window.innerWidth - 10) {

        newLeft = window.innerWidth - panel.offsetWidth - 10;

    }

    if (newTop + panel.offsetHeight > window.innerHeight - 10) {

        newTop = window.innerHeight - panel.offsetHeight - 10;

    }

    panel.style.left = newLeft + 'px';

    panel.style.top = newTop + 'px';

    panel.style.right = 'auto';

    panel.style.bottom = 'auto';

  } else {

    const rect = panel.getBoundingClientRect();

    btn.style.display = 'block';

    panel.style.display = 'none';

    const leftSide = (rect.left + rect.width/2) < window.innerWidth/2;

    let newTop = rect.top;

    let newLeft = leftSide ? rect.left : rect.right - btn.offsetWidth;

    if (newLeft < 10) newLeft = 10;

    if (newLeft + btn.offsetWidth > window.innerWidth - 10) {

        newLeft = window.innerWidth - btn.offsetWidth - 10;

    }

    btn.style.left = newLeft + 'px';

    btn.style.top = newTop + 'px';

    btn.style.right = 'auto';

    btn.style.bottom = 'auto';

  }

}

$('#logmin').onclick=()=>setPanel('log','logtoggle',false,'flex');

$('#dockmin').onclick=()=>setPanel('dock','docktoggle',false,'flex');

$('#docktoggle').onclick=()=>setPanel('dock','docktoggle',true,'flex');

$('#logtoggle').onclick=()=>setPanel('log','logtoggle',true,'flex');

$('#legmin').onclick=()=>setPanel('legend','legtoggle',false,'block');

$('#legtoggle').onclick=()=>setPanel('legend','legtoggle',true,'block');

$('#rbmin').onclick=()=>setPanel('rulebook','rbtoggle',false,'flex');

$('#rbtoggle').onclick=()=>setPanel('rulebook','rbtoggle',true,'flex');

$('#magikmin').onclick=()=>setPanel('magikpanel','magiktoggle',false,'flex');

$('#magiktoggle').onclick=()=>setPanel('magikpanel','magiktoggle',true,'flex');

  .map(([name,v])=>`<h4>${name} <span class="cnt">×${v.n} in deck</span></h4><p>${v.d}</p>`).join('')

/* ============================================================

   Part C2: shared mechanics — movement, completion, nobles

   ============================================================ */

function stepsToComplete(c){ return c.track? trackLen(c.track)-c.steps : Math.min(...TRACKS.map(trackLen)); }

function minCompletion(p){ return Math.min(...p.cands.map(stepsToComplete)); }

/* ---- 3D Interaction Async Pickers ---- */

function pickStoneAsync(promptText, validFilter) {

  return new Promise(resolve => {

    const hud = $('#movehud');

    $('#movemsg').innerHTML = promptText;

    $('#forfeit').textContent = 'Cancel';

    hud.style.display = 'flex';

    clearTileHighlights();

    SCENE.tiles.forEach(t => {

      if (validFilter(t.userData)) {

        t.material.emissive.setHex(0xaaaa55);

        t.material.emissiveIntensity = 0.6;

      } else {

        t.material.emissive.setHex(0x000000);

        t.material.emissiveIntensity = 0;

      }

    });

    PICK = {

      mode: 'stone',

      filter: validFilter,

      resolve: (val) => {

        PICK = null;

        hud.style.display = 'none';

        document.body.style.cursor = 'default';

        syncBoard(); // cleanly wipes highlighting and restores correct emissives/halos

        resolve(val);

      }

    };

    $('#forfeit').onclick = () => { if(PICK) PICK.resolve(null); };

  });

}

function addGhost(tr, endType, slotIndex) {

  const mat = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({color:0xdddd44, transparent:true, opacity:0.5, emissive:0xddaa22, emissiveIntensity:0.6});

  const m = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(.52,.56,.2,24), mat);

  const p = slotPoint(tr, slotIndex);

  m.position.set(p.x, endType==='inner' ? .28 : .14, p.z);

  m.userData = { isGhost: true, track: tr, end: endType, hovered: false };

  SCENE.tileGroup.add(m);

  SCENE.ghosts.push(m);

}

function pickDestinationAsync(srcTr) {

  return new Promise(resolve => {

    const hud = $('#movehud');

    $('#movemsg').innerHTML = "Click a <b>highlighted spot</b> to place the stone";

    $('#forfeit').textContent = 'Cancel';

    hud.style.display = 'flex';

    SCENE.ghosts.forEach(g => SCENE.tileGroup.remove(g));

    SCENE.ghosts = [];

    TRACKS.forEach(tr => {

      const L = trackLen(tr);

      const isSrc = tr === srcTr;

      const futureL = L - (isSrc ? 1 : 0);

      if (futureL < SLOTS) {

        // Moves now only ever go to the OUTER end of a dance.

        if (futureL === 0) {

          addGhost(tr, 'outer', SLOTS); // empty track — the sole slot is the outer end

        } else {

          let outerSlot = SLOTS - L;

          if (isSrc) outerSlot++;

          if (outerSlot > 0) addGhost(tr, 'outer', outerSlot);

        }

      }

    });

    PICK = {

      mode: 'dest',

      resolve: (val) => {

        PICK = null;

        hud.style.display = 'none';

        document.body.style.cursor = 'default';

        SCENE.ghosts.forEach(g => SCENE.tileGroup.remove(g));

        SCENE.ghosts = [];

        syncBoard();

        resolve(val);

      }

    };

    $('#forfeit').onclick = () => { if(PICK) PICK.resolve(null); };

  });

}

 

/* ---- Conjured Stones & Tumbling ---- */

function conjuredList(){

  const out=[];

  TRACKS.forEach(tr=>G.steps[tr].forEach((st,idx)=>{ if(st.c) out.push({tr,k:idx+1}); }));

  return out;

}

function faeOnStep(tr,k){

  const out=[];

  G.players.forEach(q=>q.cands.forEach(c=>{ if(c.track===tr&&c.steps===k) out.push(q); }));

  return out;

}

function tumbleFae(tr, k) {

  const victims = [];

  G.players.forEach(q=>q.cands.forEach(c=>{

    if(c.track===tr && c.steps===k){ c.track=null; c.steps=0; victims.push(q); }

  }));

  return victims;

}

/* Ferry: relocate a conjured stone to the OUTER end of any dance, carrying its

   riders with it (no tumble). Used by the 2 rune and the Faerie Bridge favor.

   Riders land on the new outer stone (step 1) of the destination dance.

   Implemented in two clean phases so same-track and cross-track both behave. */

async function ferryConjured(actor, fromTr, k, toTr){

  // Phase 0: tag riders so we can set them aside during the index shuffling.

  let carried=0;

  G.players.forEach(q=>q.cands.forEach(c=>{

    if(c.track===fromTr && c.steps===k){ c._ferry=true; c.track=null; carried++; }

  }));

  // Phase 1: remove the stone from its origin; any NON-rider dancer standing

  // beyond the removed slot on fromTr shifts down one step.

  G.steps[fromTr].splice(k-1,1);

  G.players.forEach(q=>q.cands.forEach(c=>{

    if(!c._ferry && c.track===fromTr && c.steps>k) c.steps--;

  }));

  // Phase 2: add a conjured stone at the OUTER end (index 0) of toTr; every

  // NON-rider dancer already on toTr shifts inward by one.

  G.steps[toTr].unshift({c:true});

  G.players.forEach(q=>q.cands.forEach(c=>{

    if(!c._ferry && c.track===toTr) c.steps++;

  }));

  // Phase 3: land the riders on the new outer stone.

  G.players.forEach(q=>q.cands.forEach(c=>{

    if(c._ferry){ c.track=toTr; c.steps=1; delete c._ferry; }

  }));

  log(`${fmtP(actor)} moves a Conjured Stone to the outer end of the <b>${toTr}</b>${carried?', carrying its Glamour'+(carried>1?'s':'')+' along':''}.`);

  syncBoard(); renderHUD();

  // A moved stone can leave a dancer standing on what is NOW the final stone

  // (the track shrank beneath them, or the insertion pushed them inward).

  // Such a dance completes IMMEDIATELY, before anything else: the dancer's

  // owner unveils the Wisp and takes the favor (and may Call), whoever

  // caused the displacement.

  for(const q of G.players){

    for(const c of q.cands){

      if(c.track && c.steps>=trackLen(c.track)){

        log(`The stones shift: ${fmtP(q)}’s Glamour stands upon the final stone: the <b>${c.track}</b> completes!`, 'alert');

        await trackComplete(q, q, c);

      }

    }

  }

}

/* Redraw the actor's OWN Court card: discard current, draw a fresh one from the

   Court deck (reshuffling the discard when the deck runs dry), look at it, keep

   it secret. Others lose whatever they'd learned about the actor's Court. */

function redrawCourt(actor){

  G.houseDiscard.push(actor.house);

  actor.house = drawFrom(G.houseDeck, G.houseDiscard);

  // Every rival's knowledge of this player's Court is now stale.

  G.players.forEach(q=>{ if(q!==actor) delete q.knownHouses[actor.i]; });

  // Their old placement pattern no longer signals their (new) allegiance.

  if(G.placeEvidence) G.placeEvidence[actor.i]={mountain:0,meadow:0,forest:0,river:0};

}

/* Redraw the actor's OWN Radiance card, UNSEEN by the actor: discard current,

   draw a fresh one (reshuffle discard when dry). The actor does NOT learn it

   (knownStatus resets to null); rivals DO see the new number. */

function redrawStatus(actor){

  G.statusDiscard.push(actor.status);

  actor.status = drawFrom(G.statusDeck, G.statusDiscard);

  actor.knownStatus = null;   // fogged to the actor, even if previously peeked

}

/* AI ferry of a conjured stone (outer-end only, carries riders, no tumble).

   When `mandatory` is true (rune 2), it will move SOME stone if any conjured

   stone exists; otherwise it may decline unless a move looks worthwhile.

   Note: ferrying to the outer end sends riders back to a dance's start, so it's

   chiefly a repositioning/retreat tool — the AI uses it to relocate a stone away

   from a rival's path, or to shift its own stalled dancer onto a fresh dance. */

async function aiFerryConjured(p, mandatory){

  const conj=conjuredList();

  if(!conj.length) return;                 // nothing to move (rune 2 requirement waived)

  // Score candidate source stones. Ferrying carries riders to an outer end, i.e.

  // it RESETS whoever rides it to the start of the destination dance.

  let src=null, srcScore=-1e9;

  conj.forEach(({tr,k})=>{

    const on=faeOnStep(tr,k);

    const rivals=on.filter(q=>q!==p);

    const selfOn=on.includes(p);

    let s;

    if(rivals.length && !selfOn){

      // resetting a rival (esp. one near the end) back to a dance start is strong

      const nearEnd=trackLen(tr)-k<=2 ? 3 : 0;

      s=5+rivals.length*2+nearEnd+(rivals.some(q=>q.status>=7)?2:0);   // threat by VISIBLE Radiance

    } else if(selfOn){

      s=-6;                                // don't reset myself

    } else if(p.cands.some(c=>c.track===tr && c.steps<k)){

      s=0.4;                               // clearing a stone ahead of my own dancer: mild

    } else {

      s=0.2;

    }

    if(s>srcScore){ srcScore=s; src={tr,k,useful:rivals.length>0 && !selfOn}; }

  });

  if(!src) return;

  // Choose a destination dance whose OUTER end has room; prefer a dance where a

  // rival is NOT already sitting at the start (so we don't help them), and that

  // isn't one of our own near-complete lanes.

  const dests=TRACKS.filter(tr=>trackLen(tr) < SLOTS + (tr===src.tr?1:0));

  let dest=null;

  const clean=dests.filter(tr=>!p.cands.some(c=>c.track===tr && trackLen(tr)-c.steps<=2));

  const pool = clean.length ? clean : dests;

  if(!pool.length) return;

  // Soft destination strategy: lengthen the dance whose favor is aimed at ME.

  // Weighted leanings, never absolutes — the coin still turns in the air.

  const myCourtHot = G.nobles[p.house] >= quorum()-2;                    // my Court gathers light -> tax the Mound peeks/hops and Fort snuffs

  const myRadPrize = p.knownStatus!=null && p.knownStatus>=5;            // my (publicly visible) Radiance invites Ring muggings -> raise their price

  const wispTools=['Wisp-Call','Wisp-Lure','Snuff Out'];

  const myKitFull  = p.intrigues.includes('Cold Iron') && p.intrigues.some(nm=>wispTools.includes(nm));  // endgame kit in hand -> freezing the card faucet favors me

  const weight=tr=>{

    let w=1;

    if(myCourtHot && (tr==='Faerie Mound' || tr==='Faerie Fort')) w+=2;

    if(myRadPrize && tr==='Faerie Ring') w+=2;

    if(tr==='Faerie Bridge') w = myKitFull ? w+2 : w*0.6;                // default reluctance to grow the shared faucet

    return w;

  };

  let tot=0; const cum=pool.map(tr=>{ tot+=weight(tr); return tot; });

  const roll=Math.random()*tot;

  dest=pool[cum.findIndex(x=>roll<x)];

  if(!dest) return;

  // If not mandatory, only bother when it's actually useful.

  if(!mandatory && !(src.useful ? Math.random()<.8 : Math.random()<.25)) return;

  const ep=EPOCH;

  await wait(450);

  if(ep!==EPOCH || G.over) return;

  await ferryConjured(p, src.tr, src.k, dest);

}

 

/* ---- drag-and-drop movement ---- */

let MOVE=null;

function reachTilesFor(owner, ci, points){

  if(!SCENE.tiles) return [];

  // Single-dancer distribution (kept for future effects): only the locked dancer may move.

  if(MOVE && MOVE.lockCi!=null && ci!==MOVE.lockCi) return [];

  const c=owner.cands[ci];

  // Guided tutorial: only the single intended dancer + tile is a legal target.

  if(TUT.guide && TUT.guide.lock){

    const L=TUT.guide.lock;

    if(ci!==L.ci) return [];

    return SCENE.tiles.filter(t=>t.userData.track===L.track && t.userData.step===L.step);

  }

  return SCENE.tiles.filter(t=>{

    const {track,step}=t.userData;

    if(c.track) return track===c.track && step>c.steps && step-c.steps<=points;

    return step<=points;

  });

}

function clearTileHighlights(){

  if(!SCENE.tiles) return;

  SCENE.tiles.forEach(t=>{ t.material.emissive && t.material.emissive.setHex(t.userData.baseEmissive||0x000000); });

}

function highlightReach(owner, ci, points){

  clearTileHighlights();

  reachTilesFor(owner,ci,points).forEach(t=>{

    t.material.emissive.setHex(0xd9b454); t.material.emissiveIntensity=.55;

  });

}

 

async function allocateHuman(actor, owner, points, opts={}){

  let lockCi = null;                 // single-dancer mode: locks after the first move

  while(points>0 && !G.over){

    const res=await seatMoveChoice(actor, owner, points, lockCi, opts);

    if(res==='stop') break;

    const c=owner.cands[res.ci];

    const cost = c.track ? res.step-c.steps : res.step;

    c.track=res.track; c.steps=res.step;

    points-=cost;

    if(opts.single) lockCi=res.ci;   // all remaining steps stay with this dancer

    syncBoard();

    if(c.steps>=trackLen(c.track)){

      log(`${fmtP(owner)}\u2019s Glamour completes the <b>${c.track}</b>!`);

      await trackComplete(owner, actor, c);

    }

  }

  $('#movehud').style.display='none';

  $('#forfeit').style.display='';

}

 

async function allocate(actor, owner, points, opts={}){

  if(actor.isHuman) return allocateHuman(actor, owner, points, opts);

  const ep=EPOCH;

  let lockCi=null;                   // single-dancer mode for AI distribution too

  while(points>0 && !G.over && ep===EPOCH){

    let v;

    if(opts.single && lockCi!==null){

      const c0=owner.cands[lockCi];

      if(!c0.track) break;           // locked dancer finished (reset to Glade) — excess is lost

      v={ci:lockCi};

    } else {

      v=aiAllocChoice(owner, points);

    }

    await wait(700);

    if(ep!==EPOCH || G.over) return;

    if(v==='stop') return;

    const c=owner.cands[v.ci];

    if(v.start && trackLen(v.start)<1) return;             // belt: no entry into nothing

    if(v.start){ c.track=v.start; c.steps=1; }

    else c.steps++;

    if(opts.single) lockCi=v.ci;

    syncBoard();

    if(c.steps>=trackLen(c.track)){

      log(`${fmtP(owner)}\u2019s Glamour completes the <b>${c.track}</b>!`);

      await trackComplete(owner, actor, c);

    }

    points--;

  }

}

 

async function trackComplete(owner, actor, cand){

  const track=cand.track;

  cand.track=null; cand.steps=0; syncBoard();

  const plagued=await plagueWindow(actor);

  if(plagued){

    log(`The <b>Blight</b> withers the dance; no Wisp is unveiled.`, 'alert');

  } else {

    const h=await pickHouseForNoble(actor);

    await placeNoble(h, actor);

  }

  // In the Masquerade, every completed dance also grants a Faerie Magik card

  // (in the Midsummer Dance, Magik flows from the Faerie Bridge path instead).

  if(G.mode && G.mode.completionMagik){

    drawIntrigue(owner);

    log(`${fmtP(owner)} gains a <b>Faerie Magik</b> card for the completed dance.`);

  }

  if(actor===owner){ await kingdomAction(owner, track); }

  else log(`${fmtP(actor)} receives no favor (forced dance).`);

}

 

async function placeNoble(houseId, actor){

  if(!HOUSE_BY_ID[houseId]){   // expired/failed choice upstream: the Wisp is never placed

    log(`The moment passes; no Wisp is unveiled.`, 'sys');

    return;

  }

  G.nobles[houseId]++; syncBoard();

  if(G.placeEvidence) G.placeEvidence[actor.i][houseId]++;   // public act — everyone saw it

  log(`${fmtP(actor)} unveils a Will o\u2019 the Wisp in the ${fmtH(houseId)} (${G.nobles[houseId]}).`);

  if(G.nobles[houseId]>=coupAt()){

    if(G.mode && G.mode.reactionWindows){

      log(`<b>${coupAt()} WISPS!</b> The ${fmtH(houseId)} overflows: a True Name is called here at once, though rivals may still answer with Faerie Magik!`, 'alert');

    } else {

      log(`<b>${coupAt()} WISPS!</b> The ${fmtH(houseId)} can hold no more: a True Name is called here!`, 'alert');

    }

    await callForThrone(houseId, actor, true);

  } else if(!actor.isHuman){

    // EVERY human seat gets the window, in seat order (previously only the

    // host's local seat did). The Wisp count is rebuilt per seat: an earlier

    // human's response (a Snuff, a Lure) can change it mid-loop.

    for(const q of G.players){

      if(G.over) break;

      if(!q.isHuman || q===actor) continue;

      const txt=`${fmtP(actor)} unveils a Wisp in the ${fmtH(houseId)}: now <b>${G.nobles[houseId]}</b> Wisp${G.nobles[houseId]===1?'':'s'} there. (callable at ${quorum()}, forced at ${coupAt()}.)`;

      if(G.mode && G.mode.magik) await humanReactionPopup(q, 'A Wisp is unveiled', txt, 'noble');

      else await seatNotice(q, 'A Wisp is unveiled', txt);

    }

  }

}

 

async function pickHouseForNoble(actor){

  if(actor.isHuman){

    let houses=HOUSES;

    if(TUT.guide){ houses=HOUSES.filter(h=>h.id===TUT.guide.court); }

    const opts=houses.map(h=>{

      const n=G.nobles[h.id], warn=n+1>=coupAt();

      return {label:h.name, cls:'house'+h.id+(warn?' warn':''),

        sub:`${n} Wisp${n===1?'':'s'}`+(warn?': unveiling here FORCES the Call for a True Name!':(n+1>=quorum()?': enough to call a True Name':'')),

        value:h.id};

    });

    return await seatChoose(actor, 'Unveil a Wisp', TUT.guide? 'Place your Wisp in your Court, the Forest.' : 'Choose a Court for the new Will o\u2019 the Wisp.', opts);

  }

  return aiPickHouse(actor);

}

 

/* ============================================================

   Part C3: Kingdom Actions

   ============================================================ */

async function kingdomAction(p, track){

  if(p.isHuman) return humanKingdomAction(p, track);

  return aiKingdomAction(p, track);

}

 

async function humanKingdomAction(p, track){

  const anyNobles=HOUSES.some(h=>G.nobles[h.id]>0);

  const per={

    'Faerie Ring':[

      {label:'Swap your Radiance', sub:'Trade Radiance cards with a rival; you\u2019ll see what you receive.', value:'swapStatus'},

      {label:'Look at your own Radiance', sub:'Finally learn your worth.', value:'lookStatus'},

    ],

    'Faerie Fort':[

      anyNobles && {label:'Lure a Wisp', sub:'Lure a Wisp into a different Court.', value:'swapNoble'},

      anyNobles && {label:'Snuff two Wisps', sub:'Put out two Wisps, from any Courts.', value:'removeNoble'},

    ].filter(Boolean),

    'Faerie Mound':[

      {label:'Swap your Court', sub:'Trade Court cards. Both of you will see your new Court.', value:'swapHouse'},

      {label:'Look at a rival\u2019s Court', sub:'Learn which Court they belong to.', value:'lookHouse'},

    ],

    // Faerie Bridge is handled specially below (Magik card + move/flip).

    'Faerie Bridge':[]

  };

  // ---- Faerie Bridge: gain a Faerie Magik card, then EITHER move OR flip a stone ----

  if(track==='Faerie Bridge'){

    // The Call can still be made from a completed Faerie Bridge if the Court qualifies.

    const callHouses=housesAtQuorum();

    if(TUT.guide){

      const callOpt=callHouses.find(h=>h.id===TUT.guide.court);

      if(callOpt) return callForThrone(callOpt.id, p, false);

    }

    // Baseline: always draw a Magik card.

    drawIntrigue(p);

    log(`${fmtP(p)} completes the Faerie Bridge and gains a <b>Faerie Magik</b> card.`);

    // Offer a Call first if available (winning takes priority over a stone play).

    if(callHouses.length){

      const callOpts=callHouses.map(h=>({label:`✦ CALL FOR YOUR TRUE NAME: ${h.name}`, cls:'warn',

        sub:'All Fae reveal. The highest Radiance in this Court joins the High Fae.', value:{call:h.id}}));

      callOpts.push({label:'Not yet: take a stone action', value:'stone'});

      const cv=await seatChoose(p, 'Faerie Bridge: the Call?', 'Your Court holds enough Wisps. You may Call for your True Name now, or take your stone favor instead.', callOpts);

      if(cv && cv.call) return callForThrone(cv.call, p, false);

    }

    // Secondary: move or flip a stone (or skip).

    const conj=conjuredList();

    const sopts=[{label:'Flip a stone', sub:'Turn any stone conjured/regular; anyone on it tumbles.', value:'flip'}];

    if(conj.length) sopts.push({label:'Move a Conjured Stone', sub:'Carry a conjured stone (and its Glamours) to the outer end of any dance.', value:'move'});

    sopts.push({label:'Skip the stone action', sub:'Keep just the Magik card.', value:'skip'});

    const sv=await seatChoose(p, 'Faerie Bridge: Stone Favor', 'You gained a Faerie Magik card. Now move or flip a stone, if you like.', sopts);

    if(sv==='flip') await ACTIONS.flipStone(p);

    else if(sv==='move') await ACTIONS.moveStone(p);

    return;

  }

  const opts=[...per[track]];

  housesAtQuorum().forEach(h=>opts.push({label:`✦ CALL FOR YOUR TRUE NAME: ${h.name}`, cls:'warn',

    sub:'All Fae reveal. The highest Radiance in this Court joins the High Fae.', value:{call:h.id}}));

  opts.push({label:'Pass', sub:'Take no favor.', value:'pass'});

  if(TUT.guide){

    // Guided tutorial: the only path forward is to Call in the Forest.

    const callOpt=opts.find(o=>o.value && o.value.call===TUT.guide.court);

    const only=[callOpt || opts[0]];

    const v=await seatChoose(p, `${track}: High Fae Favor`, 'Your dance is complete! Completing a Dance normally lets you take a favor. But your Court now holds enough Wisps, so you can do the thing that wins the game: Call for your True Name.', only);

    if(v && v.call) return callForThrone(v.call, p, false);

    return;

  }

  const v=await seatChoose(p, `${track}: High Fae Favor`, 'Your dance is complete. The High Fae grant one favor.', opts);

  if(v==null || v==='pass') return;   // null: expired/failed choice — the favor lapses

  if(v.call) return callForThrone(v.call, p, false);

  await ACTIONS[v](p);

}

 

async function choosePlayer(actor, title, desc){

  const cands=others(actor);

  if(actor.isHuman){

    return await seatChoose(actor, title, desc, cands.map(q=>({

      label:q.name, sub:`Radiance ${q.status}`+(actor.knownHouses[q.i]?` · ${HOUSE_BY_ID[actor.knownHouses[q.i]].name}`:''), value:q })));

  }

  return null;

}

async function chooseHouseFrom(actor, title, desc, filter){

  const hs=HOUSES.filter(h=>!filter || filter(h));

  return await seatChoose(actor, title, desc, hs.map(h=>({label:h.name, cls:'house'+h.id,

    sub:`${G.nobles[h.id]} Wisp${G.nobles[h.id]===1?'':'s'}`, value:h.id})));

}

 

const ACTIONS={

  async swapStatus(p){

    const t=p.isHuman? await choosePlayer(p,'Swap Radiance','You will receive their visible Radiance; they receive yours.') : p._target;

    if(!t) return;   // expired/failed choice — the favor lapses

    const a=p.status, b=t.status;

    p.status=b; t.status=a; p.knownStatus=b; t.knownStatus=a;

    log(`${fmtP(p)} swaps Radiance with ${fmtP(t)}.`);

    logTo(p, `Your Radiance is now <b>${b}</b>.`, 'sys');

    logTo(t, `Your Radiance is now <b>${a}</b>.`, 'sys');

    await seatNotice(p, 'Radiance swapped', `You took ${t.name}\u2019s card: your Radiance is now <b>${b}</b> (and they now hold your old <b>${a}</b>).`);

    renderHUD();

  },

  async lookStatus(p){

    p.knownStatus=p.status;

    log(`${fmtP(p)} gazes upon their own Radiance.`);

    logTo(p, `You gaze upon your Radiance: it is <b>${p.status}</b>.`, 'sys');

    if(p.isHuman){

      await seatNotice(p, 'Your Radiance', `Your Radiance is <b>${p.status}</b>. The card turns away again; remember it, or consult The Telling.`);

    }

    renderHUD();

  },

  async swapNoble(p){

    let from,to;

    if(p.isHuman){

      from=await chooseHouseFrom(p,'Lure a Wisp: from','Draw a Wisp out of…', h=>G.nobles[h.id]>0);

      if(from==null) return;   // expired/failed choice — the favor lapses

      to=await chooseHouseFrom(p,'Lure a Wisp: into','…and let it settle in:', h=>h.id!==from);

      if(to==null) return;

    } else { from=p._from; to=p._to; }

    G.nobles[from]--; log(`${fmtP(p)} lures a Wisp away from the ${fmtH(from)}…`);

    await placeNoble(to,p);

  },

  async removeNoble(p){

    // The Fort favor snuffs TWO Wisps in total, each from ANY Court (the same

    // Court twice is legal). The Snuff Out card still takes only one.

    const first=p.isHuman? await chooseHouseFrom(p,'Snuff two Wisps (first)','Put out a Wisp of…', x=>G.nobles[x.id]>0) : p._from;

    if(first==null) return;

    G.nobles[first]--; syncBoard();

    log(`${fmtP(p)} snuffs out a Wisp of the ${fmtH(first)} (${G.nobles[first]}).`);

    if(!HOUSES.some(h=>G.nobles[h.id]>0)) return;   // nothing left burning anywhere

    let second=null;

    if(p.isHuman){

      second=await chooseHouseFrom(p,'Snuff two Wisps (second)','…and put out one more, of:', x=>G.nobles[x.id]>0);

    } else {

      // Second target re-scored after the first flame dies: armed and near-armed

      // Courts first, then the biggest visible threat.

      let bv=-1;

      HOUSES.forEach(h=>{

        if(h.id===p.house || G.nobles[h.id]<1) return;

        const n=G.nobles[h.id], t=rivalThreatIn(p,h.id);

        const v = (n>=quorum()-1 ? 10+t : t);

        if(v>bv){ bv=v; second=h.id; }

      });

    }

    if(second==null) return;

    G.nobles[second]--; syncBoard();

    log(`${fmtP(p)} snuffs out a second Wisp, of the ${fmtH(second)} (${G.nobles[second]}).`);

  },

  async swapHouse(p){

    const t=p.isHuman? await choosePlayer(p,'Swap Court','Trade Court cards. Both of you will see your new Court.') : p._target;

    if(!t) return;   // expired/failed choice — the favor lapses

    const a=p.house, b=t.house;

    p.house=b; t.house=a;

    p.knownHouses[t.i]=a; t.knownHouses[p.i]=b;

    logTo(p, `You now belong to the ${fmtH(b)}.`, 'sys');

    logTo(t, `You now belong to the ${fmtH(a)}.`, 'sys');

    G.players.forEach(q=>{ if(q!==p&&q!==t){ delete q.knownHouses[p.i]; delete q.knownHouses[t.i]; }});

    if(G.placeEvidence){

      G.placeEvidence[p.i]={mountain:0,meadow:0,forest:0,river:0};

      G.placeEvidence[t.i]={mountain:0,meadow:0,forest:0,river:0};

    }

    log(`${fmtP(p)} swaps Courts with ${fmtP(t)}.`);

    await seatNotice(p, 'Court swapped', `You now belong to the <b>${HOUSE_BY_ID[b].name}</b>. ${t.name} took your old card.`);

    renderHUD();

  },

  async lookHouse(p){

    const t=p.isHuman? await choosePlayer(p,'Look at a Court','Secretly learn which Court a rival belongs to.') : p._target;

    if(!t) return;   // expired/failed choice — the favor lapses

    p.knownHouses[t.i]=t.house;

    log(`${fmtP(p)} peeks at ${fmtP(t)}\u2019s Court card.`);

    logTo(p, `You peek: ${fmtP(t)} belongs to the ${fmtH(t.house)}.`, 'sys');

    if(p.isHuman){

      await seatNotice(p, 'Allegiance glimpsed', `${t.name} belongs to the <b>${HOUSE_BY_ID[t.house].name}</b>. The card turns facedown again; remember it, or consult The Telling.`);

    }

    renderHUD();

  },

  async flipStone(p){

    if(p.isHuman){

       const pick = await seatPickStone(p, 'Click any stone to flip it (Regular ↔ Conjured)', ud => true);

       if(!pick) return; // cancelled — no flip taken

       const st = G.steps[pick.tr][pick.k-1];

       st.c = !st.c;

       const v = tumbleFae(pick.tr, pick.k);

       log(`${fmtP(p)} flips step ${pick.k} of the <b>${pick.tr}</b> to ${st.c?'Conjured':'Regular'}.`);

       v.forEach(q=>log(`The stone flips, and ${fmtP(q)}\u2019s Glamour tumbles!`, 'alert'));

       syncBoard(); renderHUD();

    } else {

       const targets = [];

       TRACKS.forEach(tr=>G.steps[tr].forEach((st,idx)=>{

          const k=idx+1, on=faeOnStep(tr,k);

          if(on.length>0 && !on.includes(p)) targets.push({tr,k});

       }));

       let choice = targets.length ? pick(targets) : {tr:TRACKS[TRACKS.length-1], k:1};

       const st = G.steps[choice.tr][choice.k-1];

       st.c = !st.c;

       const v = tumbleFae(choice.tr, choice.k);

       log(`${fmtP(p)} flips step ${choice.k} of the <b>${choice.tr}</b> to ${st.c?'Conjured':'Regular'}.`);

       v.forEach(q=>log(`The stone flips, and ${fmtP(q)}\u2019s Glamour tumbles!`, 'alert'));

       syncBoard(); renderHUD();

    }

  },

  async moveStone(p){

    if(p.isHuman){

       const conj = conjuredList();

       if(!conj.length) { await seatNotice(p, 'Move Stone', 'No conjured stones to move!'); return; }

       

       while(true){

           const srcPick = await seatPickStone(p, "Click a <b>glowing Conjured Stone</b> to move", ud => G.steps[ud.track][ud.step-1].c);

           if(!srcPick) return;

           const destPick = await seatPickDest(p, srcPick.tr);

           if(!destPick) continue;

           await ferryConjured(p, srcPick.tr, srcPick.k, destPick.tr);

           break;

       }

    } else {

       await aiFerryConjured(p, false);

    }

  }

};

 

/* ============================================================

   Part D: Intrigues & reaction windows

   ============================================================ */

function takeIntrigue(p, name){

  const i=p.intrigues.indexOf(name);

  if(i>=0) p.intrigues.splice(i,1);

}

function drawIntrigue(p){

  // The Faerie Magik deck NEVER reshuffles. Spent cards rest in the discard,

  // reachable only by Whispered Lore — so the Magik economy is finite by design.

  if(!G.intrigueDeck.length){

    log(`The Faerie Magik deck is spent; no card remains to draw.`, 'sys');

    return;

  }

  p.intrigues.push(G.intrigueDeck.pop());

  renderHUD();

}

 

async function humanReactionPopup(seatP, title, desc, context){

  const me=seatP;

  if(seatClockExpired(me)) return null;   // this seat's clock has run out — windows pass

  if(!me.isHuman) return null;

  if(me.i!==MY_SEAT && !seatRemote(me)) return null;   // human, but unreachable from here

  while(!G.over){

    if(seatClockExpired(me)) return null;   // the response clock expired between prompts

    const opts=[];

    if(context==='call'){

      // At a Call, only Wisp manipulation and lore recall are possible — no Blight.

      ['Wisp-Lure','Snuff Out','Whispered Lore'].forEach(n=>{

        if(me.intrigues.includes(n)) opts.push({label:n, sub:INTRIGUE_DEFS[n].d, value:n});

      });

      if(!opts.length) return null;   // nothing playable — don't even show the popup

      opts.push({label:'Let the Call stand', sub:'Continue to the reveal.', value:null, cls:'passopt'});

      const v=await seatChoose(me, title, desc, opts, 'reaction');

      if(v===null) return null;

      await playActiveIntrigue(me, v);

      continue;

    }

    if(context==='intrigue' && me.intrigues.includes('Cold Iron'))

      opts.push({label:'Cold Iron', cls:'warn', sub:INTRIGUE_DEFS['Cold Iron'].d, value:'Cold Iron'});

    if(context==='completion' && me.intrigues.includes('Blight'))

      opts.push({label:'Blight', cls:'warn', sub:INTRIGUE_DEFS['Blight'].d, value:'Blight'});

    ['Scrying Pool','Wisp-Lure','Snuff Out','Wisp-Call'].forEach(n=>{

      if(me.intrigues.includes(n)) opts.push({label:n, sub:INTRIGUE_DEFS[n].d+' (anytime)', value:n});

    });

    opts.push({label:'No Magik to use', sub:'Continue play.', value:null, cls:'passopt'});

    const v=await seatChoose(me, title, desc, opts, 'reaction');

    if(v===null) return null;

    if(v==='Cold Iron' || v==='Blight') return v;

    await playActiveIntrigue(me, v);

  }

  return null;

}

 

async function breachWindow(p, name){

  if(!(G.mode && G.mode.reactionWindows)) return false;

  const order=[];

  for(let k=1;k<G.players.length;k++) order.push(G.players[(p.i+k)%G.players.length]);

  for(const q of order){

    // A player may answer REPEATEDLY in the same window: if their Cold Iron is

    // itself countered, they may spend another copy on the original card.

    let mayRespond=true;

    while(mayRespond && !G.over){

      mayRespond=false;

      let cancels=false;

      if(q.isHuman){

        const r=await humanReactionPopup(q, 'Faerie Magik!',

          `${fmtP(p)} plays <b>${name}</b>. <i>${INTRIGUE_DEFS[name].d}</i>`, 'intrigue');

        cancels = r==='Cold Iron';

        if(G.over) return false;

      } else if(q.intrigues.includes('Cold Iron')){

        if(name==='Cold Iron'){

          // Counter the counter (the original card would stand). Fight harder

          // for the chain when Calls are near: cold iron is for the endgame.

          cancels = Math.random() < (boardHeat(q)>0.5 ? .75 : .4);

        } else {

          // Counter only Magik that materially harms q, judged from q's own view.

          let harm=0;

          if(name==='Blight' && G.players[G.turn]===q) harm=0.8;             // my completion Wisp being blocked

          if((name==='Snuff Out'||name==='Wisp-Lure') && p._from===q.house && G.nobles[q.house]>=quorum()-1 && pWinCall(q,q.house)>=0.45)

            harm=0.85;                                                        // draining the Court that arms MY Call

          if(name==='Wisp-Call' && p.status>=7)                               // a strong rival arming some Call

            harm=Math.max(harm, HOUSES.some(h=>G.nobles[h.id]>=quorum()-1 && pWinCall(q,h.id)<0.3) ? 0.5 : 0.15);

          cancels = Math.random() < harm;

        }

      }

      if(cancels){

        takeIntrigue(q,'Cold Iron');

        log(`${fmtP(q)} plays <b>Cold Iron</b>: ${fmtP(p)}\u2019s ${name} is undone. The cold iron is spent, gone from the game.`, 'alert');

        renderHUD();

        // A Cold Iron is itself Faerie Magik — it can be countered by another Cold Iron.

        const countered = await breachWindow(q, 'Cold Iron');

        if(countered){

          log(`The counter is itself undone: ${fmtP(p)}\u2019s <b>${name}</b> stands!`, 'alert');

          renderHUD();

          // Same player may try again if they hold another Cold Iron.

          mayRespond = q.intrigues.includes('Cold Iron');

          continue;

        }

        if(name!=='Cold Iron') G.intrigueDiscard.push(name);   // spent Cold Irons never enter the discard

        renderHUD();

        return true;

      }

    }

    if(G.over) return false;

  }

  return false;

}

 

async function plagueWindow(actor){

  if(!(G.mode && G.mode.reactionWindows)) return false;

  for(const q of G.players){

    if(q===actor) continue;

    let plays=false;

    if(q.isHuman){

      const r=await humanReactionPopup(q, 'A dance is complete',

        `${fmtP(actor)} completed a dance and is about to unveil a Wisp.`, 'completion');

      plays = r==='Blight';

      if(G.over) return false;

    } else if(q.intrigues.includes('Blight')){

      // Judge from q's own view, legally: the completer's Radiance is public.

      // Blight matters most when the coming Wisp could arm a Call q loses.

      const strongActor = actor.status>=7;

      const armable = HOUSES.some(h=>{

        const n=G.nobles[h.id];

        if(n<quorum()-1) return false;

        // a Court one Wisp (or none) from callable — would q lose a Call there?

        return pWinCall(q,h.id) < 0.35;

      });

      const p_ = armable ? 0.7 : (strongActor ? 0.35 : 0.08);

      plays = Math.random() < p_;

    }

    if(plays){

      takeIntrigue(q,'Blight');

      log(`${fmtP(q)} plays <b>Blight</b>!`);

      const canceled=await breachWindow(q,'Blight');

      if(!canceled){ G.intrigueDiscard.push('Blight'); renderHUD(); return true; }

      renderHUD();

    }

  }

  return false;

}

 

async function playActiveIntrigue(p, name){

  if(!INTRIGUE_DEFS[name] || !p.intrigues.includes(name)) return 0;   // never resolve a card not truly held

  if((name==='Snuff Out'||name==='Wisp-Lure') && !HOUSES.some(h=>G.nobles[h.id]>0)){

    await seatNotice(p, name, 'There are no Wisps on the board; the Magik would fizzle. The card stays in your hand.');

    return 0;

  }

  takeIntrigue(p, name);

  log(`${fmtP(p)} plays <b>${name}</b>.`);

  renderHUD();

  const canceled=await breachWindow(p, name);

  if(canceled) return 0;

  let pts=0;

  switch(name){

    case 'Bountiful Harvest': pts=3; break;

    case 'Scrying Pool':

      p.knownStatus=p.status;

      logTo(p, `The scrying pool shows your Radiance: it is <b>${p.status}</b>.`, 'sys');

      await seatNotice(p, 'Scrying Pool', `The still water shows it: your Radiance is <b>${p.status}</b>. Remember it, or consult The Telling.`);

      break;

    case 'Whispered Lore': {

      const uniq=[...new Set(G.intrigueDiscard)];

      if(!uniq.length){ await seatNotice(p, 'Whispered Lore','The lore is silent; no Magik has been discarded yet.'); break; }

      let choiceN;

      if(p.isHuman) choiceN=await seatChoose(p, 'Whispered Lore','Take one Faerie Magik from the discards.', uniq.map(n=>({label:n, sub:INTRIGUE_DEFS[n].d, value:n})));

      else choiceN=['Wisp-Call','Midsummer Reel','Blight','Snuff Out','Bountiful Harvest','Wisp-Lure','Scrying Pool'].find(nm=>uniq.includes(nm)) || pick(uniq);

      G.intrigueDiscard.splice(G.intrigueDiscard.indexOf(choiceN),1);

      p.intrigues.push(choiceN);

      log(`${fmtP(p)} recalls <b>${choiceN}</b> from whispered lore.`);

      break;

    }

    case 'Wisp-Lure': {

      let from,to;

      if(p.isHuman){

        from=await chooseHouseFrom(p,'Wisp-Lure: from','Lure a Wisp out of…', h=>G.nobles[h.id]>0);

        to=await chooseHouseFrom(p,'Wisp-Lure: into','…and let it drift into:', h=>h.id!==from);

      } else { from=p._from; to=p._to; }

      if(from==null || to==null){   // expired/failed choice — the Magik fizzles into the discard

        G.intrigueDiscard.push(name); renderHUD();

        return 0;

      }

      G.nobles[from]--;

      log(`${fmtP(p)} sings a lure, and a Wisp drifts from the ${fmtH(from)}.`);

      G.intrigueDiscard.push(name); renderHUD();

      await placeNoble(to,p);

      return 0;

    }

    case 'Snuff Out': {

      const h=p.isHuman? await chooseHouseFrom(p,'Snuff Out','Put out a Wisp of…', x=>G.nobles[x.id]>0) : p._from;

      if(h==null) break;   // expired/failed choice — the Magik fizzles into the discard

      G.nobles[h]--; syncBoard();

      log(`${fmtP(p)} snuffs out a Wisp of the ${fmtH(h)} (${G.nobles[h]}).`);

      break;

    }

    case 'Wisp-Call': {

      const h=await pickHouseForNoble(p);

      G.intrigueDiscard.push(name); renderHUD();

      await placeNoble(h,p);

      return 0;

    }

  }

  G.intrigueDiscard.push(name);

  renderHUD();

  return pts;

}

 

/* ============================================================

   Part D2: Call for the Throne & reveal

   ============================================================ */

/* When a True Name is called, the dance pauses: rivals (not the caller) may

   lure or snuff Wisps, or recall lore — never Blight. If the Court drops below

   the needed Wisps, the Call fades and play continues. */

async function callWindow(caller, houseId, need){

  if(!(G.mode && G.mode.reactionWindows)) return;

  const order=[];

  for(let k=1;k<G.players.length;k++) order.push(G.players[(caller.i+k)%G.players.length]);

  for(const q of order){

    if(G.over) return;

    if(G.nobles[houseId] < need) return;   // already broken — no further responses needed

    if(q.isHuman){

      await humanReactionPopup(q, 'A True Name is Called!',

        `${fmtP(caller)} calls for a True Name in the ${fmtH(houseId)} (<b>${G.nobles[houseId]}</b> Wisps; the Call needs <b>${need}</b>). You may respond before the reveal.`, 'call');

    } else {

      // AI responds if it expects to LOSE this Call (its own win probability

      // in the called Court is low) and one Wisp suffices to break it.

      const losing = pWinCall(q, houseId) < 0.4;

      if(losing && G.nobles[houseId]===need){   // one Wisp is enough to break it

        if(q.intrigues.includes('Snuff Out') && Math.random()<.85){

          q._from=houseId;

          await playActiveIntrigue(q,'Snuff Out');

        } else if(q.intrigues.includes('Wisp-Lure') && Math.random()<.7){

          q._from=houseId;

          q._to = (q.house!==houseId && G.nobles[q.house]+1<coupAt() && !knownStrongerShares(q)) ? q.house

                  : pick(HOUSES.filter(h=>h.id!==houseId)).id;

          await playActiveIntrigue(q,'Wisp-Lure');

        }

      }

    }

  }

}

async function callForThrone(houseId, caller, isCoup){

  const need = isCoup ? coupAt() : quorum();

  banner('A TRUE NAME IS CALLED');

  log(`${isCoup?'The Court can hold no more: fate itself cries out for':fmtP(caller)+' cries out for'} a <b>True Name</b> in the ${fmtH(houseId)}!`, 'alert');

  // The pause: rivals may respond with Faerie Magik before the reveal.

  await callWindow(caller, houseId, need);

  if(G.over) throw new GameOver();   // a nested Call resolved during the window

  if(G.nobles[houseId] < need){

    log(`The ${fmtH(houseId)} no longer holds enough Wisps (<b>${G.nobles[houseId]}</b> of ${need}): <b>the Call fades away!</b>`, 'alert');

    banner('THE CALL FADES');

    syncBoard(); renderHUD();

    return;   // canceled — the dance goes on

  }

  if(isCoup && !G.players.some(p=>p.house===houseId)){

    G.nobles[houseId] = quorum()-1;

    log(`No Fae belongs to the ${fmtH(houseId)}: the Call finds no one, and <b>the gathered light scatters</b> (${quorum()-1} Wisps remain).`, 'alert');

    banner('THE CALL FADES');

    syncBoard(); renderHUD();

    return;   // the dance goes on

  }

  G.over=true;

  SCENE.callCrown();

  await wait(1800);

  const contenders=G.players.filter(p=>p.house===houseId);

  let winner=null;

  contenders.forEach(p=>{ if(!winner||p.status>winner.status) winner=p; });

  const trueName = winner ? bestowTrueName(houseId) : null;

  if(winner) log(`The High Fae whisper ${fmtP(winner)}\u2019s True Name: <b>${trueName}</b>.`, 'alert');

  const bestowal = winner

    ? `<div style="margin:2px 0 12px; font-family:var(--disp); letter-spacing:.06em;">\u2726 The High Fae whisper the True Name \u2726<br><b style="font-size:21px; color:var(--gold); display:inline-block; margin-top:4px;">${trueName}</b></div>`

    : '';

  $('#revsub').innerHTML = bestowal + `${isCoup?'The Court could hold no more: a True Name is forced':'A True Name is called'} in the <b style="color:${HOUSE_BY_ID[houseId].css}">${HOUSE_BY_ID[houseId].name}</b>. All Courts and Radiance are revealed.` +

    (winner? '' : '<br><b>No Fae belonged to this Court: no True Name is granted.</b>');

  const rows=$('#revrows'); rows.innerHTML='';

  [...G.players].sort((a,b)=>b.status-a.status).forEach(p=>{

    const h=HOUSE_BY_ID[p.house];

    const r=document.createElement('div');

    r.className='revrow'+(p===winner?' winner':'');

    r.innerHTML=`<span class="crownmark">${p===winner?'\u2726':''}</span>

      <span class="nm"><span class="dot" style="display:inline-block;width:9px;height:9px;border-radius:50%;background:${p.color};margin-right:6px"></span>${p.name}</span>

      <span class="chip cbg cbg-${p.house}" style="background-color:${h.css}; background-size:26px; background-position:right 6px center; padding-right:34px;">${h.name.toUpperCase()}</span>

      <span class="st">${p.status}</span>`;

    rows.appendChild(r);

  });

  $('#revtitle').textContent = winner ? (winner.isHuman? 'YOU JOIN THE HIGH FAE' : `${winner.name.toUpperCase()} JOINS THE HIGH FAE`) : 'NO TRUE NAME IS GRANTED';

  if(TUT.act3){

    // Teaching caption framed around the Court-sharer, per the tutorial's lesson.

    const sharers=G.players.filter(p=>p!==caller && p.house===houseId);

    const sharer=sharers.length? sharers.reduce((a,b)=>b.status>a.status?b:a) : null;

    const elsewhereHigh=[...G.players].reduce((a,b)=>b.status>a.status?b:a);

    let html = bestowal +

      `You called in the <b style="color:${HOUSE_BY_ID[houseId].css}">${HOUSE_BY_ID[houseId].name}</b> and <b>won with a Radiance of ${caller.status}</b>.`;

    if(sharer){

      html += `<br><br>You won because <b>${sharer.name} shared your Court but held only a ${sharer.status}</b>, lower than your ${caller.status}. Among the Fae in a called Court, the highest Radiance wins. Had ${sharer.name}\u2019s Radiance been higher than yours, <b>${sharer.name} would have won instead.</b>`;

    }

    html += `<br><br>One more thing: <b>${elsewhereHigh.name} held a ${elsewhereHigh.status}</b>, higher than yours, but belonged to another Court, so it didn\u2019t matter. <i>And remember: everyone else could see your ${caller.status}, but you Called without knowing it yourself. In a real game, use favors like <b>Look at your own Radiance</b> to learn your number, and watch your rivals\u2019, before you Call.</i>`;

    $('#revsub').innerHTML = html;

    const btn=$('#revbtn');

    btn.textContent='Continue → free practice';

    btn.onclick=()=>{

      $('#reveal').style.display='none';

      btn.textContent='Play Again'; btn.onclick=()=>location.reload();

      TUT.act3=false;

      if(TUT.act3Continue){ const r=TUT.act3Continue; TUT.act3Continue=null; r(); }

    };

    $('#reveal').style.display='flex';

    throw new GameOver();

  }

  $('#reveal').style.display='flex';

  if(NET.role==='host' && NET.inGame){

    clockStop();

    hostPersistClear();

    netAll({type:'reveal', sub:$('#revsub').innerHTML, rows:$('#revrows').innerHTML});

    const btn=$('#revbtn');

    btn.textContent='Play Again \u2014 Same Table';

    btn.onclick=()=>hostRematch();

  }

  throw new GameOver();

}

 

/* ============================================================

   Part D3: turns — human & AI

   ============================================================ */

async function humanTurn(p){

  banner(p.i===MY_SEAT ? 'Your turn' : `${p.name}’s turn`);

  while(true){

    const ev=await seatArm(p, ['honor','skip','intrigue']);

    if(ev.type==='end') return;   // force-released (e.g. tutorial Continue) — bail out entirely

    if(ev.type==='skip'){

      p.hand.push(...p.discard.splice(0)); p.hand.sort((a,b)=>a-b);

      log(`${fmtP(p)} sits out the dance and reclaims their discards.`);

      renderHUD(); return;

    }

    if(ev.type==='intrigue'){

      if(ev.name==='Midsummer Reel'){

        const amt=await seatChoose(p, 'Midsummer Reel','Dance in place of a Fae Rune. Choose your steps; the chosen rune\u2019s power applies (the 1 and 2 must perform their stone action first, just like the real runes).',

          [1,2,3,4,5,6].map(n=>({label:String(n), value:n})).concat([{label:'Never mind', value:null}]));

        if(amt===null) continue;

        // For 1/2, confirm the mandatory stone action is possible/committed BEFORE spending the Reel,

        // so the player can back out (as with the real runes). The 2's move is waived only if no

        // conjured stones exist.

        let reelFlip=null, reelFerry=null;

        if(amt===1){

          reelFlip = await seatPickStone(p,

            "Midsummer Reel as a <b>1</b>: you must <b>flip a stone</b> first: click any stone.", ()=>true);

          if(!reelFlip) continue;   // backed out — Reel stays in hand

        } else if(amt===2 && conjuredList().length){

          while(true){

            const srcPick=await seatPickStone(p,

              "Midsummer Reel as a <b>2</b>: you must <b>move a Conjured Stone</b> first: click a glowing conjured stone.",

              ud=>G.steps[ud.track][ud.step-1].c);

            if(!srcPick){ reelFerry='cancel'; break; }

            const destPick=await seatPickDest(p, srcPick.tr);

            if(!destPick) continue;

            reelFerry={src:srcPick, dest:destPick};

            break;

          }

          if(reelFerry==='cancel') continue;   // backed out — Reel stays in hand

        }

        takeIntrigue(p,'Midsummer Reel');

        log(`${fmtP(p)} plays <b>Midsummer Reel</b> in place of a Fae Rune (${amt}).`);

        renderHUD();

        const canceled=await breachWindow(p,'Midsummer Reel');

        if(!canceled) G.intrigueDiscard.push('Midsummer Reel');   // breachWindow already discards it when canceled

        if(!canceled){

          // The Reel dances as the chosen rune, with the SAME mandatory stone actions.

          if(amt===1 && reelFlip){

            const st=G.steps[reelFlip.tr][reelFlip.k-1]; st.c=!st.c;

            const vv=tumbleFae(reelFlip.tr,reelFlip.k);

            log(`${fmtP(p)} flips step ${reelFlip.k} of the <b>${reelFlip.tr}</b> to ${st.c?'Conjured':'Regular'}.`);

            vv.forEach(q=>log(`The stone flips, and ${fmtP(q)}\u2019s Glamour tumbles!`, 'alert')); syncBoard(); renderHUD();

          }

          if(amt===2 && reelFerry && reelFerry.src){

            await ferryConjured(p, reelFerry.src.tr, reelFerry.src.k, reelFerry.dest.tr);

          }

          if(amt===3){

            const c3=await seatChoose(p, 'The Reel\u2019s Gift (3)','Dance 3 steps, or spend the Reel to redraw your own Court.',

              [{label:'Dance 3 steps', value:'dance'},

               {label:'Redraw your Court', sub:'Discard your Court, draw a new one, look, keep it secret.', value:'redraw'}]);

            if(c3==='redraw'){

              redrawCourt(p);

              log(`${fmtP(p)} redraws their Court via the Reel.`, 'sys');

              await seatNotice(p, 'Your Court is redrawn', `You now belong to the <b>${HOUSE_BY_ID[p.house].name}</b>. Only you know this.`);

              renderHUD(); break;

            }

          }

          if(amt===4){

            const c4=await seatChoose(p, 'The Reel\u2019s Gift (4)','Dance 4 steps, or spend the Reel to blindly redraw your own Radiance.',

              [{label:'Dance 4 steps', value:'dance'},

               {label:'Redraw your Radiance', sub:'Draw a new number you cannot see; rivals can.', value:'redraw'}]);

            if(c4==='redraw'){

              redrawStatus(p);

              log(`${fmtP(p)} blindly redraws their Radiance via the Reel.`, 'sys');

              await seatNotice(p, 'Your Radiance is redrawn', `You draw a fresh Radiance <b>unseen</b>: rivals see the new number, you do not.`);

              renderHUD(); break;

            }

          }

          if(amt===5){

            const c5=await seatChoose(p, 'The Reel\u2019s Gift (5)','Dance 5 steps, or spend the Reel to force a rival to discard their Court or Radiance and draw anew.',

              [{label:'Dance 5 steps', value:'dance'},

               {label:'Force a redraw', sub:'A rival discards their Court or Radiance and draws a new one.', value:'force'}]);

            if(c5==='force'){

              const t=await choosePlayer(p,'Force a Redraw','Choose a rival; they will discard their Court or Radiance and draw a new one.');

              if(!t) break;   // expired/failed choice — the Reel is spent, the force fizzles

              const which=await seatChoose(p, 'Court or Radiance?', `${t.name} must discard and redraw…`,

                [{label:'Their Court', value:'court'},{label:'Their Radiance', value:'radiance'}]);

              if(which==null) break;

              if(which==='court'){

                redrawCourt(t);

                log(`${fmtP(p)} spends the Reel: ${fmtP(t)} is forced to discard their Court and draw anew.`, 'alert');

                await seatNotice(t, 'Your Court is torn away', `${p.name} forces you to redraw: you now belong to the <b>${HOUSE_BY_ID[t.house].name}</b>. Only you know this.`);

              } else {

                redrawStatus(t);

                log(`${fmtP(p)} spends the Reel: ${fmtP(t)} is forced to blindly redraw their Radiance.`, 'alert');

                await seatNotice(t, 'Your Radiance is torn away', `${p.name} forces you to redraw your Radiance <b>unseen</b>: everyone can see your new number but you.`);

              }

              renderHUD();

              break;

            }

          }

          if(amt===6 && HOUSES.some(h=>G.nobles[h.id]>0)){

            const c6=await seatChoose(p, 'The Reel\u2019s Gift (6)','Dance 6 steps, or spend the Reel to lure a Wisp between Courts.',

              [{label:'Dance 6 steps', value:'dance'},

               {label:'Lure a Wisp', sub:'Move one Wisp from any Court into another.', value:'lure'}]);

            if(c6==='lure'){

              const from=await chooseHouseFrom(p,'Lure: from','Draw a Wisp out of…', h=>G.nobles[h.id]>0);

              if(from==null) break;   // expired/failed choice — the Reel is spent, the lure fizzles

              const to=await chooseHouseFrom(p,'Lure: into','…and let it settle in:', h=>h.id!==from);

              if(to==null) break;

              G.nobles[from]--; syncBoard();

              log(`A Wisp drifts from the ${fmtH(from)}…`);

              await placeNoble(to,p);

              break;

            }

          }

          await allocate(p,p,amt);

        }

        break;

      }

      const pts=await playActiveIntrigue(p, ev.name);

      if(pts>0) await allocate(p,p,pts);

      continue;

    }

    if(ev.type==='honor'){

      const v=ev.v;

      const powers = G.mode && G.mode.runePowers;

      // ----- Runes 3/4/5 offer an OR-choice BEFORE the card is spent (so "keep" can back out) -----

      let orChoice=null;                 // 'dance' | 'redrawCourt' | 'redrawStatus' | 'lure'

      if(powers && v===3){

        const c=await seatChoose(p, 'The Third Rune',

          'Move 3, or instead discard your Court and draw a new one, seen only by you.',

          [{label:'Move 3', value:'dance'},

           {label:'Discard Court, draw new Court', sub:'Seen only by you.', value:'redrawCourt'},

           {label:'Keep the rune', sub:'Choose a different card instead.', value:null}]);

        if(c===null) continue;

        orChoice=c;

      } else if(powers && v===4){

        const c=await seatChoose(p, 'The Fourth Rune',

          'Move 4, or instead discard your Radiance and draw a new one. Rivals see the new number; you do not.',

          [{label:'Move 4', value:'dance'},

           {label:'Discard Radiance, draw new Radiance', sub:'A blind gamble: rivals see it, you don\u2019t.', value:'redrawStatus'},

           {label:'Keep the rune', sub:'Choose a different card instead.', value:null}]);

        if(c===null) continue;

        orChoice=c;

      } else if(powers && v===5){

        const c=await seatChoose(p, 'The Fifth Rune',

          'Move 5, or instead force a rival to discard their Court or their Radiance and draw a new one.',

          [{label:'Move 5', value:'dance'},

           {label:'Force a redraw', sub:'A rival of your choosing discards their Court or Radiance and draws anew.', value:'force'},

           {label:'Keep the rune', sub:'Choose a different card instead.', value:null}]);

        if(c===null) continue;

        orChoice=c;

      } else if(powers && v===6){

        const anyW=HOUSES.some(h=>G.nobles[h.id]>0);

        const c=await seatChoose(p, 'The Sixth Rune',

          'Move 6, or instead lure a Will o\u2019 the Wisp into a different Court.',

          [{label:'Move 6', value:'dance'}]

          .concat(anyW?[{label:'Lure a Wisp', sub:'Lure a Wisp into a different Court.', value:'lure'}]:[])

          .concat([{label:'Keep the rune', sub:'Choose a different card instead.', value:null}]));

        if(c===null) continue;

        orChoice=c;

      }

      // ----- Runes 1/2 do a mandatory stone action FIRST; confirm the source before spending -----

      let flipPick=null, ferry=null;

      if(powers && v===1){

        // Mandatory flip: must pick a stone (any stone is legal). Cancel = keep the rune.

        flipPick = await seatPickStone(p,

          "<b>Flip a stone, then move 1</b>: click any stone to flip it (anyone on it tumbles, including you).",

          () => true

        );

        if(!flipPick) continue;   // backed out — rune stays in hand

      } else if(powers && v===2){

        const conj=conjuredList();

        if(conj.length>0){

          // Mandatory move of a conjured stone (outer end, carries riders). Cancel = keep the rune.

          while(true){

            const srcPick = await seatPickStone(p,

              "<b>Move a Conjured Stone, then move 2</b>: click a glowing conjured stone (its Glamours ride along).",

              ud => G.steps[ud.track][ud.step-1].c

            );

            if(!srcPick){ ferry='cancel'; break; }

            const destPick = await seatPickDest(p, srcPick.tr);

            if(!destPick) continue;          // pick a different source

            ferry={src:srcPick, dest:destPick};

            break;

          }

          if(ferry==='cancel') continue;     // backed out — rune stays in hand

        }

        // If no conjured stones exist, the move requirement is waived — just dance 2.

      }

      // ----- Commit: spend the card -----

      p.hand.splice(p.hand.indexOf(v),1); p.discard.push(v);

      renderHUD();

      // ----- Resolve OR-effects that replace dancing -----

      if(orChoice==='redrawCourt'){

        redrawCourt(p);

        log(`${fmtP(p)} spends the <b>3</b> rune to redraw their Court.`, 'sys');

        await seatNotice(p, 'Your Court is redrawn', `You discard your old Court and draw a fresh one: you now belong to the <b>${HOUSE_BY_ID[p.house].name}</b>. Only you know this; the card turns facedown again.`);

        renderHUD();

        if(!p.hand.length){ p.hand.push(...p.discard.splice(0)); p.hand.sort((a,b)=>a-b);

          log(`${fmtP(p)} has danced their whole Fae Rune hand; all discards return.`, 'sys'); }

        break;

      }

      if(orChoice==='redrawStatus'){

        redrawStatus(p);

        log(`${fmtP(p)} spends the <b>4</b> rune to blindly redraw their Radiance.`, 'sys');

        await seatNotice(p, 'Your Radiance is redrawn', `You discard your old Radiance and draw a fresh one, <b>unseen</b>. Your rivals can see the new number, but you cannot. It may be higher; it may be lower.`);

        renderHUD();

        if(!p.hand.length){ p.hand.push(...p.discard.splice(0)); p.hand.sort((a,b)=>a-b);

          log(`${fmtP(p)} has danced their whole Fae Rune hand; all discards return.`, 'sys'); }

        break;

      }

      if(orChoice==='force'){

        const t=await choosePlayer(p,'Force a Redraw','Choose a rival; they will discard their Court or Radiance and draw a new one.');

        if(!t) break;   // expired/failed choice — the rune is spent, the force fizzles

        const which=await seatChoose(p, 'Court or Radiance?',

          `${t.name} must discard and redraw…`,

          [{label:'Their Court', sub:'They draw a new allegiance, seen only by them.', value:'court'},

           {label:'Their Radiance', sub:'They draw a new number, visible to all but them.', value:'radiance'}]);

        if(which==null) break;

        if(which==='court'){

          redrawCourt(t);

          log(`${fmtP(p)} spends the <b>5</b> rune: ${fmtP(t)} is forced to discard their Court and draw anew.`, 'alert');

          await seatNotice(t, 'Your Court is torn away', `${p.name} forces you to redraw: you now belong to the <b>${HOUSE_BY_ID[t.house].name}</b>. Only you know this.`);

        } else {

          redrawStatus(t);

          log(`${fmtP(p)} spends the <b>5</b> rune: ${fmtP(t)} is forced to blindly redraw their Radiance.`, 'alert');

          await seatNotice(t, 'Your Radiance is torn away', `${p.name} forces you to redraw your Radiance <b>unseen</b>: everyone can see your new number but you.`);

        }

        renderHUD();

        if(!p.hand.length){ p.hand.push(...p.discard.splice(0)); p.hand.sort((a,b)=>a-b);

          log(`${fmtP(p)} has danced their whole Fae Rune hand; all discards return.`, 'sys'); }

        break;

      }

      if(orChoice==='lure'){

        log(`${fmtP(p)} spends the <b>6</b> rune as a lure.`);

        const from=await chooseHouseFrom(p,'Lure: from','Draw a Wisp out of…', h=>G.nobles[h.id]>0);

        if(from==null) break;   // expired/failed choice — the rune is spent, the lure fizzles

        const to=await chooseHouseFrom(p,'Lure: into','…and let it settle in:', h=>h.id!==from);

        if(to==null) break;

        G.nobles[from]--; syncBoard();

        log(`A Wisp drifts from the ${fmtH(from)}…`);

        await placeNoble(to,p);

        if(!p.hand.length){ p.hand.push(...p.discard.splice(0)); p.hand.sort((a,b)=>a-b);

          log(`${fmtP(p)} has danced their whole Fae Rune hand; all discards return.`, 'sys'); }

        break;

      }

      // ----- Otherwise: dance the steps (after resolving the mandatory 1/2 stone action) -----

      log(`${fmtP(p)} dances a <b>${v}</b>.`);

      renderHUD();

      if(v===1 && flipPick){

        const st=G.steps[flipPick.tr][flipPick.k-1];

        st.c=!st.c;

        const vict=tumbleFae(flipPick.tr, flipPick.k);

        log(`${fmtP(p)} flips step ${flipPick.k} of the <b>${flipPick.tr}</b> to ${st.c?'Conjured':'Regular'}.`);

        vict.forEach(q=>log(`The stone flips, and ${fmtP(q)}\u2019s Glamour tumbles!`, 'alert'));

        syncBoard(); renderHUD();

      }

      if(v===2 && ferry && ferry.src){

        await ferryConjured(p, ferry.src.tr, ferry.src.k, ferry.dest.tr);

      }

      await allocate(p,p,v);

      if(!p.hand.length){

        p.hand.push(...p.discard.splice(0)); p.hand.sort((a,b)=>a-b);

        log(`${fmtP(p)} has danced their whole Fae Rune hand; all discards return.`, 'sys');

      }

      break;

    }

  }

  // Post-dance window: play remaining Faerie Magik, or end the turn.

  // In Masquerade there is no Magik — the turn simply ends.

  if(!(G.mode && G.mode.magik)) return;

  while(true){

    renderHUD();

    const ev=await seatArm(p, ['intrigue','end']);

    if(ev.type==='end') break;

    if(ev.name==='Midsummer Reel'){ await seatNotice(p, 'Midsummer Reel','This dances in place of a Fae Rune, and you have already danced this turn.'); continue; }

    const pts=await playActiveIntrigue(p, ev.name);

    if(pts>0) await allocate(p,p,pts);

  }

}

 

/* ============================================================

   AI BRAIN — belief-based decisions, per-player, no hidden info.

   Every function below reasons ONLY from what that player can see:

   - its own Court; its own Radiance ONLY if peeked (knownStatus)

   - every rival's Radiance (public, face-out)

   - Courts it has peeked/learned (knownHouses)

   - public events: wisp placements (placeEvidence), wisp counts,

     rune hands (public on the stands), Magik card COUNTS (public)

   No AI ever reads another player's hidden Court, hidden Magik hand,

   or another player's private knowledge. AIs share no state: each

   computes its own beliefs, so they cannot collude.

   ============================================================ */

function maxVisible(p){ return Math.max(...others(p).map(o=>o.status)); }

/* p's belief distribution over rival o's Court. Combines:

   deck composition (16 cards, minus p's own, minus known others) and

   public placement behavior (players tend to feed their own Court). */

function courtBeliefs(p, o){

  const kn=p.knownHouses[o.i];

  if(kn){ const w={}; HOUSES.forEach(h=>w[h.id]= h.id===kn?1:0); return w; }

  const counts={mountain:4,meadow:4,forest:4,river:4};

  counts[p.house]--;

  others(p).forEach(x=>{ const k=p.knownHouses[x.i]; if(k && x!==o) counts[k]--; });

  const ev=(G.placeEvidence&&G.placeEvidence[o.i])||{};

  const w={}; let tot=0;

  /* Human-calibrated evidence curve: players often bluff their first wisp or

     two, but three or more into one Court is too expensive to fake. So the

     1st placement is weak evidence, the 2nd moderate, the 3rd+ near-decisive. */

  const EV_CURVE=[0, 0.5, 1.6, 7.0];

  HOUSES.forEach(h=>{

    const base=Math.max(0.05, counts[h.id]);

    const e=ev[h.id]||0;

    const evid = e<EV_CURVE.length ? EV_CURVE[e] : EV_CURVE[3] + 3.0*(e-3);

    w[h.id]=base*(1+evid); tot+=w[h.id];

  });

  HOUSES.forEach(h=>w[h.id]/=tot);

  return w;

}

function pInCourt(p,o,H){ return courtBeliefs(p,o)[H]||0; }

/* p's legal belief about its OWN Radiance: exact if peeked, else uniform

   over the values it cannot see (its own card + the undealt pool). */

function selfStatusDist(p){

  if(p.knownStatus!==null) return [{v:p.knownStatus,w:1}];

  const u=unseenStatuses(p);

  return u.map(v=>({v,w:1/u.length}));

}

function selfStatusMean(p){ return selfStatusDist(p).reduce((a,x)=>a+x.v*x.w,0); }

/* P(p wins a Call in Court H right now).

   opts.assumeNot: a rival treated as certainly NOT in H (e.g. after swapping

   Courts with them, they hold p's old card). opts.house: evaluate as if p's

   Court were `house` (for swap/redraw planning). */

function pWinCall(p, H, opts){

  opts=opts||{};

  const myHouse = opts.house || p.house;

  if(myHouse!==H) return 0;

  let pw=0;

  selfStatusDist(p).forEach(({v,w})=>{

    let q=1;

    others(p).forEach(o=>{

      if(o.status<=v) return;                    // can't beat me

      const pi = (opts.assumeNot===o) ? 0 : pInCourt(p,o,H);

      q*=(1-pi);

    });

    pw+=w*q;

  });

  return pw;

}

/* Expected strongest rival Radiance lurking in H, from p's view (for blocking). */

function rivalThreatIn(p,H){

  let t=0;

  others(p).forEach(o=>{

    const pi=pInCourt(p,o,H);

    if(pi>0.28) t=Math.max(t, o.status*Math.min(1, pi*1.5));

  });

  return t;

}

/* Is a known (peeked) rival with a stronger number sharing my Court? */

function knownStrongerShares(p){

  const m=selfStatusMean(p);

  return others(p).some(o=>p.knownHouses[o.i]===p.house && o.status>m+0.5);

}

/* "Am I building toward a winnable Call in my own Court?" */

function wantsWin(p){ return pWinCall(p, p.house) >= 0.45; }

/* Which dance's FAVOR do I most need right now? */

function preferredTrack(p){

  // Bridge-aware valuation (validated by head-to-head simulation): the Bridge

  // is a real resource, favored when card-poor, sometimes crossed regardless.

  if(p.knownStatus===null && Math.random()<.5) return 'Faerie Ring';

  if(TRACKS.includes('Faerie Bridge') && trackLen('Faerie Bridge')>0){

    if(p.intrigues.length<2 && Math.random()<.55) return 'Faerie Bridge';

    if(Math.random()<.2) return 'Faerie Bridge';

  }

  // Fort control: a mid-to-endgame tactic. When a dangerous enemy Court is one

  // Wisp from armed, or the whole board runs hot, the lure-1/snuff-2 favor is

  // worth the trip in its own right. Midsummer only: the Masquerade's track

  // chain already ends at the Fort, so it needs no extra pull there.

  if(TRACKS.includes('Faerie Bridge')){

    const danger=HOUSES.some(h=>h.id!==p.house && G.nobles[h.id]>=quorum()-1 && rivalThreatIn(p,h.id)>2);

    if(danger && Math.random()<.45) return 'Faerie Fort';

    if(boardHeat(p)>=.5 && Math.random()<.2) return 'Faerie Fort';

  }

  if(p.knownStatus===null) return 'Faerie Ring';           // self-knowledge first

  const unknownStrong=others(p).filter(o=>!p.knownHouses[o.i] && o.status>=p.knownStatus);

  if(unknownStrong.length && Math.random()<.75) return 'Faerie Mound'; // scout the threats

  if(p.knownStatus<maxVisible(p) && Math.random()<.6) return 'Faerie Ring'; // trade up

  if(TRACKS.includes('Faerie Bridge') && p.intrigues.length===0 && Math.random()<.45) return 'Faerie Bridge';

  return 'Faerie Fort';                                     // wisp economy

}

function aiAllocChoice(owner, pts){

  let best=null;

  owner.cands.forEach((c,ci)=>{

    if(c.track){

      const need=trackLen(c.track)-c.steps;

      if(need<=pts && (!best || need<best.need)) best={ci, need};

    }

  });

  if(best) return {ci:best.ci};

 

  const isConj=(tr,step)=>{ const st=G.steps[tr]&&G.steps[tr][step-1]; return !!(st&&st.c); };

  let adv=null;

  owner.cands.forEach((c,ci)=>{ if(c.track && (!adv||c.steps>owner.cands[adv.ci].steps)) adv={ci}; });

  if(adv){

    if(pts===1){

      const c=owner.cands[adv.ci];

      if(isConj(c.track, c.steps+1)){

        const alt=owner.cands.findIndex((c2,ci2)=>

          ci2!==adv.ci && c2.track && c2.steps+1<=trackLen(c2.track) && !isConj(c2.track, c2.steps+1));

        if(alt>=0) return {ci:alt};

      }

    }

    return adv;

  }

  const idle=owner.cands.findIndex(c=>!c.track);

  let st=preferredTrack(owner);

  if(trackLen(st)<1) st=TRACKS.find(t=>trackLen(t)>=1);   // never enter an empty dance

  if(!st) return 'stop';

  return {ci:idle, start:st};

}

/* Wisp placement — the discipline fix. Build the OWN Court unless a known

   stronger rival shares it; never arm an enemy Court; force the ceiling only

   when likely to win the resulting Call. */

function aiPickHouse(p){

  const q=quorum(), coup=coupAt();

  const pwOwn=pWinCall(p, p.house);

  const blocked=knownStrongerShares(p);

  const forceGate=Math.max(0.42, 0.55 - 0.2*boardHeat(p));   // hot board: forcing at lower odds beats losing

  /* Decoy play — the same bluff level humans use: sometimes on the very first

     wisp, occasionally the second, never after. Only when the tempo is

     affordable (own Court nowhere near a Call, calm board) and the decoy is

     safe (never arms an enemy Court, avoids strong believed occupants).

     The false placement pollutes every rival's read of this AI. */

  if(G.placeEvidence){

    const mine=Object.values(G.placeEvidence[p.i]).reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0);

    const bluffP = mine===0 ? 0.38 : mine===1 ? 0.15 : 0;

    if(bluffP && Math.random()<bluffP && !blocked &&

       G.nobles[p.house]<=q-3 && boardHeat(p)<0.35){

      let d=null, ds=-1e9;

      HOUSES.forEach(h=>{

        if(h.id===p.house) return;

        const n=G.nobles[h.id];

        if(n+1>=q) return;                                   // never arm an enemy Court, even as theater

        const s = -n - rivalThreatIn(p,h.id)*0.7 + Math.random()*0.3;

        if(s>ds){ ds=s; d=h.id; }

      });

      if(d) return d;

    }

  }

  let bestId=null, best=-1e9;

  HOUSES.forEach(h=>{

    const n=G.nobles[h.id], own=h.id===p.house, n1=n+1;

    let s;

    if(n1>=coup){

      // Forces an immediate Call in h: only ever in my own Court, only when I likely win.

      s = own ? (pwOwn>=forceGate ? 200*pwOwn : -500) : -1e6;

    } else if(own){

      s = 10 + n1*2 + pwOwn*30;

      if(n1>=q) s += pwOwn*25 - 8;              // arming my own Call: great if I win it

      if(blocked) s -= 45;                      // feeding a Court a stronger known rival shares

    } else {

      // Dumping: pure damage control. Never bring an enemy Court to quorum;

      // prefer the Court whose believed occupants are weakest.

      const threat=rivalThreatIn(p, h.id);

      s = 1 - n*1.0 - threat*0.7 - (n1>=q ? 14+threat : 0);

    }

    if(s>best){ best=s; bestId=h.id; }

  });

  return bestId;

}

/* How likely is the game to end AGAINST p before its next Call opportunity?

   Built ONLY from public information: rival dancer positions and rune hands

   (both visible on the stands), Wisp counts — combined with p's own private

   Court beliefs. 0 = calm board, 1 = the axe is falling. */

function boardHeat(p){

  const m=selfStatusMean(p);

  const armed=HOUSES.filter(h=>h.id!==p.house && G.nobles[h.id]>=quorum());

  const near =HOUSES.filter(h=>h.id!==p.house && G.nobles[h.id]===quorum()-1);

  const coupThreat = HOUSES.some(h=>h.id!==p.house && G.nobles[h.id]===coupAt()-1);

  const myArmed = G.nobles[p.house]>=quorum();

  let heat=0;

  others(p).forEach(o=>{

    const need=minCompletion(o);                       // dancer positions: public

    const maxR=o.hand.length? Math.max(...o.hand) : 0; // rune hands: public

    const soon = need<=maxR ? 1 : 0.4;                 // can finish next turn vs. soon-ish

    let endT=0;

    // A completion lets o Call in a Court o belongs to. Any resolved Call in a

    // Court that isn't mine is an automatic loss for me.

    armed.forEach(h=>{ endT=Math.max(endT, pInCourt(p,o,h.id)); });

    near.forEach(h=>{  endT=Math.max(endT, 0.5*pInCourt(p,o,h.id)); });

    // My own armed Court is ALSO danger if a known-stronger rival shares it:

    // they can Call it and beat me.

    if(myArmed && p.knownHouses[o.i]===p.house && o.status>m) endT=Math.max(endT, 0.8);

    heat += soon*endT;

  });

  if(coupThreat) heat += 0.35;   // one placed Wisp forces a Call in a Court that isn't mine

  return Math.min(1, heat);

}

/* Should p Call in its own Court now? The threshold is DYNAMIC:
