   it falls as board heat rises (calling at 40% beats losing outright) and

   rises when waiting has real value (unpeeked self, unscouted strong rivals,

   a visible higher Radiance to swap for). Discounted by breakability when at

   exactly quorum (rivals' hidden Magik — counts are public — may snuff it). */

function aiShouldCall(p){

  if(G.nobles[p.house] < quorum()) return false;

  let pw = pWinCall(p, p.house);

  if(G.nobles[p.house]===quorum() && G.mode && G.mode.reactionWindows){

    const rivalCards = others(p).reduce((a,o)=>a+o.intrigues.length,0);

    pw *= Math.pow(0.93, rivalCards);

  }

  const heat = boardHeat(p);

  const m=selfStatusMean(p);

  let upside=0;                                          // value of waiting

  if(p.knownStatus===null) upside+=0.06;                 // could peek my own number

  upside += Math.min(0.06, 0.03*others(p).filter(o=>!p.knownHouses[o.i] && o.status>=m).length); // could scout threats

  if(p.knownStatus!==null && maxVisible(p)>p.knownStatus) upside+=0.05;  // could swap up

  const thr = Math.min(0.70, Math.max(0.36, 0.55 + upside - 0.26*heat));

  if(pw >= thr) return true;

  // Smooth boundary: a narrow linear ramp just below the threshold (no cliff,

  // no reads of the AI's exact bar) — not recklessness, just no hard edge.

  const ramp=(pw-(thr-0.08))/0.08;

  return ramp>0 && Math.random()<ramp*0.5;

}

async function aiKingdomAction(p, track){

  await wait(500);

  const qh=housesAtQuorum();

  if(qh.some(h=>h.id===p.house)){

    if(aiShouldCall(p)) return callForThrone(p.house, p, false);

  }

  if(track==='Faerie Bridge'){

     // Baseline: always gain a Faerie Magik card.

     drawIntrigue(p);

     log(`${fmtP(p)} completes the Faerie Bridge and gains a <b>Faerie Magik</b> card.`);

     // Secondary: move OR flip a stone. Prefer flipping a rival off a regular stone

     // (a flip tumbles them outright); ferry a rival off a conjured stone otherwise.

     const enemiesOnStones = [];

     TRACKS.forEach(tr=>G.steps[tr].forEach((st,idx)=>{

        const k=idx+1, on=faeOnStep(tr,k);

        if(on.length && !on.includes(p)) enemiesOnStones.push({tr,k,c:st.c});

     }));

     const regularEnemies = enemiesOnStones.filter(e=>!e.c);

     const conjuredEnemies = enemiesOnStones.filter(e=>e.c);

     if(regularEnemies.length){ await ACTIONS.flipStone(p); return; }         // flip tumbles them

     if(conjuredEnemies.length){ await aiFerryConjured(p, false); return; }   // ferry resets them

     // No rival to disrupt: mild coin-flip, and often just keep the card.

     if(Math.random()<0.4){ if(Math.random()<0.5) await ACTIONS.flipStone(p); else await aiFerryConjured(p, false); }

     return;

  }

  if(track==='Faerie Ring'){

    const top=others(p).reduce((a,b)=>a.status>b.status?a:b);

    if(p.knownStatus!==null){

      // Trade up: take the highest visible Radiance if it beats what I hold.

      if(top.status>p.knownStatus){ p._target=top; return ACTIONS.swapStatus(p); }

      // already holding the best it can see — refresh its knowledge rather than trade down

      return ACTIONS.lookStatus(p);

    }

    // Unknown own number: swapping loses no secrecy (Radiance is public to others)

    // and gains knowledge AND material in ONE favor. Swap immediately unless my

    // hidden card has a real chance of already beating the best visible.

    const u=unseenStatuses(p);

    const pBeat=u.filter(v=>v>top.status).length/Math.max(1,u.length);

    if(pBeat<=0.25){ p._target=top; return ACTIONS.swapStatus(p); }

    return ACTIONS.lookStatus(p);

  }

  if(track==='Faerie Fort'){

    // Value-compare: feed my own Court vs snuff the most dangerous rival Court.

    const donors=HOUSES.filter(h=>h.id!==p.house && G.nobles[h.id]>0);

    const canFeed = donors.length && G.nobles[p.house]+1<coupAt() && !knownStrongerShares(p);

    const feedVal = canFeed ? pWinCall(p,p.house)*(G.nobles[p.house]+1>=quorum()? 26 : 14) : -1;

    let snuffVal=-1, snuffTarget=null;

    const heat=boardHeat(p);

    HOUSES.filter(h=>h.id!==p.house && G.nobles[h.id]>0).forEach(h=>{

      const n=G.nobles[h.id], threat=rivalThreatIn(p,h.id);

      // Late-game control: armed and near-armed enemy Courts are worth real value,

      // scaling with how hot the board runs.

      // The favor takes TWO Wisps: armed and near-armed Courts fall further.

      const v = (n>=quorum()? (26+threat*1.3)*(1+heat*0.5)

               : n===quorum()-1? (14+threat*0.9)*(1+heat*0.5)

               : threat*0.35);

      if(v>snuffVal){ snuffVal=v; snuffTarget=h.id; }

    });

    if(feedVal>snuffVal && canFeed){

      // Steal from the most dangerous donor so the lure defends AND builds.

      p._from=donors.reduce((a,b)=> rivalThreatIn(p,a.id)+G.nobles[a.id] >= rivalThreatIn(p,b.id)+G.nobles[b.id] ? a : b).id;

      p._to=p.house;

      return ACTIONS.swapNoble(p);

    }

    if(snuffTarget && snuffVal>1){ p._from=snuffTarget; return ACTIONS.removeNoble(p); }

    if(canFeed){ p._from=donors[0].id; p._to=p.house; return ACTIONS.swapNoble(p); }

    log(`${fmtP(p)} lets the favor pass; no Wisps to move.`);

    return;

  }

  // ---- Faerie Mound: the Court-knowledge engine ----

  // 1) Escape a shared Court: if a KNOWN stronger rival shares mine, swap into a

  //    known-better Court (evaluated by actual post-swap win probability).

  if(knownStrongerShares(p)){

    let best=null, bestGain=0.06;

    others(p).forEach(o=>{

      const H=p.knownHouses[o.i];

      if(H===undefined || H===p.house) return;

      // After the swap I hold H and o certainly holds my old Court (not H).

      const gain = pWinCall(p, H, {house:H, assumeNot:o}) - pWinCall(p, p.house);

      if(gain>bestGain){ bestGain=gain; best=o; }

    });

    if(best){ p._target=best; return ACTIONS.swapHouse(p); }

  }

  // 2) The Court-Hopper: a KNOWN rival sits in a meaningfully richer Court, and

  //    the seat is winnable — hop into the gathered light instead of scouting on.

  {

    let best=null, bestScore=0;

    const myGuess = p.knownStatus!=null ? p.knownStatus : selfStatusMean(p);

    others(p).forEach(o=>{

      // Peek-certified knowledge, or strong placement-evidence inference: the

      // hopper reads where a rival sinks their Wisps.

      const H = p.knownHouses[o.i]

             || HOUSES.map(h=>h.id).find(hid=>hid!==p.house && pInCourt(p,o,hid)>=0.7);

      if(!H || H===p.house) return;

      const gain=G.nobles[H]-G.nobles[p.house];

      if(gain<1 || G.nobles[H]<quorum()-2) return;           // near-armed riches only

      const sharer=others(p).find(x=>x!==o && p.knownHouses[x.i]===H && x.status>myGuess+1);

      if(sharer) return;                                     // a known stronger Fae waits there

      const score=gain + (G.nobles[H]>=quorum()-1 ? 2 : 0) + (p.knownHouses[o.i] ? 1 : 0);

      if(score>bestScore){ bestScore=score; best=o; }

    });

    if(best && Math.random() < (bestScore>=4 ? 0.8 : 0.55)){

      p._target=best; return ACTIONS.swapHouse(p);

    }

  }

  // 3) Scout: peek the STRONGEST unknown rival — the one whose allegiance most

  //    changes my win probability either way.

  const unknown=others(p).filter(o=>!p.knownHouses[o.i]).sort((a,b)=>b.status-a.status);

  if(unknown.length){ p._target=unknown[0]; return ACTIONS.lookHouse(p); }

  // 4) All known: consider a pure-upgrade swap into a stronger position.

  {

    let best=null, bestGain=0.10;

    others(p).forEach(o=>{

      const H=p.knownHouses[o.i];

      if(H===p.house) return;

      const gain = pWinCall(p, H, {house:H, assumeNot:o}) - pWinCall(p, p.house);

      if(gain>bestGain){ bestGain=gain; best=o; }

    });

    if(best){ p._target=best; return ACTIONS.swapHouse(p); }

  }

  // 5) Nothing better — refresh knowledge of the strongest rival.

  p._target=others(p).reduce((a,b)=>a.status>b.status?a:b);

  return ACTIONS.lookHouse(p);

}

/* Redraw own Court? Only when the current Court is a losing seat: a known

   stronger rival shares it, or win probability there is hopeless. */

function aiWantsRedrawCourt(p){

  if(knownStrongerShares(p)) return Math.random()<0.8;

  if(pWinCall(p,p.house)<0.15 && G.nobles[p.house]<quorum()-1) return Math.random()<0.4;

  return false;

}

/* Blind-redraw own Radiance? Never a blind gamble (EV-neutral, loses nothing

   but gains nothing). Only when p has PEEKED and knows its number is low

   relative to the pool it would draw from — a genuinely positive-EV reroll.

   Uses ONLY knownStatus (self-knowledge) — never reads the hidden card. */

function aiWantsRedrawStatus(p){

  if(p.knownStatus===null) return false;               // unknown → EV-neutral, skip

  const pool=unseenStatuses(p).filter(v=>v!==p.knownStatus);   // the deck it would draw from

  if(!pool.length) return false;

  const mean=pool.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0)/pool.length;

  const contesting = G.nobles[p.house]>=quorum()-2;    // its Court is arming a Call

  return contesting && p.knownStatus<=4 && mean>p.knownStatus+1 && Math.random()<0.6;

}

/* Pick the AI's mandatory flip target: prefer flipping a stone under a rival who

   is close to finishing; never flip under itself if avoidable; else a harmless

   empty stone. Rival threat is judged by their VISIBLE Radiance (public). */

function aiPickFlip(p){

  let best=null, bestScore=-1e9;

  TRACKS.forEach(tr=>G.steps[tr].forEach((st,idx)=>{

    const k=idx+1, on=faeOnStep(tr,k);

    let s;

    const rivalsHere=on.filter(q=>q!==p);

    const selfHere=on.includes(p);

    if(rivalsHere.length){

      // tumbling a rival is great, especially one near the end of this dance,

      // and especially a HIGH-Radiance rival (their number is public).

      const nearEnd=trackLen(tr)-k<=2 ? 3 : 0;

      const strong=rivalsHere.some(q=>q.status>=7)?2:0;

      s=6+rivalsHere.length*2+nearEnd+strong;

      if(selfHere) s-=8;                           // but not if it also tumbles me

    } else if(selfHere){

      s=-20;                                       // never volunteer to tumble only myself

    } else {

      // harmless flip: prefer empty stones with no dancer nearby; slight noise

      s=1 - (idx*0.02) + Math.random()*0.5;

    }

    if(s>bestScore){ bestScore=s; best={tr,k}; }

  }));

  return best;

}

/* End-of-action Magik window for the AI (mirrors the human's post-dance loop):

   up to two valuable anytime plays with freshly drawn or held cards. */

async function aiPostMagik(p){

  if(!(G.mode && G.mode.magik)) return;

  const ep=EPOCH;

  for(let k=0;k<2 && !G.over && ep===EPOCH;k++){

    // Learn own number — the highest-value card while unknown.

    if(p.intrigues.includes('Scrying Pool') && p.knownStatus===null){

      await playActiveIntrigue(p,'Scrying Pool'); continue;

    }

    // Recall spent Magik: Whispered Lore turns the discard pile into a toolbox.

    if(p.intrigues.includes('Whispered Lore')){

      const uniq=[...new Set(G.intrigueDiscard)];

      const prize=['Wisp-Call','Midsummer Reel','Blight','Snuff Out','Bountiful Harvest'].find(nm=>uniq.includes(nm));

      if(prize && (p.intrigues.length<=2 || boardHeat(p)>=0.35) && Math.random()<0.7){

        await playActiveIntrigue(p,'Whispered Lore'); continue;

      }

    }

    // Arm my own Call when one Wisp short of quorum and I'd likely win it.

    if(p.intrigues.includes('Wisp-Call') && G.nobles[p.house]===quorum()-1 &&

       G.nobles[p.house]+1<coupAt() && pWinCall(p,p.house)>=Math.max(0.40, 0.50-0.15*boardHeat(p))){

      await playActiveIntrigue(p,'Wisp-Call'); continue;

    }

    // Defuse a Court sitting at/above quorum that I would lose to.

    let target=null, danger=0;

    HOUSES.filter(h=>h.id!==p.house).forEach(h=>{

      const n=G.nobles[h.id];

      if(n>=quorum()){ const t=rivalThreatIn(p,h.id); if(6+t>danger){ danger=6+t; target=h.id; } }

      else if(n===coupAt()-1){ if(9>danger){ danger=9; target=h.id; } }

    });

    if(target && p.intrigues.includes('Snuff Out')){

      p._from=target; await playActiveIntrigue(p,'Snuff Out'); continue;

    }

    if(target && p.intrigues.includes('Wisp-Lure') && G.nobles[p.house]+1<coupAt() && !knownStrongerShares(p)){

      p._from=target; p._to=p.house; await playActiveIntrigue(p,'Wisp-Lure'); continue;

    }

    break;

  }

}

async function aiTurn(p){

  const ep=EPOCH;

  banner(`${p.name}\u2019s turn`);

  await wait(850);

  if(ep!==EPOCH) return;

  if(p.intrigues.includes('Scrying Pool') && p.knownStatus===null && Math.random()<.9)

    await playActiveIntrigue(p,'Scrying Pool');

  if(ep!==EPOCH) return;

  // Defuse an imminent forced Call in an enemy Court I'd lose (the ceiling is one away).

  const danger=HOUSES.find(h=>G.nobles[h.id]===coupAt()-1 && h.id!==p.house);

  if(danger && p.intrigues.includes('Snuff Out') && Math.random()<.8){

    p._from=danger.id; await playActiveIntrigue(p,'Snuff Out');

  }

  if(ep!==EPOCH) return;

  // COMBO: if I can complete a dance this turn and my Court sits at quorum-2,

  // a Wisp-Call now + the completion Wisp = quorum → I can Call from the favor.

  if(p.intrigues.includes('Wisp-Call') && G.mode && G.mode.magik){

    const canComplete = p.hand.some(v=>v>=minCompletion(p)) || p.intrigues.includes('Midsummer Reel');

    const heat=boardHeat(p);

    const combo = canComplete && G.nobles[p.house]===quorum()-2 && pWinCall(p,p.house)>=Math.max(0.40, 0.50-0.15*heat);

    const build = G.nobles[p.house]>=quorum()-2 && G.nobles[p.house]+1<coupAt() && pWinCall(p,p.house)>=Math.max(0.42, 0.55-0.15*heat);

    if((combo || build) && G.nobles[p.house]+1<coupAt()){

      await playActiveIntrigue(p,'Wisp-Call');

    }

  }

  if(G.over || ep!==EPOCH) return;

  // ---- OR-choice pre-check: spend a 3/4/5 rune on its alternate effect instead of dancing ----

  // Only when the AI isn't about to complete a dance this turn (dancing takes priority then).

  if(G.mode && G.mode.runePowers){

    const canComplete = p.hand.some(v=>v>=minCompletion(p));

    if(!canComplete || Math.random()<0.35){

      // Redraw Court (rune 3)

      if(p.hand.includes(3) && aiWantsRedrawCourt(p)){

        p.hand.splice(p.hand.indexOf(3),1); p.discard.push(3);

        redrawCourt(p);

        log(`${fmtP(p)} spends the <b>3</b> rune to redraw their Court.`, 'sys');

        if(!p.hand.length){ p.hand.push(...p.discard.splice(0)); log(`${fmtP(p)} reclaims their discards.`, 'sys'); }

        renderHUD(); await aiPostMagik(p); await wait(500); return;

      }

      // Redraw Radiance (rune 4)

      if(p.hand.includes(4) && aiWantsRedrawStatus(p)){

        p.hand.splice(p.hand.indexOf(4),1); p.discard.push(4);

        redrawStatus(p);

        log(`${fmtP(p)} spends the <b>4</b> rune to blindly redraw their Radiance.`, 'sys');

        if(!p.hand.length){ p.hand.push(...p.discard.splice(0)); log(`${fmtP(p)} reclaims their discards.`, 'sys'); }

        renderHUD(); await aiPostMagik(p); await wait(500); return;

      }

      // Lure a Wisp (rune 6) — feed the AI's own Court toward a Call

      if(p.hand.includes(6) && wantsWin(p) && !knownStrongerShares(p) && G.nobles[p.house]<quorum() && G.nobles[p.house]+1<coupAt()){

        const donors=HOUSES.filter(h=>h.id!==p.house && G.nobles[h.id]>0);

        if(donors.length && Math.random()<0.6){

          p.hand.splice(p.hand.indexOf(6),1); p.discard.push(6);

          // Steal from the Court that most threatens me (defence + offence in one move).

          const from=donors.reduce((a,b)=> rivalThreatIn(p,a.id)+G.nobles[a.id] >= rivalThreatIn(p,b.id)+G.nobles[b.id] ? a : b).id;

          G.nobles[from]--; syncBoard();

          log(`${fmtP(p)} spends the <b>6</b> rune as a lure, and a Wisp drifts from the ${fmtH(from)}…`);

          await placeNoble(p.house,p);

          if(!p.hand.length){ p.hand.push(...p.discard.splice(0)); log(`${fmtP(p)} reclaims their discards.`, 'sys'); }

          renderHUD(); await aiPostMagik(p); await wait(500); return;

        }

      }

      // Force a redraw (rune 5), three triggers in priority order:

      // (1) DEFUSE an imminent Call — a rival poised to finish a dance beside

      //     an armed Court they likely belong to gets their Radiance torn into

      //     the fog. Even a lucky reroll leaves them blind at the worst moment.

      // (2) Tear the table's dominant number (visible 8/9) away.

      // (3) Eject a KNOWN stronger rival from my own Court.

      if(p.hand.includes(5)){

        const m=selfStatusMean(p);

        const top=others(p).reduce((a,b)=>a.status>b.status?a:b);

        const shared=others(p).find(o=>p.knownHouses[o.i]===p.house && o.status>m);

        let t=null, which=null;

        let defuse=null;

        others(p).forEach(o=>{

          if(defuse) return;

          const need=minCompletion(o), maxR=o.hand.length?Math.max(...o.hand):0;

          if(need>maxR) return;                            // can't finish soon (hands are public)

          HOUSES.forEach(h=>{

            if(defuse) return;

            if(G.nobles[h.id]<quorum()-1) return;          // Court not armed or near-armed

            if(pInCourt(p,o,h.id)<0.5) return;             // act on conviction, not weak suspicion

            const iLose = h.id!==p.house || o.status>m;    // a Call there goes against me

            if(iLose) defuse=o;

          });

        });

        if(defuse && Math.random()<0.75){ t=defuse; which='radiance'; }

        else if(top.status>=8 && top.status>m && Math.random()<0.5){ t=top; which='radiance'; }

        else if(shared && Math.random()<0.55){ t=shared; which='court'; }

        if(t){

          p.hand.splice(p.hand.indexOf(5),1); p.discard.push(5);

          if(which==='court'){

            redrawCourt(t);

            log(`${fmtP(p)} spends the <b>5</b> rune: ${fmtP(t)} is forced to discard their Court and draw anew.`, 'alert');

            await seatNotice(t, 'Your Court is torn away', `${p.name} forces you to redraw: you now belong to the <b>${HOUSE_BY_ID[t.house].name}</b>. Only you know this.`);

          } else {

            redrawStatus(t);

            log(`${fmtP(p)} spends the <b>5</b> rune: ${fmtP(t)} is forced to blindly redraw their Radiance.`, 'alert');

            await seatNotice(t, 'Your Radiance is torn away', `${p.name} forces you to redraw your Radiance <b>unseen</b>: everyone can see your new number but you.`);

          }

          if(!p.hand.length){ p.hand.push(...p.discard.splice(0)); log(`${fmtP(p)} reclaims their discards.`, 'sys'); }

          renderHUD(); await aiPostMagik(p); await wait(500); return;

        }

      }

    }

  }

  if(G.over || ep!==EPOCH) return;

 

  const need=minCompletion(p);

  let pts=null, playedCard=null;

  if(!p.hand.some(v=>v>=need) && need<=6 && p.intrigues.includes('Midsummer Reel')){

    takeIntrigue(p,'Midsummer Reel');

    log(`${fmtP(p)} plays <b>Midsummer Reel</b> in place of a Fae Rune (${need}).`);

    renderHUD();

    const canceled=await breachWindow(p,'Midsummer Reel');

    if(!canceled) G.intrigueDiscard.push('Midsummer Reel');   // breachWindow already discards it when canceled

    pts = canceled? 0 : need;

    if(!canceled){

      playedCard = need;   // the Reel dances as the chosen rune — its power (flip/move/etc.) applies below

    }

  } else {

    let card = p.hand.filter(v=>v>=need).sort((a,b)=>a-b)[0];

    if(!card) card = need>4 && p.hand.includes(1) ? 1 : Math.max(...p.hand);

    if(p.intrigues.includes('Bountiful Harvest') && !p.hand.some(v=>v>=need) && Math.max(...p.hand)+3>=need && Math.random()<.7){

      await playActiveIntrigue(p,'Bountiful Harvest');

      card=Math.max(...p.hand);

      p.hand.splice(p.hand.indexOf(card),1); p.discard.push(card);

      log(`${fmtP(p)} dances a <b>${card}</b>.`);

      pts=card+3; playedCard=card;

    } else {

      p.hand.splice(p.hand.indexOf(card),1); p.discard.push(card);

      log(`${fmtP(p)} dances a <b>${card}</b>.`);

      pts=card; playedCard=card;

    }

  }

  if(ep!==EPOCH) return;

  renderHUD();

  // Rune 1 played to dance → MANDATORY flip first (tumbles whoever's on it). Midsummer only.

  if(playedCard===1 && !G.over && G.mode && G.mode.runePowers){

    const fp=aiPickFlip(p);

    if(fp){

      await wait(400); if(ep!==EPOCH||G.over) return;

      const st=G.steps[fp.tr][fp.k-1]; st.c=!st.c;

      const vict=tumbleFae(fp.tr, fp.k);

      log(`${fmtP(p)} flips step ${fp.k} of the <b>${fp.tr}</b> to ${st.c?'Conjured':'Regular'}.`);

      vict.forEach(q=>log(`The stone flips, and ${fmtP(q)}\u2019s Glamour tumbles!`, 'alert'));

      syncBoard(); renderHUD();

    }

  }

  if(ep!==EPOCH) return;

  // Rune 2 played to dance → MANDATORY move of a conjured stone (if any exist). Midsummer only.

  if(playedCard===2 && !G.over && G.mode && G.mode.runePowers) await aiFerryConjured(p, true);

  if(ep!==EPOCH) return;

  if(pts>0) await allocate(p,p,pts);

  if(ep!==EPOCH) return;

  if(!p.hand.length){

    p.hand.push(...p.discard.splice(0));

    log(`${fmtP(p)} has danced their whole Fae Rune hand; all discards return.`, 'sys');

  }

  renderHUD();

  // Post-dance window: use freshly drawn or held Magik immediately (parity with the human).

  if(!G.over && ep===EPOCH) await aiPostMagik(p);

  if(ep!==EPOCH) return;

  renderHUD();

  await wait(500);

}

 

/* ============================================================

   Boot, Dragging and Controls

   ============================================================ */

function makeDraggable(el, handleSelector) {

  let pos1 = 0, pos2 = 0, pos3 = 0, pos4 = 0;

  let isDragging = false;

  const handle = handleSelector ? (el.querySelector(handleSelector) || el) : el;

  handle.style.cursor = 'move';

 

  handle.addEventListener('mousedown', dragStart, { passive: false });

  handle.addEventListener('touchstart', dragStart, { passive: false });

  // Prevent drag-clicks from activating buttons

  el.addEventListener('click', (e) => {

    if(isDragging) { e.stopPropagation(); e.preventDefault(); }

  }, true);

  function dragStart(e) {

    if (e.type === 'mousedown' && e.button !== 0) return;

   

    const target = e.target;

    if (target.tagName === 'BUTTON' && !target.classList.contains('loghead') && target !== handle) {

      return;

    }

   

    const clientX = e.type === 'touchstart' ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;

    const clientY = e.type === 'touchstart' ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;

   

    pos3 = clientX;

    pos4 = clientY;

   

    document.addEventListener('mouseup', dragEnd);

    document.addEventListener('touchend', dragEnd);

    document.addEventListener('mousemove', dragMove, { passive: false });

    document.addEventListener('touchmove', dragMove, { passive: false });

  }

  function dragMove(e) {

    isDragging = true;

    const clientX = e.type === 'touchmove' ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;

    const clientY = e.type === 'touchmove' ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;

   

    pos1 = pos3 - clientX;

    pos2 = pos4 - clientY;

    pos3 = clientX;

    pos4 = clientY;

   

    const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();

    let newTop = rect.top - pos2;

    let newLeft = rect.left - pos1;

   

    const pad = 10;

    newTop = Math.max(pad, Math.min(window.innerHeight - el.offsetHeight - pad, newTop));

    newLeft = Math.max(pad, Math.min(window.innerWidth - el.offsetWidth - pad, newLeft));

   

    el.style.right = 'auto';

    el.style.bottom = 'auto';

    el.style.left = newLeft + 'px';

    el.style.top = newTop + 'px';

   

    if (e.cancelable) {

      e.preventDefault();

    }

  }

  function dragEnd() {

    document.removeEventListener('mouseup', dragEnd);

    document.removeEventListener('touchend', dragEnd);

    document.removeEventListener('mousemove', dragMove);

    document.removeEventListener('touchmove', dragMove);

    setTimeout(() => isDragging = false, 50);

  }

}

/* ---------- THE ASSEMBLY: every dancer confirms before the first turn ----------

   Shows each human their view of the table — turn order, colors, and every

   Radiance they can legitimately see (their own faces away) — and waits for

   ALL of them to click Ready. Host-authoritative through the seat wrappers,

   so remote seats get the same gate over the wire; an away seat resolves

   instantly and never blocks the table. No clocks run during the gate. */

let READY_GATE=false;

function readyHTML(viewer){

  const rows=G.players.map((q,idx)=>{

    const rad=(q===viewer)? '<span style="opacity:.75">? \u00b7 faces away</span>' : `<b>${q.status}</b>`;

    const tag=(q===viewer)? ' <span style="opacity:.7">(you)</span>' : (q.isHuman? '' : ' <span style="opacity:.55">(fae)</span>');

    return `<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;gap:16px;margin:3px 0;">`+

      `<span><span style="display:inline-block;width:9px;height:9px;border-radius:50%;background:${q.color};border:1px solid #0006;margin-right:6px;"></span>${idx+1}. ${q.name}${tag}</span>`+

      `<span>Radiance ${rad}</span></div>`;

  }).join('');

  return `<div style="text-align:left">${rows}</div><div class="hr"></div>`+

    `The dance proceeds in this order, beginning with <b>${G.players[0].name}</b>.`;

}

async function readyGate(){

  const humans=G.players.filter(q=>q.isHuman);

  READY_GATE=true;

  try{

    if(humans.length>1) log(`<b>The dance assembles</b> \u2014 awaiting every dancer\u2019s ready\u2026`, 'sys');

    await Promise.all(humans.map(async q=>{

      await seatChoose(q, 'The Dance Assembles', readyHTML(q), [{label:'\u2726 Ready to Begin', value:1}]);

      if(humans.length>1) log(`${fmtP(q)} is ready.`, 'sys');

    }));

  } finally { READY_GATE=false; }

  banner('THE DANCE BEGINS');

}

async function gameLoop(){

  const ep=EPOCH;

  try{

    while(!G.over && ep===EPOCH){

      if(NET.role==='host' && NET.inGame){ await reconcileSeats(); hostPersist(); }

      if(G.over || ep!==EPOCH) break;

      const p=G.players[G.turn];

      renderHUD();

      const clocked = NET.role==='host' && NET.inGame && NET.cfg && NET.cfg.timer>0 && p.isHuman

                      && (p.i===MY_SEAT || !!connForSeat(p.i));   // an away human's turn passes instantly — no clock flash

      if(clocked) clockStart(p);

      try{

        if(p.isHuman) await humanTurn(p); else await aiTurn(p);

      } finally { if(clocked) clockStop(); }

      if(G.over || ep!==EPOCH) break;

      G.turn=(G.turn+1)%G.players.length;

    }

  }catch(e){ if(!(e instanceof GameOver)) console.error(e); }

  if(ep===EPOCH) renderHUD();

}

// Peeping UI handlers

$('#modalpeek').onclick = () => {

  $('#modalwrap').style.display = 'none';

  $('#peekbanner').style.display = 'flex';

};

$('#modalrestore').onclick = () => {

  $('#peekbanner').style.display = 'none';

  $('#modalwrap').style.display = 'flex';

};

$('#quitbtn').onclick = () => { $('#quitconfirm').style.display='flex'; };

$('#quityes').onclick = () => {

  // A DELIBERATE quit abandons the saved game (host) or saved seat (guest);

  // a crash or refresh never reaches this handler, so Resume/Rejoin survive those.

  LEAVING=true;

  try{ if(NET.role==='host' && NET.inGame) hostPersistClear(); }catch(e){}

  try{ if(NET.role==='guest' && NET.inGame) localStorage.removeItem(SEAT_KEY); }catch(e){}

  location.reload();

};

$('#quitno').onclick = () => { $('#quitconfirm').style.display='none'; };

 

addEventListener('error', e=>{ try{

  const where=e.filename? ` (${String(e.filename).split('/').pop()}:${e.lineno})` : '';

  const msg=(e.message==='Script error.'||e.message==='Script error')

    ? 'A network-library error was hidden by the browser. Check the console (F12) for details.'

    : `${e.message}${where}`;

  console.error('[Faerie Dances]', e.error||e.message, e.error&&e.error.stack||'');

  log(`\u26a0 Something went wrong: ${msg}`, 'alert');

}catch(_){} });

addEventListener('unhandledrejection', e=>{ try{

  console.error('[Faerie Dances]', e.reason);

  log(`\u26a0 Something went wrong: ${(e.reason&&e.reason.message)||e.reason}`, 'alert');

}catch(_){} });

/* UI-side boot shared by solo play, the multiplayer host, and joining guests

   (guests never run newGame or the loop — they render broadcast state). */

function bootShell(modeId){

  const mode = MODES[modeId] || MODES.midsummer;

  TRACKS = mode.tracks;              // must be set before init3D draws threads/edges

  $('#setup').style.display='none';

  $('#dock').style.display='flex';

  $('#quitbtn').style.display='block';

  init3D(mode);

  return mode;

}

function bootGame(nPlayers, modeId, opts){

  const mode = bootShell(modeId);

  newGame(nPlayers, mode.id, opts);

  if(FORCE_WIRE) log(`<b>FORCE_WIRE is ON</b>: your own choices travel the loopback wire (serialize \u2192 answer \u2192 validate). Any snag appears here in red.`, 'sys');

  refreshRulebook(mode);

  syncBoard();

  renderHUD();

  finishBootUI(mode);

}

function refreshRulebook(mode){

  $('#rulebook .rbbody').innerHTML =

    RULEBOOK_HTML[mode.id].replace(/__Q__/g, quorum()).replace(/__C__/g, coupAt());

}

function finishBootUI(mode){

  // Mode-dependent reference UI: each game shows only its own rules.

  refreshRulebook(mode);

  $('#magiktoggle').style.display = mode.magik ? 'block' : 'none';

  $('#fdlegrow').style.display = mode.tracks.includes('Faerie Bridge') ? '' : 'none';

  // Wire up draggability for maximized panels

  makeDraggable($('#log'), '.loghead');

  makeDraggable($('#rulebook'), '.loghead');

  makeDraggable($('#legend'), '.loghead');

  makeDraggable($('#magikpanel'), '.loghead');

  makeDraggable($('#chatpanel'), '.loghead');

  // Touching a panel brings it to the front of the panel stack

  ['#log','#rulebook','#legend','#magikpanel'].forEach(s=>{

    const el=$(s); el.addEventListener('pointerdown', ()=>bringToFront(el));

  });

  // Wire up draggability for minimized toggles

  // Any center-transformed element must freeze to honest left/top before its

  // first drag, or the drag math jumps by half its width.

  const freezeCenter=el=>{

    if(el.style.position!=='fixed' || (el.style.transform!=='none' && !/^scale/.test(el.style.transform))){

      const r=el.getBoundingClientRect();

      const k=el._scale||1;

      el.style.position='fixed'; el.style.left=r.left+'px'; el.style.top=r.top+'px';

      el.style.bottom='auto'; el.style.transform=(k!==1?'scale('+k+')':'none'); el.style.margin='0';

      el.style.transformOrigin='top left';

    }

  };

  // Proportional panel resizing: a header grip scales the whole panel, fonts

  // and all, between 55% and 190%. One transform, everything in step.

  const makeResizable=(el, minBtn)=>{

    if(!el || el._rzWired) return;

    el._rzWired=true;

    const corner=document.createElement('div');

    corner.className='cornerctl';

    if(minBtn){                                     // relocated live: its onclick rides along

      minBtn.style.position='static'; minBtn.style.top='auto'; minBtn.style.right='auto';

      corner.appendChild(minBtn);

    }

    const g=document.createElement('span');

    g.className='rgrip'; g.title='Drag to resize'; g.textContent='\u2922';

    corner.appendChild(g);

    el.appendChild(corner);

    let s0=1, d0=1;

    const pt=e=>e.touches?e.touches[0]:e;

    const move=e=>{

      const t=pt(e), r=el.getBoundingClientRect();

      const d=Math.hypot(t.clientX-r.left, t.clientY-r.top);

      const k=Math.max(.55, Math.min(1.9, s0*(d/d0)));

      el._scale=k;

      el.style.transformOrigin='top left';

      el.style.transform='scale('+k+')';

      if(e.cancelable) e.preventDefault();

    };

    const up=()=>{

      document.removeEventListener('pointermove',move); document.removeEventListener('pointerup',up);

      document.removeEventListener('touchmove',move); document.removeEventListener('touchend',up);

    };

    const down=e=>{

      e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();

      freezeCenter(el);

      const t=pt(e), r=el.getBoundingClientRect();

      s0=el._scale||1;

      d0=Math.max(24, Math.hypot(t.clientX-r.left, t.clientY-r.top));

      document.addEventListener('pointermove',move); document.addEventListener('pointerup',up);

      document.addEventListener('touchmove',move,{passive:false}); document.addEventListener('touchend',up);

    };

    g.addEventListener('pointerdown',down);

    g.addEventListener('touchstart',down,{passive:false});

  };

  makeResizable($('#log'), $('#logmin'));

  makeResizable($('#rulebook'), $('#rbmin'));

  makeResizable($('#legend'), $('#legmin'));

  makeResizable($('#magikpanel'), $('#magikmin'));

  makeResizable($('#chatpanel'), $('#chatmin'));

  makeResizable($('#dock'), $('#dockmin'));

  makeResizable($('#modal'), $('#modalpeek'));

  [['#modal','#mtitle'], ['#peekbanner',null], ['#banner',null]].forEach(([sel,head])=>{

    const el=$(sel);

    if(!el || el._dragWired) return;

    el._dragWired=true;

    (head?$(head):el).addEventListener('pointerdown', ()=>freezeCenter(el));

    makeDraggable(el, head);

  });

  // The hand dock drags by its slim header; the shared scale-aware freezer

  // converts the centering transform to honest coordinates WITHOUT touching

  // any resize the player has applied.

  const dockEl=$('#dock');

  $('#dockhead').addEventListener('pointerdown', ()=>freezeCenter(dockEl));

  makeDraggable(dockEl, '#dockhead');

  makeDraggable($('#docktoggle'));

  makeDraggable($('#logtoggle'));

  makeDraggable($('#rbtoggle'));

  makeDraggable($('#legtoggle'));

  makeDraggable($('#magiktoggle'));

  makeDraggable($('#tutcontinue'));

}

async function joinDance(modeId){

  const n=await choose(

    MODES[modeId].name,

    'How many Fae at the dance? (you + AI rivals)',

    [ {label:'3 Fae', sub:'An intimate revel.',            value:3},

      {label:'4 Fae', sub:'A fine number for a dance.',    value:4},

      {label:'5 Fae', sub:'A crowded glade.',              value:5},

      {label:'6 Fae', sub:'A grand ball.',                 value:6},

      {label:'Back',  sub:'Return to the moonlit menu.',   value:null, cls:'passopt'} ]);

  if(!n) return;

  const q=await sliderChoose(

    'Wisps for a Call',

    'A Court holding this many Wisps may host a Call for a True Name. Three more than this <b>forces</b> a Call at once.',

    5, 10, 5, v=>`${v} Wisps (the ${v+2}th forces a Call)`);

  if(q==null) return;

  bootGame(n, modeId, {quorum:q});

  log(`You belong to the ${fmtH(G.players[MY_SEAT].house)}. Your Radiance faces away from you: dance blind, or find a way to glimpse it.`, 'sys');

  await readyGate();

  gameLoop();

}

/* ============================================================

   MULTIPLAYER — host-a-room over PeerJS (WebRTC, free public broker).

   The HOST's browser owns the game engine; guests join by code and

   render broadcast state from their own seat's perspective.

   Stage 2: guests join, sit, and spectate a live game (their seats

   play via AI). Stage 3 hands remote humans their turns. Stage 4

   enforces the turn clock configured here.

   ============================================================ */

const NET={ role:null, peer:null, conns:[], seatOf:new Map(), names:{}, cfg:null, code:null,

            inGame:false, lastSync:0, syncT:null, pendingState:null, crumbs:[],

            tokens:{}, myToken:null, myName:'', booted:false };

const CODE_ALPHA='ABCDEFGHJKMNPQRSTUVWXYZ23456789';   // no ambiguous glyphs

function mkCode(){ let s=''; for(let i=0;i<5;i++) s+=CODE_ALPHA[Math.floor(Math.random()*CODE_ALPHA.length)]; return s; }

function mkToken(){ let s=''; for(let i=0;i<16;i++) s+=CODE_ALPHA[Math.floor(Math.random()*CODE_ALPHA.length)]; return s; }

/* A guest's claim to its seat, kept in localStorage so a refresh (or a whole

   browser restart) can walk back into the room. The token is a bearer secret

   for the seat: never logged, never included in diagnostics. */

const SEAT_KEY='faerie-dances-last-seat';

function savedSeat(){ try{ const j=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(SEAT_KEY)||'null'); return (j && j.code && j.token)? j : null; }catch(e){ return null; } }

function saveSeat(o){ try{ localStorage.setItem(SEAT_KEY, JSON.stringify(o)); }catch(e){} }

/* ---------- host game persistence ----------

   The host snapshots the FULL game (its own machine already holds it all) at

   every TURN BOUNDARY: state as of "this seat is about to act". A resume

   therefore always replays from the start of the interrupted turn — a valid,

   fair position — never from the middle of a half-executed turn, which the

   state object alone cannot represent. Cleared when a True Name resolves or

   the host deliberately quits; a refresh or crash leaves it for Resume. */

const HOST_KEY='faerie-dances-host-game';

function savedHost(){ try{ const j=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(HOST_KEY)||'null');

  return (j && j.code && j.cfg && j.g && j.g.modeId)? j : null; }catch(e){ return null; } }

function hostPersist(){

  if(NET.role!=='host' || !NET.inGame || !G || G.over) return;

  try{

    localStorage.setItem(HOST_KEY, JSON.stringify({

      code:NET.code, cfg:NET.cfg, names:NET.names, tokens:NET.tokens,

      g:snapG(null), t:Date.now()

    }));

  }catch(e){ crumbPush('Persist failed: '+((e&&e.message)||e)); }

}

function hostPersistClear(){ try{ localStorage.removeItem(HOST_KEY); }catch(e){} }

function peerIdFor(code){ return 'faerie-dances-room-'+code; }

/* Protocol version: bumped whenever the wire format changes. A guest whose

   file speaks a different protocol is turned away at the door with a clear

   message — a silent cross-version desync would be far worse than a bounce. */

const NET_VER=1;

/* The broker (signaling) connection can drop while the game's own P2P wires

   stay healthy — laptop sleep, a wifi blip. Without the broker, no NEW dials

   (rejoins!) can arrive, so reconnect to it automatically with backoff. */

function wireBrokerAutoReconnect(peer, who){

  let tries=0;

  peer.on('open', ()=>{ tries=0; });

  peer.on('disconnected', ()=>{

    if(peer.destroyed) return;

    if(tries>=5){ netCrumb(who+': broker connection lost for good \u2014 existing wires continue, but new joins/rejoins cannot arrive.'); return; }

    tries++;

    netCrumb(who+': broker connection lost \u2014 reconnecting ('+tries+'/5)\u2026');

    setTimeout(()=>{ try{ if(!peer.destroyed) peer.reconnect(); }catch(e){} }, 1500*tries);

  });

}

/* ---------- the faerie roads: ICE / relay configuration ----------

   Default is public STUN only. When two networks cannot punch a direct path

   (the signature: signaling delivered, data channel never opens), a TURN

   relay is required, and both host AND guests must use the same one. The

   relay box on the room forms accepts either the JSON iceServers array a

   TURN provider hands out, or simple lines: turn:host:port|username|credential

   Stored in localStorage; also settable via setRelay('...') in the console. */

const RELAY_KEY='faerie-dances-relay';

function relayRaw(){ try{ return localStorage.getItem(RELAY_KEY)||''; }catch(e){ return ''; } }

function parseRelay(raw){

  raw=(raw||'').trim();

  if(!raw) return [];

  if(raw[0]==='[' || raw[0]==='{'){

    try{

      const j=JSON.parse(raw);

      const arr=Array.isArray(j)? j : (Array.isArray(j.iceServers)? j.iceServers : [j]);

      return arr.filter(s=>s && s.urls);

    }catch(e){ crumbPush('Relay config is not valid JSON: '+((e&&e.message)||e)); return []; }

  }

  const out=[];

  raw.split(/\n+/).forEach(line=>{

    const parts=line.split('|').map(x=>x.trim());

    if(!parts[0]) return;

    const s={urls:parts[0]};

    if(parts[1]) s.username=parts[1];

    if(parts[2]) s.credential=parts[2];

    out.push(s);

  });

  return out;

}

function iceConfig(){

  const relay=parseRelay(relayRaw());

  const servers=[{urls:'stun:stun.l.google.com:19302'}].concat(relay);

  crumbPush('ICE config: '+servers.length+' server entr'+(servers.length===1?'y':'ies')

    +(relay.length? ' (relay configured)' : ' (STUN only — no relay)'));

  return {debug:0, config:{iceServers:servers}};

}

window.setRelay=function(raw){

  try{ if(raw==null || String(raw).trim()==='') localStorage.removeItem(RELAY_KEY);

       else localStorage.setItem(RELAY_KEY, String(raw)); }catch(e){}

  const n=parseRelay(relayRaw()).length;

  crumbPush('Relay config saved: '+n+' server entr'+(n===1?'y':'ies')+'.');

  return n;

};

/* Crumb the ICE lifecycle of a DataConnection: connection/gathering states and

   the FIRST candidate of each type. The fingerprint reads like this —

   srflx seen: STUN worked (your public address was discovered);

   relay seen: the TURN relay is reachable and credentialed;

   neither: UDP is blocked outright on this network;

   states checking→failed: no candidate pair could meet in the middle. */

function wireIceSpy(conn, who){

  const seen={};

  const attach=()=>{

    const pc=conn.peerConnection;

    if(!pc) return false;

    if(pc._faerieSpy) return true;

    pc._faerieSpy=true;

    try{

      pc.addEventListener('iceconnectionstatechange', ()=>crumbPush('ICE '+who+': state '+pc.iceConnectionState));

      pc.addEventListener('icegatheringstatechange', ()=>crumbPush('ICE '+who+': gathering '+pc.iceGatheringState));

      pc.addEventListener('icecandidate', ev=>{

        const c=ev.candidate;

        if(!c || !c.candidate) return;

        const m=/ typ (\w+)/.exec(c.candidate);

        const typ=m? m[1] : '?';

        if(seen[typ]) return;

        seen[typ]=true;

        crumbPush('ICE '+who+': first '+typ+' candidate'

          +(typ==='relay'? ' — TURN relay reachable' : typ==='srflx'? ' — STUN worked' : ''));

      });

    }catch(e){}

    return true;

  };

  if(!attach()){

    const iv=setInterval(()=>{ if(attach()) clearInterval(iv); }, 200);

    setTimeout(()=>clearInterval(iv), 15000);

  }

}

function netUnavailable(){

  if(typeof Peer==='undefined')

    return 'Multiplayer needs an internet connection (the PeerJS library did not load).';

  if(typeof RTCPeerConnection==='undefined' && typeof webkitRTCPeerConnection==='undefined')

    return 'This viewer cannot open the faerie roads: it has no WebRTC. Open this file in Safari or Chrome (not an in-app preview) to host or join a room.';

  return null;

}

function netAll(msg){ NET.conns.forEach(c=>{ try{ c.send(msg); }catch(e){} }); }

function snapG(viewSeat){

  // Strip the mode object (rebound by id on arrival) and every _underscore

  // scratch field — transient AI intent like _target holds live player

  // references, which are circular and meaningless to a spectator anyway.

  const s=JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(G, (k,v)=> (k==='mode' || (typeof k==='string' && k.charAt(0)==='_'))? undefined : v));

  s.modeId=G.mode.id;

  if(viewSeat==null) return s;   // host-local/debug view only — never send this on the wire

  // PER-SEAT REDACTION: a client receives exactly what its player could see at

  // a physical table, and nothing more. Everything hidden stays host-side.

  // Decks and the facedown discards travel as counts only (order is host-only).

  s.statusDeckN=s.statusDeck.length;       delete s.statusDeck;

  s.houseDeckN=s.houseDeck.length;         delete s.houseDeck;

  s.intrigueDeckN=s.intrigueDeck.length;   delete s.intrigueDeck;

  s.houseDiscardN=s.houseDiscard.length;   delete s.houseDiscard;    // discarded Courts were secret

  s.statusDiscardN=s.statusDiscard.length; delete s.statusDiscard;

  // (intrigueDiscard stays: played Magik is announced and Lore-searchable — public.)

  // Which claimed seats currently have no wire (public: the table can see an empty chair,

  // whether its cards are momentarily danced by the Fae or not).

  try{ s.away=G.players.filter(pp=>pp.i!==MY_SEAT && NET.names[pp.i]!=null && !connForSeat(pp.i)).map(pp=>pp.i); }catch(e){ s.away=[]; }

  s.players.forEach(p=>{

    if(p.i===viewSeat){

      if(p.knownStatus===null) p.status=null;   // your own Radiance faces away from you

    } else {

      p.house=null;                             // rivals' Courts are facedown

      p.knownStatus=null; p.knownHouses={};     // rivals' private knowledge is theirs alone

      p.intrigueCount=p.intrigues.length;       // Magik hands are secret; counts are public

      p.intrigues=[];

    }

  });

  return s;

}

function applyState(s){

  const modeId=s.modeId; delete s.modeId;

  s.mode=MODES[modeId];

  G=s;

  TRACKS=G.mode.tracks;

  syncBoard(); renderHUD();

}

/* Guest: a state broadcast that lands while a board prompt (stone pick or

   dancer move) is open would replace G and rebuild the tiles under the

   prompt's highlights and captured player refs. Defer it; apply on resolve. */

function flushPendingState(){

  if(NET.pendingState && !PICK && !MOVE){

    const s=NET.pendingState; NET.pendingState=null; applyState(s);

  }

}

/* ---------- RPC: the host asks a remote seat for a decision ---------- */

let RPC_SEQ=1; const RPC_PENDING=new Map();   // id -> {seat, res}

function connForSeat(seat){ for(const [c,s] of NET.seatOf) if(s===seat) return c; return null; }

function netStateTo(c){

  const seat=NET.seatOf.get(c);

  if(seat==null) return;                        // no seat, no state — never ship the unredacted view

  try{ c.send({type:'state', g:snapG(seat)}); }catch(e){}

}

function netStateAll(){ NET.conns.forEach(c=>netStateTo(c)); }

function rpcTo(seat, kind, payload){

  const c=connForSeat(seat);

  if(!c) return Promise.resolve(null);          // seat unreachable — caller falls to a safe default

  netStateTo(c);                                 // the prompt must render against current truth

  const id=RPC_SEQ++;

  return new Promise(res=>{

    RPC_PENDING.set(id, {seat, res});

    try{ c.send({type:'rpc', id, kind, payload}); }

    catch(e){ RPC_PENDING.delete(id); res(null); }

  });

}

function rpcFail(seat){   // seat vanished: resolve everything it owed as null

  for(const [id,e] of [...RPC_PENDING]){ if(e.seat===seat){ RPC_PENDING.delete(id); e.res(null); } }

}

const seatRemote=p=> NET.role==='host' && p.isHuman && p.i!==MY_SEAT;

/* ---------- THE TURN CLOCK (host authority) ----------

   The main deadline wraps the OWNER's decisions only. Whenever the engine

   asks anyone ELSE for a decision (reaction windows: Blight, Cold Iron,

   Wisp-unveiled, the Call), the main clock PAUSES and the responder gets a

   short response clock of their own — so nobody can wait out a rival's turn

   by simply not answering "No Magik to use". Response expiry closes only

   that window ("the moment passes"); turn expiry keeps its old meaning:

   only already-committed actions stand, everything else defaults. */

let CLOCK=null;            // {seat, expired, endsAt, t, pausedRemain?}

let ACTIVE_CHOOSE=null;    // the on-screen modal's resolver (cancellable)

let CLOCK_UI=null;         // {endsAt, iv}

const REACT_SECS=10;       // a reaction window's whole allowance, per prompt

let REACT=null;            // {seat, expired, t, cancels:[]}

let REACT_DEPTH=0;

function clockExpired(){ return !!(CLOCK && CLOCK.expired); }

/* Is the clock that governs THIS seat's prompt expired? The owner answers to

   the main clock; a responder answers to the reaction clock; and once the

   main clock has expired, every prompt in the turn defaults (old behavior). */

function seatClockExpired(p){

  if(CLOCK && CLOCK.expired) return true;

  if(REACT && REACT.seat===p.i && REACT.expired) return true;

  return false;

}

function clockStart(p){

  const secs=NET.cfg.timer;

  CLOCK={seat:p.i, expired:false, endsAt:Date.now()+secs*1000, t:setTimeout(clockExpire, secs*1000)};

  clockShow(secs, p.i===MY_SEAT? 'Your turn' : p.name);

  netAll({type:'clock', secs, seat:p.i, name:p.name});

}

function clockStop(){

  if(!CLOCK) return;

  clearTimeout(CLOCK.t); CLOCK=null; clockHide();

  netAll({type:'clock', secs:0, seat:-1});

}

function clockPause(){

  if(!CLOCK || CLOCK.expired || CLOCK.pausedRemain!=null) return;

  clearTimeout(CLOCK.t);

  CLOCK.pausedRemain=Math.max(0, CLOCK.endsAt-Date.now());

}

function clockResume(){

  if(!CLOCK){   // an AI turn has no main clock — just clear the reaction chip everywhere

    clockHide(); netAll({type:'clock', secs:0, seat:-1});

    return;

  }

  if(CLOCK.expired || CLOCK.pausedRemain==null) return;

  const remain=CLOCK.pausedRemain; delete CLOCK.pausedRemain;

  CLOCK.endsAt=Date.now()+remain;

  CLOCK.t=setTimeout(clockExpire, remain);

  const p=G && G.players[CLOCK.seat];

  const nm=p? p.name : '';

  clockShow(Math.max(1, Math.ceil(remain/1000)), CLOCK.seat===MY_SEAT? 'Your turn' : nm);

  netAll({type:'clock', secs:Math.max(1, Math.ceil(remain/1000)), seat:CLOCK.seat, name:nm});

}

function clockExpire(){

  if(!CLOCK || CLOCK.expired) return;

  CLOCK.expired=true;

  banner('TIME HAS RUN OUT');

  log(`<b>Time has run out</b>: only what was already committed stands; the dance moves on.`, 'alert');

  netAll({type:'clockout', seat:CLOCK.seat});

  cancelOpenPrompts();

  rpcFailAll();

}

/* ---------- the reaction clock ----------

   Does the response clock govern this prompt? Only when clocks are enabled

   at all, the seat is human, and it is NOT that seat's turn. */

function reactionGoverned(p){

  return !READY_GATE && NET.role==='host' && NET.inGame && NET.cfg && NET.cfg.timer>0 &&

         p && p.isHuman && G && !G.over && G.players[G.turn]!==p &&

         (p.i===MY_SEAT || !!connForSeat(p.i));   // an away seat's prompts default instantly — no clock theater

}

/* Begin a response window for seat p around ONE prompt. Returns {end, ctl}:

   `end` must run when the prompt resolves (finally); `ctl` is handed to the

   local choose()/notice() so expiry can cancel exactly this prompt and no

   other. Prompts inside a reaction are sequential, so each gets its own

   fresh REACT_SECS — a responder actively playing cards keeps earning time;

   a responder sitting silent loses the window once. */

function reactBegin(p){

  if(!reactionGoverned(p)) return {end:()=>{}, ctl:null};

  REACT_DEPTH++;

  if(REACT_DEPTH===1) clockPause();

  const seat=p.i;

  const ctl={};

  REACT={seat, expired:false, cancels:[()=>{ if(ctl.cancel) ctl.cancel(); }],

         t:setTimeout(()=>reactExpire(seat), REACT_SECS*1000)};

  reactShow(seat);

  const end=()=>{

    if(REACT && REACT.seat===seat){ clearTimeout(REACT.t); REACT=null; }

    REACT_DEPTH=Math.max(0, REACT_DEPTH-1);

    if(REACT_DEPTH===0) clockResume();

  };

  return {end, ctl};

}

function reactExpire(seat){

  if(!REACT || REACT.seat!==seat || REACT.expired) return;

  REACT.expired=true;

  const p=G && G.players[seat];

  banner('THE MOMENT PASSES');

  if(p) log(`${fmtP(p)} lets the moment pass; the dance moves on.`, 'sys');

  if(seat===MY_SEAT){

    // close exactly this prompt: the registered choose-canceller, plus any

    // board prompt or armed dock the responder's window owned

    (REACT.cancels||[]).forEach(c=>{ try{ c(); }catch(e){} });

    if(HUMAN){ const h=HUMAN; HUMAN=null; try{ h.res({type:'end'}); }catch(e){} }

    if(PICK){ const pk=PICK; PICK=null; try{ pk.resolve(null); }catch(e){} try{ clearTileHighlights(); }catch(e){} $('#movehud').style.display='none'; }

    if(MOVE){ const mv=MOVE; MOVE=null; try{ mv.resolve('stop'); }catch(e){} try{ clearTileHighlights(); }catch(e){} $('#movehud').style.display='none'; }

  } else {

    rpcFail(seat);   // the pending RPC resolves null; the wrapper takes its default

    const c=connForSeat(seat);

    if(c){ try{ c.send({type:'clockout', seat}); }catch(e){} }   // close their dialog

  }

}

function reactShow(seat){

  const nm=(G && G.players[seat] && G.players[seat].name) || 'A rival';

  clockShow(REACT_SECS, seat===MY_SEAT? 'Respond now' : nm+' may respond');

  netAll({type:'clock', secs:REACT_SECS, seat, name:nm, react:true});

}

function rpcFailAll(){ for(const [id,e] of [...RPC_PENDING]){ RPC_PENDING.delete(id); e.res(null); } }

/* Resolve every open prompt on THIS client with its safe default. */

function cancelOpenPrompts(){

  if(HUMAN){ const h=HUMAN; HUMAN=null; try{ h.res({type:'end'}); }catch(e){} }

  if(PICK){ const pk=PICK; PICK=null; try{ pk.resolve(null); }catch(e){} try{ clearTileHighlights(); }catch(e){} }

  if(MOVE){ const mv=MOVE; MOVE=null; try{ mv.resolve('stop'); }catch(e){} try{ clearTileHighlights(); }catch(e){} $('#movehud').style.display='none'; }

  if(ACTIVE_CHOOSE){ const a=ACTIVE_CHOOSE; ACTIVE_CHOOSE=null; $('#modalwrap').style.display='none'; try{ a(null); }catch(e){} }

  flushPendingState();   // a sync deferred behind a now-cancelled prompt applies immediately

}

/* Countdown chip — everyone at the table watches the same clock. */

function clockShow(secs, label){

  clockHide();

  const el=$('#turnclock');

  const endsAt=Date.now()+secs*1000;

  const paint=()=>{

    const r=Math.max(0, Math.ceil((endsAt-Date.now())/1000));

    el.innerHTML=`<span class="cklabel">${label}</span> <b>${Math.floor(r/60)}:${String(r%60).padStart(2,'0')}</b>`;

    el.classList.toggle('low', r<=10);

    if(r<=0 && CLOCK_UI){ clearInterval(CLOCK_UI.iv); }

  };

  el.style.display='flex';

  CLOCK_UI={endsAt, iv:setInterval(paint, 250)};

  paint();

}

function clockHide(){

  if(CLOCK_UI){ clearInterval(CLOCK_UI.iv); CLOCK_UI=null; }

  const el=$('#turnclock'); if(el) { el.style.display='none'; el.classList.remove('low'); }

}

/* A remote player's wire is gone mid-game. The Fae take up their seat: the

   open prompt takes its default, and the seat flips to AI — immediately if

   the seat is not the one currently acting, otherwise at the next turn

   boundary (reconcileSeats), so no turn machinery changes species mid-flow.

   The seat token still reclaims it: rejoin flips it back the same way. */

function hostSeatAway(seat){

  rpcFail(seat);

  const p=G && G.players && G.players[seat];

  if(p && p.isHuman && !G.over){

    const nm=NET.names[seat]||p.name;

    if(G.turn!==seat){

      p.isHuman=false;

      log(`<b>${nm}</b> has lost the thread; the Fae dance their seat until they return.`, 'alert');

    } else {

      log(`<b>${nm}</b> has lost the thread mid-turn; this turn passes, and the Fae will dance their seat until they return.`, 'alert');

    }

  }

  renderHUD();

}

/* Turn-boundary reconciliation, both directions: a claimed seat with no wire

   is danced by the Fae; a claimed seat whose wire has returned goes back to

   its human, with a catch-up notice for hidden knowledge the seat gained

   while the Fae held its cards. */

function seatReclaimFlip(p){

  p.isHuman=true;

  log(`<b>${NET.names[p.i]||p.name}</b> takes their seat back from the Fae.`, 'sys');

}

async function seatCatchUp(p){

  let caught='The Fae danced your seat while you were away; The Telling on this screen begins anew from here.';

  if(p.knownStatus!=null) caught+=` The seat has glimpsed its own Radiance: it is <b>${p.knownStatus}</b>.`;

  const kh=Object.entries(p.knownHouses||{});

  if(kh.length) caught+=' Courts the seat has seen: '+kh.map(([i,h])=>`${G.players[+i].name} \u2014 ${HOUSE_BY_ID[h].name}`).join('; ')+'.';

  await seatNotice(p, 'While you were away', caught);

}

async function reconcileSeats(){

  if(NET.role!=='host' || !NET.inGame || !G || G.over) return;

  for(const p of G.players){

    if(p.i===MY_SEAT) continue;

    if(NET.names[p.i]==null) continue;          // never claimed by a human

    const wired=!!connForSeat(p.i);

    if(p.isHuman && !wired){

      p.isHuman=false;

      log(`The Fae take up <b>${NET.names[p.i]}</b>\u2019s seat until they return.`, 'sys');

    } else if(!p.isHuman && wired){

      seatReclaimFlip(p);

      await seatCatchUp(p);

    }

  }

  renderHUD();

}

/* Host: broadcast the live state, throttled — renderHUD fires on every change. */

function netSyncSoon(){

  if(NET.role!=='host' || !NET.inGame) return;

  const now=Date.now();

  if(now-NET.lastSync>140){ NET.lastSync=now; netStateAll(); }

  else if(!NET.syncT){ NET.syncT=setTimeout(()=>{ NET.syncT=null; NET.lastSync=Date.now(); netStateAll(); }, 150); }

}

{ const _rh=renderHUD; renderHUD=function(){ _rh.apply(this, arguments); netSyncSoon(); }; }

let logLocal=null;   // the raw, never-broadcast log — for lines only this client may see

{ const _log=log; logLocal=_log; log=function(html, cls){ _log.apply(this, arguments);

    if(NET.role==='host' && NET.inGame) netAll({type:'log', html, cls}); }; }

/* A PRIVATE Telling line: rendered only on p's own client. The broadcast log()

   above ships every line to every guest, so any text that names hidden

   information (your new Court, a peeked allegiance) must travel through here. */

function logTo(p, html, cls){

  if(!p || !p.isHuman) return;

  if(p.i===MY_SEAT){ (logLocal||log)(html, cls); return; }

  const c=connForSeat(p.i);

  if(c){ try{ c.send({type:'log', html, cls}); }catch(e){} }

}

{ const _banner=banner; banner=function(txt){ _banner.apply(this, arguments);

    if(NET.role==='host' && NET.inGame) netAll({type:'banner', txt}); }; }

/* ---------- lobby state & rendering ---------- */

function lobbyModel(){

  const seats=[];

  for(let i=0;i<NET.cfg.n;i++){

    const nm=NET.names[i];

    seats.push({i, name: nm || null});

  }

  return {cfg:NET.cfg, seats, names:NET.names};

}

function renderLobby(model){

  $('#lbcode').textContent=NET.code||'—';

  const c=model.cfg;

  $('#lbcfg').textContent=`${MODES[c.mode].name} · ${c.n} seats · ${c.timer===0?'No turn limit':'Turn limit '+c.timer+'s'}`;

  const box=$('#lbseats'); box.innerHTML='';

  model.seats.forEach(s=>{

    const d=document.createElement('div');

    d.className='lbseat'+(s.name?' human':'');

    d.innerHTML=`<span class="who">${s.name? s.name : '<i style="color:var(--ink2)">Open seat</i>'}</span>

      <span class="role">${s.i===0?'HOST':(s.name?'JOINED':'AI IF UNFILLED')}</span>`;

    box.appendChild(d);

  });

  if(NET.role==='host'){

    $('#lbstart').style.display='block';

    $('#lbstatus').textContent='Share the code. Empty seats will be danced by the Fae themselves.';

  } else {

    $('#lbstart').style.display='none';

    $('#lbstatus').textContent='Waiting for the host to start the dance…';

  }

  $('#roomcreate').style.display='none'; $('#roomjoin').style.display='none';

  $('#roomlobby').style.display='block';

}

function netTeardown(){

  try{ if(typeof reconClear==='function') reconClear(); }catch(e){}

  try{ if(NET.peer) NET.peer.destroy(); }catch(e){}

  NET.role=null; NET.peer=null; NET.conns=[]; NET.seatOf=new Map(); NET.names={}; NET.inGame=false; NET.pendingState=null;

  NET.tokens={}; NET.myToken=null; NET.myName=''; NET.booted=false;

}

/* Leaving guard: closing the tab mid-game gets a browser confirm — for the

   host that's five people's game; for a guest it's their seat. The peer is

   destroyed on pagehide only, so CANCELLING the dialog costs nothing (the

   old beforeunload destroy killed the table even when the user cancelled).

   Deliberate exits set LEAVING first and skip the nag. */

let LEAVING=false;

addEventListener('beforeunload', e=>{

  if(!LEAVING && NET.inGame && G && !G.over && (NET.role==='host' || NET.role==='guest')){

    e.preventDefault(); e.returnValue='';

  }

});

addEventListener('pagehide', ()=>{ try{ if(NET.peer) NET.peer.destroy(); }catch(e){} });

/* ---------- host ---------- */

/* The inbound-guest handler, shared by a fresh room and a resumed one. */

function hostAttachConnHandlers(peer){

  peer.on('connection', c=>{ try{

    netCrumb('A guest is connecting\u2026');

    wireIceSpy(c, 'host');

    c.on('data', msg=>hostHandle(c, msg));

    c.on('error', e=>netErr('conn', e));

    c.on('close', ()=>{ try{

      const seat=NET.seatOf.get(c);

      netCrumb('A guest connection closed'+(seat!=null?' (seat '+(seat+1)+')':''));

      if(seat!=null){ NET.seatOf.delete(c); NET.conns=NET.conns.filter(x=>x!==c);

        if(!NET.inGame){ delete NET.names[seat]; delete NET.tokens[seat];

          netAll({type:'lobby', model:lobbyModel()}); renderLobby(lobbyModel()); }

        else hostSeatAway(seat);

      }

    }catch(e){ netErr('close', e); } });

  }catch(e){ netErr('connection', e); } });

}

function createRoom(cfg, hostName){

  { const why=netUnavailable(); if(why){ $('#netstatus').textContent=why; return; } }

  NET.role='host'; NET.cfg=cfg; NET.code=mkCode(); NET.names={0: hostName||'Player 1'};

  $('#lbstatus').textContent='Opening the room…';

  netCrumb('Opening room '+NET.code+' ('+location.protocol+', PeerJS '+(typeof Peer!=='undefined'?'loaded':'MISSING')+')\u2026');

  try{ NET.peer=new Peer(peerIdFor(NET.code), iceConfig()); }

  catch(e){ netErr('open-room', e); $('#lbstatus').textContent='Could not open a room here: '+(e&&e.message||e); return; }

  NET.peer.on('open', id=>{ netCrumb('Room open on the broker: '+id);

    try{ renderLobby(lobbyModel()); }catch(e){ netErr('lobby', e); } });

  wireBrokerAutoReconnect(NET.peer, 'host');

  NET.peer.on('error', err=>{

    netCrumb('Peer error: '+err.type+' \u2014 '+(err.message||''));

    if(String(err.type)==='unavailable-id'){ NET.code=mkCode(); NET.peer.destroy(); createRoom(cfg, hostName); return; }

    try{ $('#lbstatus').textContent='Room error: '+err.type; }catch(_){}

  });

  hostAttachConnHandlers(NET.peer);

  renderLobby(lobbyModel());

}

/* Resume a crashed/refreshed host's game: same room CODE (so every guest's

   saved seat token still opens the door), full state restored, play resumed

   from the start of the interrupted turn. Seats reconnect through the normal

   rejoin machinery and flip back from the Fae as they arrive. */

function resumeHostGame(saved){

  { const why=netUnavailable(); if(why){ $('#netstatus').textContent=why; return; } }

  NET.role='host'; NET.cfg=saved.cfg; NET.code=saved.code;

  NET.names=saved.names||{}; NET.tokens=saved.tokens||{};

  MY_SEAT=0;

  let tries=0;

  const openPeer=()=>{

    try{ NET.peer=new Peer(peerIdFor(NET.code), iceConfig()); }

    catch(e){ netErr('resume', e); return; }

    NET.peer.on('open', id=>netCrumb('Room reopened on the broker: '+id));

    wireBrokerAutoReconnect(NET.peer, 'host');

    NET.peer.on('error', err=>{

      netCrumb('Peer error: '+err.type+' \u2014 '+(err.message||''));

      // the crashed session's id can linger on the broker for a short while —

      // the code MUST stay the same, so wait it out instead of re-rolling

      if(String(err.type)==='unavailable-id' && tries<5){

        tries++;

        crumbPush('The old room id is still fading from the broker; waiting ('+tries+'/5)\u2026');

        try{ NET.peer.destroy(); }catch(e){}

        setTimeout(openPeer, 3000);

        return;

      }

      try{ log(`\u26a0 The room could not be reopened (${err.type}).`, 'alert'); }catch(_){}

    });

    hostAttachConnHandlers(NET.peer);

  };

  openPeer();

  const mode=bootShell(saved.g.modeId);

  finishBootUI(mode);

  chatShow(true);

  NET.inGame=true; NET.booted=true;

  applyState(saved.g);

  refreshRulebook(G.mode);

  banner('THE DANCE RESUMES');

  log(`<b>The dance resumes</b> in room <b>${NET.code}</b>, from the start of the interrupted turn. Fae hold the empty seats; rejoined players take them back as they arrive (Rejoin on their main menu).`, 'sys');

  hostPersist();

  gameLoop();

}

function crumbPush(m){ try{ NET.crumbs.push({t:Date.now(), m:String(m)}); if(NET.crumbs.length>300) NET.crumbs.shift(); }catch(_){} }

function netCrumb(msg){

  crumbPush(msg);

  console.info('%c[Faerie Dances net] '+msg, 'color:#d8b45a');

  try{ const s=(NET.role==='guest')? $('#rjstatus') : $('#lbstatus');

    if(s && !NET.inGame) s.textContent=msg; }catch(_){}

}

function netErr(where, e){

  crumbPush('ERR '+where+': '+((e&&e.message)||e));

  console.error('[Faerie Dances net] '+where, e);

  try{ const s=$('#rjstatus'); if(s && s.offsetParent) s.textContent='Error in '+where+': '+(e&&e.message||e); }catch(_){}

  try{ if(NET.inGame) log(`\u26a0 Network error in ${where}: ${(e&&e.message)||e}`, 'alert'); }catch(_){}

}

/* ---------- diagnostics: everything a remote tester should paste back ----------

   Contains NO hidden game information (safe to share publicly): build, platform,

   connection facts, seat map, public game shape, and the crumb trail. */

function diagText(){

  const lines=[];

  lines.push('FAERIE DANCES DIAGNOSTICS \u2014 '+new Date().toISOString());

  try{ lines.push('build: '+($('#buildtag')? $('#buildtag').textContent : '?')); }catch(_){}

  try{ lines.push('page: '+location.protocol+' \u00b7 '+navigator.userAgent); }catch(_){}

  lines.push('peerjs: '+(typeof Peer!=='undefined'?'loaded':'MISSING')

    +' \u00b7 webrtc: '+((typeof RTCPeerConnection!=='undefined'||typeof webkitRTCPeerConnection!=='undefined')?'yes':'NO'));

  lines.push('role: '+(NET.role||'none')+' \u00b7 room: '+(NET.code||'\u2014')+' \u00b7 my seat: '+MY_SEAT

    +' \u00b7 inGame: '+NET.inGame+' \u00b7 forceWire: '+FORCE_WIRE);

  try{ const rl=parseRelay(relayRaw());

    lines.push('relay: '+(rl.length? rl.map(s=>String(s.urls)).join(' , ') : 'none configured')); }catch(_){}

  try{ if(NET.cfg) lines.push('cfg: '+JSON.stringify(NET.cfg)); }catch(_){}

  try{ lines.push('conns: '+NET.conns.length+' \u00b7 seated: ['+[...NET.seatOf.values()].join(',')+'] \u00b7 pending RPCs: '+RPC_PENDING.size); }catch(_){}

  try{ if(G) lines.push('game: '+G.mode.id+' \u00b7 '+G.players.length+' seats ('

    +G.players.map(p=>p.isHuman?'H':'ai').join(' ')+') \u00b7 turn seat '+G.turn+' \u00b7 round '+G.round+' \u00b7 over: '+G.over); }catch(_){}

  try{ lines.push('clock: '+(CLOCK? ((CLOCK.expired?'EXPIRED':'running')+' \u00b7 seat '+CLOCK.seat) : 'idle')); }catch(_){}

  lines.push('');

  lines.push('--- crumb trail (oldest first) ---');

  NET.crumbs.forEach(c=>{ try{ lines.push(new Date(c.t).toISOString().slice(11,19)+'  '+c.m); }catch(_){} });

  return lines.join('\n');

}

async function copyDiagnostics(){

  crumbPush('Diagnostics requested.');

  const text=diagText();

  let ok=false;

  try{ await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text); ok=true; }catch(_){}

  if(!ok){

    try{

      const ta=document.createElement('textarea');

      ta.value=text; ta.style.cssText='position:fixed;left:-9999px;top:0;';

      document.body.appendChild(ta); ta.select();

      ok=document.execCommand('copy');

      document.body.removeChild(ta);

    }catch(_){}

  }

  if(ok){

    banner('DIAGNOSTICS COPIED');

    try{ const s=(NET.role==='guest')? $('#rjstatus') : $('#lbstatus');

      if(s && !NET.inGame) s.textContent='Diagnostics copied \u2014 paste them to whoever is helping you.'; }catch(_){}

  } else {

    $('#diagtext').value=text;

    $('#diagbox').style.display='flex';

    try{ $('#diagtext').select(); }catch(_){}

  }

}

function hostHandle(c, msg){

 try{

  if(msg.type==='rpcReply'){

    const e=RPC_PENDING.get(msg.id);

    if(e){ RPC_PENDING.delete(msg.id); e.res(msg.value); }

    return;

  }

  if(msg.type==='interrupt'){

    const seat=NET.seatOf.get(c);

    if(seat==null || !NET.inGame || G.over) return;

    const p=G.players[seat];

    if(!p || !p.isHuman || !p.intrigues.includes(msg.name) || !ANYTIME.includes(msg.name)) return;

    if(INTERRUPT_BUSY){ try{ c.send({type:'log', html:'The moment has passed; another Magik is already in the air.', cls:'sys'}); }catch(e){} return; }

    (async()=>{

      INTERRUPT_BUSY=true;

      try{ await playActiveIntrigue(p, msg.name); }

      catch(e){ if(!(e instanceof GameOver)) console.error(e); }

      finally{ INTERRUPT_BUSY=false; renderHUD(); }

    })();

    return;

  }

  if(msg.type==='chat'){

    const seat=NET.seatOf.get(c);

    if(seat!=null && NET.inGame && typeof msg.text==='string') chatSpeak(seat, msg.text);

    return;

  }

  if(msg.type==='hello'){

    if(msg.v!==NET_VER){

      try{ c.send({type:'badver', need:NET_VER}); c.close(); }catch(e){}

      netCrumb('A guest with a mismatched game file was turned away (their protocol: '+(msg.v==null?'pre-versioning':msg.v)+').');

      return;

    }

    // REJOIN: a returning seat token reclaims its seat, even mid-game.

    if(msg.token){

      let rSeat=null;

      for(const s in NET.tokens){ if(NET.tokens[s]===msg.token){ rSeat=+s; break; } }

      if(rSeat!=null){

        // a stale half-dead conn may still hold the seat — evict it first

        for(const [oc,os] of [...NET.seatOf]){

          if(os===rSeat){ NET.seatOf.delete(oc); NET.conns=NET.conns.filter(x=>x!==oc); try{ oc.close(); }catch(e){} }

        }

        NET.conns.push(c); NET.seatOf.set(c, rSeat);

        if(msg.name && msg.name.trim()) NET.names[rSeat]=msg.name.trim().slice(0,14);

        try{ c.send({type:'seated', seat:rSeat, token:NET.tokens[rSeat], code:NET.code}); }catch(e){}

        netCrumb('\u201c'+NET.names[rSeat]+'\u201d has found the room again (seat '+(rSeat+1)+').');

        if(NET.inGame){

          // reclaim from the Fae BEFORE the boot snapshot, so their state is

          // already human — unless it is this seat's turn being danced right

          // now, in which case the turn boundary (reconcileSeats) flips it

          let reclaimed=false;

          if(G && !G.over){

            const rp=G.players[rSeat];

            if(rp && !rp.isHuman && G.turn!==rSeat){ seatReclaimFlip(rp); reclaimed=true; }

            else if(rp && !rp.isHuman) log(`<b>${NET.names[rSeat]}</b> has found the room again; the Fae finish this turn, then hand the seat back.`, 'sys');

            else log(`<b>${NET.names[rSeat]}</b> has found the thread again; their seat resumes.`, 'sys');

          }

          try{ c.send({type:'boot', modeId:NET.cfg.mode, seat:rSeat, names:NET.names, cfg:NET.cfg, g:snapG(rSeat), rejoin:true}); }catch(e){}

          if(reclaimed){ const rp=G.players[rSeat];

            setTimeout(()=>{ (async()=>{ try{ await seatCatchUp(rp); }catch(e){} })(); }, 600); }

          renderHUD();

        } else {

          netAll({type:'lobby', model:lobbyModel()});

          renderLobby(lobbyModel());

        }

        return;

      }

      // unknown token (the host restarted, or another room) — fresh-join rules apply

    }

    // FRESH JOIN: seat the guest at the next open seat (1..n-1)

    let seat=null;

    for(let i=1;i<NET.cfg.n;i++){ if(!NET.names[i]){ seat=i; break; } }

    if(seat==null || NET.inGame){ try{ c.send({type:'full'}); c.close(); }catch(e){} return; }

    NET.conns.push(c); NET.seatOf.set(c, seat);

    NET.names[seat]=((msg.name&&msg.name.trim())||('Player '+(seat+1))).slice(0,14);

    NET.tokens[seat]=mkToken();

    try{ c.send({type:'seated', seat, token:NET.tokens[seat], code:NET.code}); }catch(e){}

    netCrumb('Guest \u201c'+NET.names[seat]+'\u201d seated at seat '+(seat+1)+'.');

    netAll({type:'lobby', model:lobbyModel()});

    renderLobby(lobbyModel());

  }

 }catch(e){ netErr('hostHandle:'+(msg&&msg.type), e); }

}

async function startNetGame(){

  const cfg=NET.cfg;

  NET.inGame=true;

  netCrumb('The dance starts: '+NET.conns.length+' guest(s) at a '+cfg.n+'-seat table.');

  $('#roomlobby').style.display='none';

  MY_SEAT=0;

  const humanSeats=Object.keys(NET.names).map(Number).sort((a,b)=>a-b);

  bootGame(cfg.n, cfg.mode, {humanSeats, names:NET.names, quorum:cfg.quorum});

  NET.conns.forEach(c=>{

    const seat=NET.seatOf.get(c);

    try{ c.send({type:'boot', modeId:cfg.mode, seat, names:NET.names, cfg, g:snapG(seat)}); }catch(e){}

  });

  chatShow(true);

  logTo(mySeatP(), `You belong to the ${fmtH(G.players[MY_SEAT].house)}. Your Radiance faces away from you: dance blind, or find a way to glimpse it.`, 'sys');

  hostPersist();

  await readyGate();

  gameLoop();

}

/* Same table, fresh deal: the room, roster, tokens, and 3D scene all stay;

   only the game state is renewed. Away seats start human and the boundary

   reconciliation hands them to the Fae until their tokens return. */

async function hostRematch(){

  $('#reveal').style.display='none';

  const cfg=NET.cfg;

  const humanSeats=Object.keys(NET.names).map(Number).sort((a,b)=>a-b);

  newGame(cfg.n, cfg.mode, {humanSeats, names:NET.names, quorum:cfg.quorum});

  refreshRulebook(G.mode);

  syncBoard(); renderHUD();

  NET.conns.forEach(c=>{

    const seat=NET.seatOf.get(c);

    if(seat==null) return;

    try{ c.send({type:'boot', modeId:cfg.mode, seat, names:NET.names, cfg, g:snapG(seat), rematch:true}); }catch(e){}

  });

  banner('A NEW DANCE BEGINS');

  log(`<b>A new dance begins</b> at the same table. The cards are dealt afresh.`, 'sys');

  logTo(mySeatP(), `You belong to the ${fmtH(G.players[MY_SEAT].house)}. Your Radiance faces away from you: dance blind, or find a way to glimpse it.`, 'sys');

  hostPersist();

  await readyGate();

  gameLoop();

}

/* ---------- guest ---------- */

function joinRoom(code, name, token){

  { const why=netUnavailable(); if(why){ $('#rjstatus').textContent=why; return; } }

  try{ if(NET.peer) NET.peer.destroy(); }catch(e){}   // a retry must not stack Peers

  NET.conns=[]; NET.seatOf=new Map();

  NET.role='guest';

  NET.myName=(name||'').trim();

  $('#rjstatus').textContent='Seeking the room…';

  netCrumb('Seeking room '+code+' ('+location.protocol+', PeerJS '+(typeof Peer!=='undefined'?'loaded':'MISSING')+(token?', with seat token':'')+')\u2026');

  try{ NET.peer=new Peer(iceConfig()); }

  catch(e){ netErr('join-room', e); $('#rjstatus').textContent='Could not reach out from here: '+(e&&e.message||e); return; }

  wireBrokerAutoReconnect(NET.peer, 'guest');

  NET.peer.on('error', err=>{ netCrumb('Peer error: '+err.type+' \u2014 '+(err.message||''));

    try{ $('#rjstatus').textContent='Could not reach the room ('+err.type+'). Check the code.'; }catch(_){} });

  NET.peer.on('open', ()=>{ try{

    netCrumb('Connected to the broker; dialing the room\u2026');

    const c=NET.peer.connect(peerIdFor(code), {reliable:true});

    NET.conns=[c];

    wireIceSpy(c, 'guest');

    // Dead-air detector: on strict networks (symmetric NAT, some corporate/school

    // firewalls) the dial neither opens nor errors — the free PeerJS broker has

    // STUN but no TURN relay, so some pairs simply cannot connect directly.

    const dialT=setTimeout(()=>{ try{

      if(!c.open){

        netCrumb('No answer after 12s: wrong code, a closed room, or a network blocking the direct connection (no TURN relay on the free broker).');

        $('#rjstatus').textContent='No answer from the room. Check the code; if it\u2019s right, one of the two networks may be blocking a direct connection (try a phone hotspot).';

      }

    }catch(_){} }, 12000);

    c.on('open', ()=>{ clearTimeout(dialT); try{ netCrumb('Wire to the host is open.'); c.send({type:'hello', name, token: token||undefined, v:NET_VER}); $('#rjstatus').textContent='Knocking…'; }catch(e){ netErr('join', e); } });

    c.on('data', msg=>guestHandle(msg));

    c.on('error', e=>{ clearTimeout(dialT); netErr('conn', e); });

    c.on('close', ()=>{ clearTimeout(dialT); try{

      netCrumb('The wire to the host closed.');

      if(NET.inGame){ guestReconnect(); } else $('#rjstatus').textContent='The room closed.';

    }catch(e){ netErr('close', e); } });

  }catch(e){ netErr('dial', e); } });

}

/* Guest: the wire died mid-game. Try to walk back in with the seat token —

   a network blip or host-side hiccup heals itself; a genuinely departed host

   exhausts the attempts and says so. Any successful seated/boot clears the loop. */

let RECON=null;

function guestReconnect(){

  if(RECON) return;

  const saved=savedSeat();

  if(!saved || !saved.token){

    banner('The host has departed');

    log('<b>The connection to the host is lost.</b> Quit to the menu to begin anew.', 'alert');

    return;

  }

  banner('THE THREAD IS LOST');

  log('<b>The thread to the host is lost</b> — reaching for the room again\u2026', 'alert');

  let attempt=0;

  const dial=()=>{

    attempt++;

    if(attempt>20){

      clearInterval(RECON); RECON=null;

      banner('The host has departed');

      log('<b>The room cannot be found.</b> If the host returns (or resumes), use Rejoin from the main menu.', 'alert');

      return;

    }

    crumbPush('Rejoin attempt '+attempt+' of 20\u2026');

    joinRoom(saved.code, saved.name||NET.myName, saved.token);

  };

  RECON=setInterval(dial, 6000);

  dial();

}

function reconClear(){ if(RECON){ clearInterval(RECON); RECON=null; } }

function guestHandle(msg){

 try{

  if(msg.type==='badver'){

    reconClear();

    crumbPush('Version mismatch: the host speaks protocol '+msg.need+', this file speaks '+NET_VER+'.');

    $('#rjstatus').textContent='Your game file and the host\u2019s don\u2019t match. Everyone must use the SAME file \u2014 ask the host to send you theirs.';

    return;

  }

  if(msg.type==='full'){ $('#rjstatus').textContent='That table is full (or the dance has begun).'; return; }

  if(msg.type==='seated'){

    reconClear();

    MY_SEAT=msg.seat; NET.myToken=msg.token; NET.code=msg.code;

    saveSeat({code:msg.code, token:msg.token, seat:msg.seat, name:NET.myName, t:Date.now()});

    return;

  }

  if(msg.type==='lobby'){ NET.cfg=msg.model.cfg; NET.code=NET.code||$('#rjcode').value.toUpperCase(); NET.names=msg.model.names; renderLobby(msg.model); return; }

  if(msg.type==='boot'){

    reconClear();

    NET.inGame=true;

    MY_SEAT=msg.seat;

    crumbPush((msg.rejoin?'Rejoin boot':'Boot')+' received; seated at seat '+(msg.seat+1)+'.');

    try{ const s=savedSeat(); if(s){ s.t=Date.now(); saveSeat(s); } }catch(e){}

    if(NET.booted){

      // a boot into a LIVE UI: a healed wire, or the host dealt a rematch —

      // either way, never boot the 3D scene twice

      $('#roomlobby').style.display='none';

      $('#reveal').style.display='none';

      applyState(msg.g);

      refreshRulebook(G.mode);

      if(msg.rematch){

        banner('A NEW DANCE BEGINS');

        log(`<b>A new dance begins</b> at the same table. You belong to the ${fmtH(G.players[MY_SEAT].house)}. Your Radiance faces away from you.`, 'sys');

      } else {

        banner('THE THREAD IS FOUND');

        log('<b>The thread is found again</b>; the dance continues.', 'sys');

      }

      return;

    }

    NET.booted=true;

    $('#roomlobby').style.display='none';

    const mode=bootShell(msg.modeId);

    finishBootUI(mode);

    chatShow(true);

    applyState(msg.g);

    refreshRulebook(mode);

    if(msg.rejoin){ banner('THE THREAD IS FOUND'); }

    log(`You sit at seat ${msg.seat+1}. You belong to the ${fmtH(G.players[MY_SEAT].house)}. Your Radiance faces away from you: dance blind, or find a way to glimpse it.`, 'sys');

    return;

  }

  if(msg.type==='state'){ if(NET.inGame){ if(PICK||MOVE) NET.pendingState=msg.g; else applyState(msg.g); } return; }

  if(msg.type==='rpc'){ guestRPC(msg); return; }

  if(msg.type==='chatline'){ if(NET.inGame) chatLine(msg.html); return; }

  if(msg.type==='clock'){

    if(msg.secs>0) clockShow(msg.secs, msg.react

      ? (msg.seat===MY_SEAT? 'Respond now' : (msg.name||'A rival')+' may respond')

      : (msg.seat===MY_SEAT? 'Your turn' : msg.name));

    else clockHide();

    return;

  }

  if(msg.type==='clockout'){ clockHide(); cancelOpenPrompts(); return; }

  if(msg.type==='reveal'){

    if(NET.inGame){

      clockHide();

      $('#revsub').innerHTML=msg.sub + '<br><i class="small" style="color:var(--ink2);">The host may begin a new dance at this table \u2014 stay, and you\u2019ll be seated in it.</i>';

      $('#revrows').innerHTML=msg.rows;
