      const btn=$('#revbtn');

      btn.textContent='Leave the Table';

      btn.onclick=()=>{ LEAVING=true; try{ localStorage.removeItem(SEAT_KEY); }catch(e){} location.reload(); };

      $('#reveal').style.display='flex';

    }

    return;

  }

  if(msg.type==='log'){ if(NET.inGame) log(msg.html, msg.cls); return; }   // guest role: no re-broadcast

  if(msg.type==='banner'){ if(NET.inGame) banner(msg.txt); return; }

 }catch(e){ netErr('guestHandle:'+(msg&&msg.type), e); }

}

/* Guest: run the host's prompt through this client's own UI, send the answer back. */

/* The prompt dispatcher a remote seat runs against its own UI. Shared verbatim

   by the FORCE_WIRE loopback (loopRPC), so the loopback exercises the exact

   code a real guest would — `send` is the only thing that differs. */

async function guestRPCCore(msg, send){

  const pl=msg.payload||{};

  try{

    if(msg.kind==='choose'){

      const opts=(pl.opts||[]).map((o,i)=>({label:o.label, sub:o.sub, cls:o.cls, value:i}));

      const idx=await choose(pl.title, pl.desc, opts, pl.cls);

      send(idx);

    } else if(msg.kind==='pickStone'){

      const legal=new Set(pl.legal||[]);

      const r=await pickStoneAsync(pl.msg, ud=>legal.has(ud.track+'|'+ud.step));

      send(r||null);

    } else if(msg.kind==='pickDest'){

      const r=await pickDestinationAsync(pl.fromTr);

      send(r||null);

    } else if(msg.kind==='notice'){

      await notice(pl.title, pl.html); send(1);

    } else if(msg.kind==='arm'){

      const ev=await armHuman(pl.kinds||['honor','skip','intrigue']);

      send({type:ev.type, v:ev.v, name:ev.name});

    } else if(msg.kind==='move'){

      const owner=G.players[pl.ownerSeat];

      const r=await localMoveChoice(owner, pl.points, pl.lockCi, {single:pl.single, noForfeit:pl.guided});

      send(r==='stop' ? 'stop' : r);

    } else send(null);

  }catch(e){ send(null); }

  finally{ flushPendingState(); }

}

async function guestRPC(msg){

  const send=v=>{ try{ NET.conns[0].send({type:'rpcReply', id:msg.id, value:v}); }catch(e){} };

  return guestRPCCore(msg, send);

}

/* ---------- Chat ----------

   A standalone minimizable chat box. Lines travel their own pipe: guests send

   raw text to the host; the host stamps the speaker from its OWN seat map

   (never trusting the wire), escapes the text, renders, and relays the built

   line to every guest. */

let CHAT_UNREAD=0;

function escapeChat(s){ return String(s).slice(0,200).replace(/[&<>"']/g, c=>({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'}[c])); }

function chatLine(lineHtml){

  const body=$('#chatbody');

  const p=document.createElement('p');

  p.innerHTML=lineHtml;

  body.appendChild(p);

  body.scrollTop=body.scrollHeight;

  if($('#chatpanel').style.display!=='flex'){

    CHAT_UNREAD++;

    const u=$('#chatunread'); u.textContent=CHAT_UNREAD; u.style.display='inline-block';

  }

}

function chatSpeak(seat, text){   // host-side authority

  const p=G && G.players && G.players[seat];

  if(!p) return;

  const t=escapeChat(text); if(!t.trim()) return;

  const line=`<b style="color:${p.color}">${escapeChat(NET.names[seat]||p.name)}:</b> ${t}`;

  chatLine(line);

  netAll({type:'chatline', html:line});

}

function sendChat(){

  const inp=$('#chatinput');

  const text=(inp.value||'').trim();

  inp.value='';

  if(!text || !NET.inGame) return;

  if(NET.role==='host') chatSpeak(MY_SEAT, text);

  else if(NET.conns[0]){ try{ NET.conns[0].send({type:'chat', text}); }catch(e){} }

}

function chatShow(open){

  $('#chattoggle').style.display='block';

  if(open){ setPanel('chatpanel','chattoggle',true,'flex');

    CHAT_UNREAD=0; $('#chatunread').style.display='none'; }

}

/* ---- corner flourishes: the board's tendril language, in the panel's top corners ---- */

(function(){

  const cv=$('#cornerfL'); if(!cv || !cv.getContext) return;

  const g=cv.getContext('2d');

  const gold=(a)=>`rgba(216,180,90,${a})`, pale=(a)=>`rgba(245,230,184,${a})`;

  g.lineCap='round';

  function wisp(x,y,r,a){

    const rg=g.createRadialGradient(x,y,0,x,y,r);

    rg.addColorStop(0,pale(a)); rg.addColorStop(1,pale(0));

    g.fillStyle=rg; g.beginPath(); g.arc(x,y,r,0,Math.PI*2); g.fill();

  }

  function leaf(x,y,len,ang,a){

    g.save(); g.translate(x,y); g.rotate(ang);

    g.fillStyle=gold(a);

    g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(0,0);

    g.quadraticCurveTo(len*0.5,-len*0.34, len,0);

    g.quadraticCurveTo(len*0.5, len*0.34, 0,0);

    g.fill(); g.restore();

  }

  function curl(x,y,r,turns,dir,a,w){

    g.strokeStyle=gold(a); g.shadowColor=gold(.55); g.shadowBlur=6;

    let ang=Math.PI, rad=r;

    g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(x+Math.cos(ang)*rad, y+Math.sin(ang)*rad*dir);

    const steps=Math.floor(26*turns);

    for(let i=1;i<=steps;i++){

      ang+=turns*2*Math.PI/steps; rad*=0.94;

      g.lineWidth=Math.max(1,w*rad/r);

      g.lineTo(x+Math.cos(ang)*rad, y+Math.sin(ang)*rad*dir);

    }

    g.stroke(); g.shadowBlur=0;

  }

  function branch(x,y,ang,len,a,tip){

    g.strokeStyle=gold(a); g.shadowColor=gold(.4); g.shadowBlur=4;

    g.lineWidth=1.9;

    const ex=x+Math.cos(ang)*len,          ey=y+Math.sin(ang)*len;

    const mx=x+Math.cos(ang-0.55)*len*0.6, my=y+Math.sin(ang-0.55)*len*0.6;

    g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(x,y); g.quadraticCurveTo(mx,my,ex,ey); g.stroke();

    g.shadowBlur=0;

    if(tip==='curl') curl(ex,ey,len*0.4,1.3, ang<0? -1:1, a*.9, 2.2);

    else { leaf(ex,ey,len*0.55,ang,a*.85); leaf(ex-4,ey+3,len*0.4,ang+0.85,a*.6); }

  }

  /* one three-strand braided arm along +x from the corner; the second arm is

     this same drawing mirrored across the diagonal (running down the side) */

  function arm(){

    const strands=[

      {phase:0.00, amp:19, alpha:.8,  w:4.2},

      {phase:0.33, amp:24, alpha:.55, w:3.0},

      {phase:0.66, amp:15, alpha:.42, w:2.3},

    ];

    const paths=strands.map(s=>{

      const pts=[];

      for(let i=0;i<=48;i++){

        const t=i/48, taper=1-0.55*t;

        const x=42+t*400;

        const y=46 + Math.sin((t*2.4+s.phase)*Math.PI*2)*s.amp*taper;

        pts.push([x,y,taper]);

      }

      for(let i=1;i<pts.length;i++){

        g.strokeStyle=gold(s.alpha); g.shadowColor=gold(.5); g.shadowBlur=5;

        g.lineWidth=Math.max(1, s.w*pts[i][2]);

        g.beginPath(); g.moveTo(pts[i-1][0],pts[i-1][1]); g.lineTo(pts[i][0],pts[i][1]); g.stroke();

      }

      g.shadowBlur=0;

      return pts;

    });

    const spots=[ [0,8,-1,'leaf'], [1,16,1,'curl'], [2,24,-1,'leaf'], [0,32,1,'curl'], [1,40,-1,'leaf'] ];

    spots.forEach(([si,pi,side,tip],k)=>{

      const [x,y]=paths[si][pi];

      branch(x,y, side*(0.95+0.1*(k%3)), 30-k*3, .62-0.05*k, tip);

    });

    const [tx,ty]=paths[0][46];

    curl(tx,ty,15,1.4,1,.55,2.4);

    wisp(210,40,14,.4);

  }

  arm();

  g.save(); g.transform(0,1,1,0,0,0); arm(); g.restore();   // second arm, down the side

  curl(58,58,36,1.8,1,.9,4.6);                              // the corner root bloom

  wisp(58,58,34,.5);

  /* right corner: the same art, mirrored by CSS */

  const cr=$('#cornerfR');

  if(cr && cr.getContext) cr.getContext('2d').drawImage(cv,0,0);

})();

/* A refresh or browser restart can walk back into a live room: the saved seat

   token drives a one-click rejoin for up to two hours. */

(function(){

  const s=savedSeat();

  if(s && s.t && Date.now()-s.t < 2*3600*1000){

    const b=$('#rejoinbtn');

    b.textContent='Rejoin '+s.code;

    b.style.display='inline-block';

    b.onclick=()=>{ $('#roomjoin').style.display='block'; $('#roomcreate').style.display='none';

      $('#rjcode').value=s.code; if(s.name) $('#rjname').value=s.name;

      joinRoom(s.code, s.name||'', s.token); };

  }

  const h=savedHost();

  if(h && h.t && Date.now()-h.t < 6*3600*1000){

    const b=$('#resumebtn');

    b.textContent='Resume '+h.code;

    b.title='Reopen your hosted game from the start of the interrupted turn';

    b.style.display='inline-block';

    b.onclick=()=>resumeHostGame(h);

  }

})();

  b.onclick=()=>{ b.closest('.mproom').style.display='none'; netTeardown(); };

});

};

const PROLOGUE_PAGES=[

  { title:'The Setting Dusk', html:`

    <p>It is almost Midsummer night, and the soft dusk is turning to a deep, starry twilight. From the edges of the wood, a barely perceptible music begins to rise, drifting like pollen through the air. It is an ancient melody to an ancient dance felt through the air before the ears.</p>

    <p>Into the sacred glade step the delegates of the four great courts: a Fae of the mountain peaks holds a flute of black obsidian; a Fae of the golden meadows carries a bow-harp of dandelion silk; from the deep forest comes a Fae with a birch-bark hoop drum; and from the winding river comes a Fae with pipes of hollowed reed. Together, they gather before the council of the High Fae.</p>` },

  { title:'The High Fae', html:`

    <p>The High Fae sit in awful majesty, possessing terrible and wondrous powers that make the very air shimmer with enchantment and mystery. They are beings of ethereal grace and breathtaking beauty, glowing with a light older than the trees. When they speak, their voices are both the soft rustling of leaves and the thunder of mighty waterfalls.</p>

    <p>They announce that it has come time for the Midsummer Dance. They make their decree:</p>

    <p class="decree">“To the noble Fae whose Radiance burns brightest in the Court in which the Wisps have thronged, to that Fae is granted a True Name with which they may join the High Council.”</p>` },

  { title:'The Dance of the Glamours', html:`

    <p>And so the noble Fae of the four courts twist and twirl, but do not dance in their true forms. Using ancient, carved runes to guide their steps, they split their presence into two shimmering Glamours. These glowing reflections glide gracefully through the ancient paths of the Faerie Mounds, the starlit circles of the Faerie Rings, and the secret borders of the Faerie Forts. Carrying them across the misty spaces of the glade are the mystical Faerie Bridges, spans of pale light that glimmer in and out of sight with the shifting of the twilight.</p>` },

  { title:'The Gathering Wisps', html:`

    <p>As the dance weaves its intricate patterns, the magic of the glade pays tribute. Floating out of the high crags, the wildflower fields, the deep woods, and the running waters, luminous will-o’-the-wisps begin to glimmer.</p>

    <p>As the Fae complete their dances, they unveil wisps in courts of their choosing to honor the grace and power of the High Fae. In return, the High Fae grant favors for unveiling the hidden wisps.</p>` },

  { title:'Trickery and Artifice', html:`

    <p>Yet as the music swells, the Glamours lose sight of their own Radiance, even while clearly seeing those of their rivals. They shift, deceive, trick, and use the artifice of Faerie Magik to ensure they gleam brighter than the rivals in the most brilliant court, desperately fighting to attain a Name from the High Fae.</p>` },

  { title:'The Call of the True Name', html:`

    <p>And so begins the Midsummer Dance, awaiting the Call of the True Name…</p>` },

];

let PROLOG_I=0;

function prologShow(i){

  PROLOG_I=Math.max(0, Math.min(PROLOGUE_PAGES.length-1, i));

  const pg=PROLOGUE_PAGES[PROLOG_I];

  $('#prologimg').src=PROLOG_IMGS[PROLOG_I];

  $('#prologimg').alt=pg.title;

  $('#prologtitle').textContent=pg.title;

  $('#prologtext').innerHTML=pg.html;

  $('#prologdots').innerHTML=PROLOGUE_PAGES.map((_,k)=>'<span class="'+(k===PROLOG_I?'on':'')+'"></span>').join('');

  $('#prologprev').style.visibility=PROLOG_I? 'visible' : 'hidden';

  $('#prolognext').textContent = PROLOG_I===PROLOGUE_PAGES.length-1 ? 'Join the Dance' : 'Next \u203a';

  $('#prologue').querySelector('.panel').scrollTop=0;

}

$('#prologuebtn').onclick=()=>{ $('#prologue').style.display='flex'; prologShow(0); };

$('#prologclose').onclick=()=>{ $('#prologue').style.display='none'; };

$('#prologprev').onclick=()=>prologShow(PROLOG_I-1);

$('#prolognext').onclick=()=>{

  if(PROLOG_I===PROLOGUE_PAGES.length-1) $('#prologue').style.display='none';

  else prologShow(PROLOG_I+1);

};

addEventListener('keydown', e=>{

  if($('#prologue').style.display!=='flex') return;

  if(e.key==='ArrowRight') $('#prolognext').click();

  else if(e.key==='ArrowLeft') prologShow(PROLOG_I-1);

  else if(e.key==='Escape') $('#prologue').style.display='none';

});

$('#beginMasq').onclick=()=>joinDance('masquerade');

$('#beginMid').onclick=()=>joinDance('midsummer');

$('#tutMasq').onclick=()=>runMasqTutorial();

$('#tutMid').onclick=()=>runMidTutorial();

/* ============================================================

   Tutorial — three acts: tour the board, practice, scripted Call

   ============================================================ */

const TUT = { steps:null, i:0, resolveContinue:null };

/* position the four shades + ring to spotlight a target rect (or center it) */

function tutSpotlight(el){

  const mask=$('#tutmask'), ring=mask.querySelector('.ring');

  const pad=8;

  let r;

  if(el && el.getBoundingClientRect){

    const b=el.getBoundingClientRect();

    if(b.width===0 && b.height===0){ el=null; }

    else r={left:b.left-pad, top:b.top-pad, right:b.right+pad, bottom:b.bottom+pad};

  }

  const W=innerWidth, H=innerHeight;

  const s=n=>mask.querySelector(`.shade[data-s="${n}"]`);

  if(!el || !r){

    // no target: dim whole screen, hide ring

    s('top').style.cssText='left:0;top:0;width:100%;height:100%;';

    ['bottom','left','right'].forEach(n=>s(n).style.cssText='width:0;height:0;');

    ring.style.opacity='0';

    return null;

  }

  ring.style.opacity='1';

  ring.style.left=r.left+'px'; ring.style.top=r.top+'px';

  ring.style.width=(r.right-r.left)+'px'; ring.style.height=(r.bottom-r.top)+'px';

  s('top').style.cssText=`left:0;top:0;width:100%;height:${Math.max(0,r.top)}px;`;

  s('bottom').style.cssText=`left:0;top:${r.bottom}px;width:100%;height:${Math.max(0,H-r.bottom)}px;`;

  s('left').style.cssText=`left:0;top:${r.top}px;width:${Math.max(0,r.left)}px;height:${r.bottom-r.top}px;`;

  s('right').style.cssText=`left:${r.right}px;top:${r.top}px;width:${Math.max(0,W-r.right)}px;height:${r.bottom-r.top}px;`;

  return r;

}

/* place the caption bubble near the spotlit rect without overflowing.

   `side` ('left'|'right') applies when the spotlight covers the whole board:

   the bubble sits at that screen edge — pick the side OPPOSITE the action.

   Defaults to 'right' (board action tends to sit left/centre). */

function tutPlaceBubble(r, side){

  const bub=$('#tutbubble');

  bub.style.display='block';

  const bw=bub.offsetWidth, bh=bub.offsetHeight, gap=16, W=innerWidth, H=innerHeight;

  let left, top;

  if(!r){ // centered

    left=(W-bw)/2; top=(H-bh)/2;

  } else if((r.right-r.left) > W*0.85 && (r.bottom-r.top) > H*0.85){

    // full-board spotlight: park at the edge opposite the action

    top=(H-bh)/2;

    left = side==='left' ? gap : W-bw-gap;

  } else {

    // prefer below, else above, else beside

    if(r.bottom+gap+bh < H){ top=r.bottom+gap; left=r.left+(r.right-r.left)/2-bw/2; }

    else if(r.top-gap-bh > 0){ top=r.top-gap-bh; left=r.left+(r.right-r.left)/2-bw/2; }

    else { top=(H-bh)/2; left=(r.right+gap+bw<W)? r.right+gap : Math.max(gap, r.left-gap-bw); }

  }

  left=Math.max(gap, Math.min(W-bw-gap, left));

  top=Math.max(gap, Math.min(H-bh-gap, top));

  bub.style.left=left+'px'; bub.style.top=top+'px';

}

function tutShow(step){

  document.querySelectorAll('.tut-raise').forEach(el=>el.classList.remove('tut-raise'));

  $('#tutmask').style.display='block';

  let r;

  if(step.focusSel){

    // Dim everything; lift the referenced fixed-position elements above the mask, glowing.

    tutSpotlight(null);

    step.focusSel.forEach(s=>{ const el=$(s); if(el) el.classList.add('tut-raise'); });

    r=null;

  } else {

    r = tutSpotlight(step.target ? step.target() : null);

  }

  $('#tuteyebrow').textContent = step.eyebrow || 'Tutorial';

  $('#tuttitle').textContent = step.title || '';

  $('#tuttext').innerHTML = step.body || '';

  $('#tutstep').textContent = (TUT.steps && TUT.steps.length>1) ? `Step ${TUT.i+1} of ${TUT.steps.length}` : '';

  $('#tutback').style.visibility = TUT.i>0 ? 'visible' : 'hidden';

  $('#tutnext').style.display='';

  $('#tutnext').textContent = step.nextLabel || 'Next';

  tutPlaceBubble(r, step.side);

}

function tutHideOverlay(){

  document.querySelectorAll('.tut-raise').forEach(el=>el.classList.remove('tut-raise'));

  $('#tutmask').style.display='none';

  $('#tutbubble').style.display='none';

}

/* ---- Act 1 step list (built at runtime so targets resolve to live nodes) ---- */

/* spotlight target spanning several elements at once (e.g. the panel buttons) */

function unionTarget(sels){

  return ()=>({ getBoundingClientRect(){

    let r=null;

    sels.forEach(s=>{

      const el=document.querySelector(s); if(!el) return;

      const b=el.getBoundingClientRect(); if(b.width===0 && b.height===0) return;

      if(!r) r={left:b.left,top:b.top,right:b.right,bottom:b.bottom};

      else { r.left=Math.min(r.left,b.left); r.top=Math.min(r.top,b.top);

             r.right=Math.max(r.right,b.right); r.bottom=Math.max(r.bottom,b.bottom); }

    });

    if(!r) return {left:0,top:0,right:0,bottom:0,width:0,height:0};

    return {left:r.left,top:r.top,right:r.right,bottom:r.bottom,width:r.right-r.left,height:r.bottom-r.top};

  }});

}

/* run one caption segment (Next/Back within it) */

function tutSeg(steps){

  TUT.steps=steps; TUT.i=0;

  return new Promise(res=>{ TUT.done=res; tutShow(steps[0]); });

}

$('#tutnext').onclick=()=>{

  if(!TUT.steps) return;

  if(TUT.i < TUT.steps.length-1){ TUT.i++; tutShow(TUT.steps[TUT.i]); }

  else { TUT.steps=null; tutHideOverlay(); if(TUT.done){ const d=TUT.done; TUT.done=null; d(); } }

};

$('#tutback').onclick=()=>{

  if(!TUT.steps || TUT.i===0) return;

  TUT.i--; tutShow(TUT.steps[TUT.i]);

};

addEventListener('resize',()=>{

  if(TUT.steps){

    const st=TUT.steps[TUT.i];

    if(st.focusSel) tutPlaceBubble(null);

    else { const r=tutSpotlight(st.target?st.target():null); tutPlaceBubble(r, st.side); }

  }

});

/* a non-blocking hint: shows the bubble with NO mask and NO button, so the

   player can act immediately. Returns a closer. Unanchored hints pin to the

   bottom corner OPPOSITE the action (`side`, default 'right'). (#4) */

function tutHint(title, html, anchorFn, side){

  $('#tutmask').style.display='none';

  $('#tuteyebrow').textContent='Your move';

  $('#tuttitle').textContent=title;

  $('#tuttext').innerHTML=html;

  $('#tutstep').textContent='';

  $('#tutback').style.visibility='hidden';

  $('#tutnext').style.display='none';

  let r=null;

  if(anchorFn){ const el=anchorFn(); if(el){ const b=el.getBoundingClientRect();

    if(b.width||b.height) r={left:b.left,top:b.top,right:b.right,bottom:b.bottom}; } }

  tutPlaceBubble(r);

  if(!r){ // pin to a bottom corner, clear of the Glade (top-centre) and the movement HUD

    const bub=$('#tutbubble');

    bub.style.left = (side==='left' ? 16 : Math.max(16, innerWidth - bub.offsetWidth - 16)) + 'px';

    bub.style.top = Math.max(80, innerHeight - bub.offsetHeight - 190)+'px';

  }

  return ()=>{ $('#tutnext').style.display=''; tutHideOverlay(); };

}

/* ---------------- hands-on checkpoints (#2) ---------------- */

async function tutDoerFirstStep(me){

  // Part 1: play a specific rune, for real.

  TUT.forceRune=3; renderHUD();

  const closeRune=tutHint('Play a rune',

    'Time to dance. <b>Click your 3 rune</b>, the only one lit. (In a real turn any rune in hand works.)',

    ()=>$('#hand'));

  await armHuman(['honor']);

  closeRune();

  TUT.forceRune=null;

  me.hand.splice(me.hand.indexOf(3),1); me.discard.push(3);

  log(`${fmtP(me)} dances a <b>3</b>.`);

  renderHUD();

  // Part 2: spend the steps by dragging.

  const closeDrag=tutHint('Dance your steps',

    'You have <b>3 steps</b>. <b>Click, tap, or drag a Glamour</b>: its reachable stones light up. Send it to one. You may split the steps between both Glamours. (This bubble drags too, if it\u2019s in your way.)');

  await allocateHuman(me, me, 3, {noForfeit:true});

  closeDrag();

}

Everything else holds: same Courts, same Radiance, same Call at 5 Wisps.` },

function midStepsFourthPath(){

Look closely: its stones <b>glow pale blue</b>. Those are <b>Conjured Stones</b>, and they\u2019re the core of what\u2019s new.` },

      body:`Every stone on the board has <b>two sides</b>: a plain side and a conjured side. The Faerie Bridge starts full of conjured ones, but <i>any</i> stone can flip either way, and conjured stones can be <b>picked up and moved</b>. Watch what that does\u2026` },

  ];

}

/* Flip demo: a rival tumbles. Ferry demo: a rider travels with the stone. */

async function midDemoStones(r1, r2){

  // --- THE FLIP ---

  r1.cands[0]={track:'Faerie Bridge', steps:2}; syncBoard();

  await tutSeg([{ target:()=>$('#c3d'), eyebrow:'Watch \u00b7 The Flip', title:'Flipping a stone',

    body:`${fmtP(r1)}\u2019s Glamour is standing on a conjured stone of the Faerie Bridge. A flip turns any stone to its other side, and anyone standing on it\u2026`,

    nextLabel:'Flip it \u2192' }]);

  const st=G.steps['Faerie Bridge'][1];

  st.c=false; tumbleFae('Faerie Bridge',2); syncBoard();

  await tutSeg([{ target:()=>$('#c3d'), eyebrow:'Watch \u00b7 The Flip', title:'The Tumble',

    body:`\u2026<b>tumbles from the dance</b>, back to waiting, and must start over. ${fmtP(r1)} just lost their whole climb. Flips are Midsummer\u2019s keenest mischief.` }]);

  st.c=true;   // restore the conjured side

  // --- THE FERRY ---

  r2.cands[0]={track:'Faerie Bridge', steps:3}; syncBoard();

  await tutSeg([{ target:()=>$('#c3d'), eyebrow:'Watch \u00b7 The Ferry', title:'Moving a Conjured Stone',

    body:`Now the gentler trick. ${fmtP(r2)}\u2019s Glamour stands on a conjured stone. A conjured stone can be <b>lifted and carried to the outer end of any dance</b>, and its dancers <b>ride along, unharmed</b>. Watch\u2026`,

    nextLabel:'Move it \u2192' }]);

  await ferryConjured(G.players[0], 'Faerie Bridge', 3, 'Faerie Ring');

  await tutSeg([{ target:()=>$('#c3d'), side:'left', eyebrow:'Watch \u00b7 The Ferry', title:'Carried to a new beginning',

    body:`The stone, and ${fmtP(r2)}\u2019s Glamour with it, now sits at the <b>start of the Faerie Ring</b>. No tumble, but all their progress on the old dance is gone: a ferry <b>relocates and resets</b>.<br><br><b>Remember the pair:</b> a <b>flip punishes</b> (a tumble off the dance); a <b>move relocates</b> (a ride to a new dance\u2019s start).` }]);

  // restore the pristine board: send the demo dancers home FIRST, then undo the ferry

  r1.cands[0]={track:null,steps:0};

  r2.cands[0]={track:null,steps:0};

  G.steps['Faerie Ring'].shift();                 // remove the ferried stone from the Ring's outer end

  G.steps['Faerie Bridge'].splice(2,0,{c:true});   // put a conjured stone back at Faerie Bridge position 3

  syncBoard();

}

function midStepsRunePowers(){

  return [

    { target:()=>$('#hand'), eyebrow:'What\u2019s New', title:'Rune powers',

      body:`Your runes now carry <b>powers</b>: see the little corner icons (hover any of them for its text). The low runes act; the higher runes choose:<br><br>

      <b>1</b>: Flip a stone, then move 1. <i>The flip is required.</i><br>

      <b>2</b>: Move a Conjured Stone, then move 2. <i>Also required (waived only if no conjured stones exist).</i><br>

      <b>3</b>: Move 3, <b>or instead</b> discard your Court, draw a new Court.<br>

      <b>4</b>: Move 4, <b>or instead</b> discard your Radiance, draw a new Radiance, <i>unseen by you</i>.<br>

      <b>5</b>: Move 5, <b>or instead</b> force a rival to discard their Court or Radiance and draw a new one.<br>

      <b>6</b>: Move 6, <b>or instead</b> lure a Wisp.` },

    { target:unionTarget(['#hand .honor[data-v="1"]','#hand .honor[data-v="2"]']), eyebrow:'Strategy', title:'The stone runes: 1 & 2',

      body:`These reshape the ground itself, and your rivals with it. A <b>flip</b> punishes: tumble a rival off their climb at the worst possible moment. A <b>move</b> relocates: carry a stone, and whoever rides it, back to a dance\u2019s beginning. Both are required, but the target is always yours to choose.` },

    { target:unionTarget(['#hand .honor[data-v="3"]','#hand .honor[data-v="4"]']), eyebrow:'Strategy', title:'The gamble runes: 3 & 4',

      body:`Each trades its steps for a different bet. The <b>3</b> gambles on <b>Court</b>: draw a new card in hopes of landing somewhere stronger, and as a bonus, whatever rivals had deduced about your loyalties goes stale. The <b>4</b> gambles on <b>Radiance</b>: draw a new card in hopes of a higher number. No muddying there: the new card faces the table like the old one, so your rivals see exactly what you drew, and you do not.` },

    { target:unionTarget(['#hand .honor[data-v="5"]','#hand .honor[data-v="6"]']), eyebrow:'Strategy', title:'The call runes: 5 & 6',

      body:`These are the endgame\u2019s cruellest mischief. <b>Lure</b> a Wisp out of a Court just before a rival Calls there, and the Call dies unspoken. Or <b>force</b> a poised rival to redraw their Radiance; even a lucky draw leaves them blind, and few dare Call blind. Spent precisely, these runes stop a True Name from ever being spoken.`,

      nextLabel:'Try a power \u2192' },

  ];

}

/* Hands-on: play the 1 for real — mandatory flip, then the step. */

async function midDoerRuneOne(me){

  TUT.forceRune=1; renderHUD();

  const closeRune=tutHint('Play your 1 rune',

    'Click your <b>1</b>, the only rune lit. Its power fires first: you <b>must flip a stone</b>.',

    ()=>$('#hand'));

  await armHuman(['honor']);

  closeRune();

  TUT.forceRune=null;

  // Mandatory flip, guided: any stone is legal. Use the real picker.

  const closeFlip=tutHint('Flip a stone',

    'Click <b>any stone</b> to flip it. (An empty one is harmless; in a real game you\u2019d aim for a stone under a rival.)');

  let fp=null;

  while(!fp){ fp = await pickStoneAsync('Click any stone to flip it', ()=>true); }

  closeFlip();

  const st=G.steps[fp.tr][fp.k-1];

  st.c=!st.c;

  const vict=tumbleFae(fp.tr, fp.k);

  log(`${fmtP(me)} flips step ${fp.k} of the <b>${fp.tr}</b> to ${st.c?'Conjured':'Regular'}.`);

  vict.forEach(q=>log(`The stone flips, and ${fmtP(q)}\u2019s Glamour tumbles!`, 'alert'));

  syncBoard(); renderHUD();

  me.hand.splice(me.hand.indexOf(1),1); me.discard.push(1);

  log(`${fmtP(me)} dances a <b>1</b>.`);

  renderHUD();

  const closeDrag=tutHint('Now your step', 'The flip is done. Now <b>click, tap, or drag a Glamour</b> onto a lit stone to spend your 1 step.');

  await allocateHuman(me, me, 1, {noForfeit:true});

  closeDrag();

}

function midStepsMagik(){

  return [

    { target:()=>$('#intrcol'), eyebrow:'What\u2019s Changed', title:'Where Magik flows from',

      body:`In the Masquerade, every completed dance fed you a Magik card. <b>Not here.</b> Beyond the one card every Fae begins with, Midsummer\u2019s Magik flows from one place only, the <b>Faerie Bridge</b>: completing it always grants a <b>Magik card</b>, then a stone action.<br><br>And remember: Once played, a Magik card is spent for good: it rests in the discard, and the deck is never rebuilt from those ashes; only <b>Whispered Lore</b> may pluck a single card back. <b>Cold Iron</b> is sterner still: once used, it passes out of the game entirely, beyond even Lore\u2019s reach.` },

      ];

}

/* The capstone: a Call can be BROKEN. Narrated live demo. */

async function demoBrokenCall(r1){

  // Stage: the Mountain Court at exactly quorum

  const before={...G.nobles};

  G.nobles={mountain:quorum(), meadow:0, forest:0, river:0};

  syncBoard();

  await tutSeg([{ target:()=>$('#c3d'), eyebrow:'The Capstone', title:'A Call is coming\u2026',

    body:`One last lesson, the most important. The <b>Mountain Court</b> holds <b>${quorum()} Wisps</b>: enough to Call. Suppose ${fmtP(r1)} finishes a dance and <b>Calls for their True Name</b> there\u2026`,

    nextLabel:'The Call! \u2192' }]);

  banner('A TRUE NAME IS CALLED');

  await tutSeg([{ target:()=>$('#c3d'), eyebrow:'The Capstone', title:'\u2026but the Call can be answered',

    body:`A Call does not end the dance on its own. It <i>pauses</i>: every rival gets a chance to respond with Faerie Magik, luring or snuffing Wisps, before anything is revealed. Watch what a single <b>Snuff Out</b> does\u2026`,

    nextLabel:'Snuff it \u2192' }]);

  G.nobles.mountain--; syncBoard();

  banner('THE CALL FADES');

  await tutSeg([{ target:()=>$('#c3d'), eyebrow:'The Capstone', title:'The Call fades',

    body:`The Mountain drops to <b>${G.nobles.mountain} Wisps</b>, below the ${quorum()} the Call needs: <b>the Call fades away</b>, and ${fmtP(r1)}\u2019s moment is lost.<br><br><b>The lesson cuts both ways</b>: hold a Snuff Out or Wisp-Lure to break a rival\u2019s Call, and never Call at exactly ${quorum()} unless you know the table can\u2019t answer.<br><b>And beware the ceiling</b>: the <b>${coupAt()}th Wisp</b> placed in a Court calls a True Name there <b>at once</b>, whether anyone wishes it or not.` }]);

  G.nobles=before; syncBoard();

}

async function midPractice(){

  newGame(4, 'midsummer');

  syncBoard(); renderHUD();

  banner('The Midsummer revel begins');

  log(`<b>Free practice.</b> This is a real Midsummer Dance. You belong to the ${fmtH(G.players[0].house)}. Play as long as you like.`, 'sys');

  $('#tutcontinue span').innerHTML='You\u2019re in a <b>real game</b> now.<br>Play on, or wrap up the tour.';

  $('#tutcontinuebtn').textContent='Finish tutorial';

  $('#tutcontinue').style.display='flex';

  $('#tutcontinuebtn').onclick=()=>{

    $('#tutcontinue').style.display='none';

    log(`<b>Tutorial complete.</b> The Midsummer music has begun. Dance well!`, 'sys');

    banner('The Midsummer music has begun\u2026');

  };

  gameLoop().then(()=>{ $('#tutcontinue').style.display='none'; });

}

async function runMidTutorial(){

  bootGame(4, 'midsummer');

  makeDraggable($('#tutbubble'));

  const me=G.players[0], r1=G.players[1], r2=G.players[2];

  // A stable teaching hand: exactly one Magik card, and let it be a friendly one.

  me.intrigues=['Scrying Pool']; renderHUD();

  TUT.tourActive=true;

  try{

    await tutSeg(midStepsWelcome());

    await tutSeg(midStepsFourthPath());

    await midDemoStones(r1, r2);

    await tutSeg(midStepsRunePowers());

    await midDoerRuneOne(me);

    await tutSeg(midStepsMagik());

    await tutSeg(midStepsDanceFavor());

    await tutModal('The Midsummer music has begun\u2026',

      `Now you know Midsummer: the <b>Faerie Bridge</b> feeds you Magik, <b>flips punish</b> and <b>moves relocate</b>, the low runes <b>must</b> act, the middle runes <b>may</b> gamble, and the <b>5</b> can force a rival\u2019s hand. Everything else is the Masquerade you already know.<br><br>Time for a real Midsummer Dance.`,

      'Begin free practice');

  }catch(e){

    if(!(e instanceof GameOver)){

      console.error('Tutorial error:', e);

      tutHideOverlay();

      log(`\u26a0 The tour hit a snag (${(e&&e.message)||e} \u00b7 ${((e&&e.stack)||'').split(String.fromCharCode(10))[1]||''}). You can Quit to the menu and restart it.`, 'alert');

      banner('The tour stumbled');

    }

  }finally{

    TUT.forceRune=null;

    TUT.tourActive=false;

  }

  await midPractice();

}

async function demoFavors(r1,r2){

  await tutSeg([{ target:()=>$('#c3d'), eyebrow:'The Favors', title:'The six favors',

    body:`Each dance grants its own favors when you complete it:<br>

      \u2022 The <b>Faerie Ring</b> affects <b>Radiance</b>: swap yours with a rival, or peek at your own<br>

      \u2022 The <b>Faerie Fort</b> affects <b>Wisps</b>: lure one into another Court, or snuff <b>two</b>, from any Courts<br>

      \u2022 The <b>Faerie Mound</b> affects <b>Courts</b>: swap yours with a rival, or peek at a rival\u2019s<br><br>

      Let me show you each, live.` }]);

  // FAERIE RING: visibly swap two rivals' Radiance on their stands

  const a=r1.status, b=r2.status;

  r1.status=b; r2.status=a; renderHUD();

  await tutSeg([{ target:()=>$('#rivals'), eyebrow:'Watch \u00b7 Faerie Ring', title:'Radiance favors',

    body:`Look at the stands: ${fmtP(r1)} and ${fmtP(r2)} just <b>swapped Radiance</b> (${a} \u2194 ${b}).<br><br><b>Why you\u2019d want this:</b> the win is <i>highest Radiance in the called Court</i>. Swap yourself the 9 you can see on someone\u2019s stand, or peek at your own hidden number before you commit.` }]);

  r1.status=a; r2.status=b; renderHUD();

  // FAERIE MOUND: a rival swaps Courts with YOU, before your eyes

  const me=G.players[MY_SEAT];

  const rr = [r1,r2].find(p=>p.house!==me.house) || r1;

  const rrOld=rr.house;

  if(rr.house===me.house) rr.house = HOUSES.find(h=>h.id!==me.house).id;   // the lesson needs a visible change

  await tutSeg([{ target:()=>$('#myhouse'), eyebrow:'Watch \u00b7 Faerie Mound', title:'Court favors',

    body:`This is <b>your Court card</b>: you belong to the ${fmtH(me.house)}. Keep your eye on it: ${fmtP(rr)} is about to spend a Mound favor\u2026` }]);

  const mine=me.house; me.house=rr.house; rr.house=mine;   // the swap, live

  renderHUD(); syncBoard();

  await tutSeg([{ target:()=>$('#myhouse'), eyebrow:'Watch \u00b7 Faerie Mound', title:'\u2026and the Courts change hands',

    body:`${fmtP(rr)} <b>swapped Courts with you</b>: you now belong to the ${fmtH(me.house)}, and ${fmtP(rr)} holds your old allegiance.<br><br><b>Why you\u2019d want this:</b> you only win in a Court you belong to. <b>Swap</b> to slip into a Wisp-rich Court, or <b>Peek</b> to learn a rival\u2019s allegiance first.` }]);

  me.house=mine; rr.house=rrOld;                            // the lesson ends; the veil falls back

  renderHUD(); syncBoard();

  // FAERIE FORT: drift the demo Wisp from Meadow to Forest

  G.nobles.meadow--; G.nobles.forest++; syncBoard();

  await tutSeg([{ target:()=>$('#c3d'), eyebrow:'Watch \u00b7 Faerie Fort', title:'Wisp favors',

    body:`The Meadow\u2019s Wisp just <b>drifted into the Forest</b>. Fort favors <b>lure</b> a Wisp into a different Court or <b>snuff two</b>, from any Courts Court entirely.<br><br><b>Why you\u2019d want this:</b> Wisps arm the Call. Build your Court\u2019s count, bleed a rival\u2019s, or break a Call at the last moment.` }]);

  G.nobles.forest--; G.nobles.meadow++; syncBoard();

  await tutSeg([{ target:()=>$('#c3d'), eyebrow:'Remember', title:'The six favors',

    body:`That\u2019s all of it: the <b>Ring</b> affects Radiance, the <b>Fort</b> affects Wisps, the <b>Mound</b> affects Courts.<br><br>Hover the <b>gold icons</b> along each board edge, or open <b>Dance Favors</b>, any time you forget. Now, let\u2019s win.`,

    nextLabel:'Begin: your winning turn \u2192' }]);

}

/* a simple centered notice used by the tutorial (separate from in-game choose) */

function tutModal(title, html, btn){

  return new Promise(res=>{

    $('#tutmask').style.display='block';

    tutSpotlight(null);

    $('#tuteyebrow').textContent='Tutorial';

    $('#tuttitle').textContent=title;

    $('#tuttext').innerHTML=html;

    $('#tutstep').textContent='';

    $('#tutback').style.visibility='hidden';

    $('#tutnext').style.display='';

    $('#tutnext').textContent=btn||'Continue';

    tutPlaceBubble(null);

    const handler=()=>{ $('#tutnext').removeEventListener('click',handler); tutHideOverlay(); res(); };

    $('#tutnext').addEventListener('click',handler);

  });

}

/* ---------------- the guided winning turn ---------------- */

async function tutGuidedWin(){

  tutHideOverlay();

  newGame(4, 'masquerade');

  G.over=false;

  const me=G.players[0];

  const myCourt='forest';

  me.house=myCourt; me.status=5;              // mid Radiance \u2014 and we WIN

  const r1=G.players[1], r2=G.players[2], r3=G.players[3];

  r1.house=myCourt;    r1.status=3;           // shares my Court, but lower \u2014 I beat them

  r2.house='mountain'; r2.status=9;           // highest number in the game, but WRONG Court

  r3.house='river';    r3.status=7;           // also high, also wrong Court

  const ringLen=trackLen('Faerie Ring');

  me.cands=[{track:'Faerie Ring', steps:ringLen-1}, {track:null, steps:0}];

  me.hand=[1]; me.discard=[2,3,4,5,6];

  G.players.forEach(q=>{ q.intrigues=[]; });   // no reactions can derail the guided turn

  G.nobles={mountain:0, meadow:0, forest:quorum()-1, river:0};

  syncBoard(); renderHUD();

  TUT.guide={court:myCourt, lock:null};

  TUT.act3=true;   // tells callForThrone to show the teaching caption + practice exit

  await tutModal('One move from winning',

    `A set-up moment. You belong to the <b>Forest Court</b>, and it already holds <b>${quorum()-1} Wisps</b>, one short of the ${quorum()} needed to Call.<br><br>One of your dancers is a single step from finishing the <b>Faerie Ring</b>. Finish it, and you can unveil the Wisp that arms your Call.`,

    'Show me');

  // play the 1 \u2014 no gate, just a hint (#4)

  const closeRune=tutHint('Play your Fae Rune', 'Play your only rune, the <b>1</b>. Click it now.', ()=>$('#hand'));

  const ev=await armHuman(['honor']);

  closeRune();

  me.hand.splice(me.hand.indexOf(ev.v),1); me.discard.push(ev.v);

  log(`${fmtP(me)} dances a <b>1</b>.`);

  renderHUD();

  // drag to finish \u2014 no gate, drag immediately (#4)

  TUT.guide.lock={ci:0, track:'Faerie Ring', step:ringLen};

  clearTileHighlights();

  const tgt=SCENE.tiles.find(t=>t.userData.track==='Faerie Ring' && t.userData.step===ringLen);

  if(tgt){ tgt.material.emissive.setHex(0xd9b454); tgt.material.emissiveIntensity=.7; }

  const closeDrag=tutHint('Finish the Dance', 'Click, tap, or drag your <b>glowing Glamour</b> to the <b>lit stone</b> to complete the Faerie Ring.');

  try {

    await allocate(me, me, 1);

  } catch(e){ if(!(e instanceof GameOver)) throw e; }

  finally { closeDrag(); }

  TUT.guide=null;

  // wait for the reveal's Continue button

  await new Promise(res=>{ TUT.act3Continue=res; });

}

/* ---------------- free practice \u2192 a real game ---------------- */

async function tutPractice(){

  newGame(4, 'masquerade');

  syncBoard(); renderHUD();

  banner('A real dance begins');

  log(`<b>Free practice.</b> This is a real Masquerade. You belong to the ${fmtH(G.players[0].house)}. Play as long as you like.`, 'sys');

  $('#tutcontinue span').innerHTML='You\u2019re in a <b>real game</b> now.<br>Play on, or wrap up the tour.';

  $('#tutcontinuebtn').textContent='Finish tutorial';

  $('#tutcontinue').style.display='flex';

  $('#tutcontinuebtn').onclick=()=>{

    $('#tutcontinue').style.display='none';

    log(`<b>Tutorial complete.</b> The dance is yours; play on! When you\u2019re ready for conjured stones, rune powers, and Faerie Magik, try the <b>Midsummer Dance</b>.`, 'sys');

    banner('The dance is yours');

  };

  gameLoop().then(()=>{ $('#tutcontinue').style.display='none'; });

}

async function runMasqTutorial(){

  bootGame(4, 'masquerade');

  makeDraggable($('#tutbubble'));    // the hint bubble can be moved out of the way

  G.nobles.meadow=1; syncBoard();   // demo Wisp for the tour

  const me=G.players[0], r1=G.players[1], r2=G.players[2];

  TUT.tourActive=true;

  try{

    await tutSeg(stepsWelcome());

      await tutSeg(stepsSecrets(me));

    await tutSeg(stepsRunes());

    await tutDoerFirstStep(me);

    await tutSeg(stepsDances());

    await tutSeg(stepsPayoff());

    await demoFavors(r1,r2);

    await demoBrokenCall(r1);

    await tutGuidedWin();

  }catch(e){

    if(!(e instanceof GameOver)){

      console.error('Tutorial error:', e);

      tutHideOverlay();

      log(`\u26a0 The tour hit a snag (${(e&&e.message)||e} \u00b7 ${((e&&e.stack)||'').split(String.fromCharCode(10))[1]||''}). You can Quit to the menu and restart it.`, 'alert');

      banner('The tour stumbled');

    }

  }finally{

    TUT.forceRune=null;

    TUT.tourActive=false;

  }

  await tutPractice();

}

/* The Masquerade tutorial is wired to #tutMasq above; the Midsummer Dance

   tutorial (Stage 3) will teach the delta: stones, rune powers, Faerie Magik. */

</script>
